ānandam ekam amṛtam ajam vijñānam akṣaram asarvam sarvam abhayam namasyāmaḥ prajāpatim vedānteṣu vipratipadyante vipaścitaḥ kecid aprāmāṇyam manyante ātmanaḥ pramāṇa antara siddha tve teṣām anuvādaka tvam asiddha tve saṃbandha agrahaṇāt  apadārtha tve vākyasya aviṣaya tvāt pravṛtti nivṛtti anupadeśe ca apuruṣa artha tvāt anye tu pratipatti kartavya tā prāmāṇya vyājena aprāmāṇyam eva āhuḥ anye tu karma vidhi virodhāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt ca śruta artha parigrahe upacarita arthān manyante tad nirāsa artham ucyate ānandam iti parām ca devatām guṇa abhidhāna lakṣaṇayā stutyā kāya vāc manaḥ prahvatā lakṣaṇayā ca praṇatyā pūjayati prakaraṇa artham ca upakṣipati vipratipatti nirākaraṇa mukhena vedāntānām evaṃbhūte arthe prāmāṇya pratipādanāt yatas  bhavati eṣaḥ api prakaraṇa arthaḥ atra kecid  ānanda ātmaka tve brahmaṇaḥ ānanda rāgāt mumukṣu pravṛttiḥ syāt  rāga nibandhanā ca pravṛttiḥ saṃsāra bījam iti na muktaye syāt  śāntasya dāntasya ca ātmani darśanam ucyate na ca ānanda anurāgāt pravartamānaḥ śāntaḥ  bhavati tasmāt sakala duḥkha atige brahma tattve duḥkhebhya udvignaḥ sukhebhyaḥ ca vīta rāgaḥ pravartamānaḥ  mucyate ānanda śrutayaḥ ca sakala duḥkha atikramam eva āhuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ  hi kṣudh duḥkha ādi nivṛttau sukha śabdaḥ sā eva ca sukham iti anye na ca āśma ādau prasaṅgaḥ pratyak vṛtteḥ upalabhyamānāyāḥ sukha tvāt  tad viśiṣṭa ātma upalabdheḥ vā tān pratyāha ānandam iti na tāvat duḥkha nivṛttiḥ eva sukham yugapad sukha duḥkhayoḥ darśanāt saṃtāpavataḥ śītahrade nimagna ardha kāyasya atha sati api animagna ardha kāya duḥkhe itarasya abhāvāt sukham iti kumbhīpāke pacyamānasya naraka antara duḥkha abhāvāt sukhitva prasaṅgaḥ eka indriya dvāra duḥkhasya ca indriya antar dvāra duḥkha abhāvāt itas ca aduḥkhasya api viṣaya viśeṣa saṃparkāt saṃvedya āhlāda utpatteḥ yatra api duḥkha vigamaḥ tatra api na tanmātram eva sukham anna pāna viśeṣa upādānāt  duḥkha vigamaḥ  hi yaiḥ taiḥ anna pānaiḥ sidhyati na ca sa viśeṣavān yena tad viśeṣāya tad sādhana viśeṣaḥ  apekṣyeta sukhe tu atiśayavat tvādi uktā tad sādhana atiśaya apekṣā yad api manyante yadā api na anyat duḥkham nivartyam tadā api kāmasya duḥkha ātmaka tvāt tad nibarhaṇa rūpam sukham tatra api akāmasya viṣaya viśeṣa upabhoge na sukhitā syāt  bhavati ca madhyasthaḥ  api ramaṇīya viṣaya saṃparke hlādavān syāt etad  yatra eva kāmaḥ sa eva sukhayati viṣayaḥ na itaraḥ tasmāt kāma nivṛttya eva viṣayāḥ sukhayitāraḥ anyathā ya ekasya sukhaḥ sa sarvasya syāt  kāma nivṛttyā tu sukha tve yatra yasya kāmaḥ  abhiruciḥ sa eva tasya sukha iti yujyate tatra akāmasya api viṣaya viśeṣa upabhogāt kāma abhivyaktau tad nivṛttau tad sukhitvam iti tad api asāram yatas  viṣaya upabhogā na avaśyam kāma nibarhaṇāḥ uktam hi ‘na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyatiiti tathā ‘bhoga abhyāsam anu vivardhante rāgāḥ kauśalāni ca indriyāṇāmiti viṣaya doṣa darśanāt api ca kāma nivṛttiḥ tatra upabhoga tulya āhlādaḥ syāt  samāne ca prārthita artha lābhe pramoda bhedaḥ  na syāt  kāma nivṛtteḥ aviśeṣāt  syāt etad  kāma atireke tad nivṛttau sukha atiśaya abhimānaḥ itaratra anyathā iti tad ca na kāma atirekāt prayasyantam avāptaḥ  arthaḥ  na tathā prīṇayati yathā prārthitaḥ  vinā prayāsāt upanataḥ tathā hi kleśāt avāptaḥ  ayam iti na tena tathā prīyate yathā anāśaṃsita upanatena kāma abhāva mātre ca sukhe akāmita viṣaya upabhoge na bhoga avasthāyāḥ pūrva apare avasthe bhidyeyātām kāma pradhvaṃse vā para avasthā na bhidyeta bhoga avasthāyām prabuddha adhvastakāma eva iti ced pūrvā parayoḥ api dvayoḥ avasthayoḥ tarhi sukhī itaratra duḥkhī iti anubhava viruddham āpadyeta aprāptaḥ ca smaraṇa viparivartī viṣayaḥ kāmasya udbodhakaḥ prāptaḥ  nivartakaḥ prāptasya udbodha tve na tatas  nivṛttiḥ syāt  na ca yatra kāmaḥ tatra sukham manoratha śata arthitasya api upabhogena kasyacid duḥkhi tva darśanāt sukha pūrvakaḥ tu kāmaḥ anubhūta tad bhāve tad darśanāt  yā api kācid ananubhūte api jāti viśeṣa bhājām kāma pravṛttiḥ sā api prāc bhavīya anubhava nibandhanā yathā ca kasyacid kvacid kāmaḥ  jāti bheda ādi nimittaḥ tathā kiñcid kasyacid sukham iti na avyavasthā api ca kāma nivṛttyā api kecid dūyante tad abhāve viṣaya upabhoga sāmarthya abhāvāt na tarhi nivṛtti kāmāḥ nivṛtti kāmā viṣayam prati tasya kutaścid nimittāt anupabhogya tvāt kim iti tarhi dūyante anubhūta carasya tad janmanaḥ sukhasya aprāpteḥ yathā pitta ādi upahata indriyā viśiṣṭebhyaḥ  anna pānebhyaḥ  nivṛtti kāmāḥ tathā eva kāma nivṛttyā tapyante tatra anubhūta cara tad janma āhlāda vicchedāt na anyaḥ  hetuḥ tasmāt pratyātma vedanīya sukha pratyākhyānam ayuktam sukha saṅgi jana upacchandanāya tu tatrabhavadbhiḥ varṇitam iti paśyāmaḥ tad evam duḥkha nivṛtteḥ anyat sukham sa ca ānanda śabdasya mukhyaḥ  arthaḥ śabda pramāṇake ca yathāśabdam pratipattiḥ yuktā na ca rāga nibandhanā tatra pravṛttiḥ na hi icchā mātram rāgaḥ avidyā kṣiptam abhūta guṇa abhiniveśam rāgam ācakṣate tattva darśana vaimalyāt tu tattve cetasaḥ prasādaḥ  abhiruciḥ abhi icchā na rāga pakṣe vyavasthāpyate yathā saṃsāra asāra tā tattva darśana niṣpannaḥ  na udvegaḥ tatas  dveṣa pakṣe anyathā sarva duḥkha atige api tattve tad dveṣa nibandhanā pravṛttiḥ iti saṃsāra anubandhaḥ syāt  api ca dṛṣṭa para utkarṣa rāgibhyaḥ  api indriya jaya upadiśyate sādhana tvena kāma ādi tyāga ātmakaḥ tathā iha api bhaviṣyati katham ca tatra samīhita itara viṣaya abhiṣvaṅga niṣedhaḥ sarva niṣedhe apravṛtti darśanāt  tathā uttama sukha rāga āditarasmāt upanatāt api nivṛttiḥ tathā ca uktam ‘kāma ātma tā na praśastā na ca eva iha asti akāma tāiti syāt etad  ānandaḥ ced brahmaṇi saṃvedyaḥ kartuḥ anyat karma iti dvaita prasaṅgaḥ kartṛ karma bhāvaḥ ca na kriyām karaṇam ca antareṇa yatas  tatas  ‘a ānandam brahmaiti ca na syāt  tadvat tayā vyapadeśe advitīyam iti na yujyate asaṃvedane san= apisat kalpa iti vyartham tad saṃkīrtanam puruṣa artha tvāya hi tad saṃkīrtanam asaṃvedyaḥ ca katham puruṣa arthaḥ ucyate phalavat kartṛvat ca idam draṣṭavyam tathā hi pramāṇasya phalam artha antaram anartha antaram vā sarva parīkṣakaiḥ pratijñāyate prajñāyate ca na ca tad asaṃvedyam tad asaṃvedya tve sarva asaṃvedya tva prasaṅgāt  tad kṛta tvāt saṃvedya bhāvasya bhāvānām na ca saṃvedyam phala antara anupalabdheḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt saṃvedyam ātma prakāśa tvāt  asaṃvedyam ca viṣayavat karma bhāva abhāvāt yathā ca kartari ātmani asaṃvedye saṃvid eva na syāt  na hi tadā evam bhavati mayā idam viditam iti na hi ātmā saṃvedyaḥ phale viṣaye ca anusaṃdhātum śakyaḥ ananusaṃdhāne ca sva para saṃvedyayoḥ kaḥ  atiśayaḥ na ca saṃvedyaḥ karma tve kartuḥ vyatireka prasaṅgāt  anātma tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt ātma prakāśa tā eva tasya saṃvedya tā tathā brahmaṇaḥ sva ātma prakāśasya ānanda svabhāvaḥ  na saṃvedyaḥ karma tva abhāvāt na ca asaṃvedyaḥ sva prakāśa tvāt  ‘tatkena kam paśyet  aiti api niṣedhaḥ karma viṣayaḥ tathā hi sarva karma pratyasta maya hetuka eva sa ucyate ‘yadā asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūtiti anye manyante dvividhā dharmāḥ bhāva rūpā abhāva rūpāḥ ca iti tatra abhāva rūpā na advaitam vighnanti yathā ‘ekam amṛtam ajamiti na hi bheda udaya vyayānām nivṛttiḥ kiñcid vastu yena dvaitam āvahet  ānandaḥ ca yadi bhāvaḥ tasya dharmi tve vijñānam dharmaḥ syāt  atha vijñānam dharmi rūpam ānandaḥ  dharmaḥ na hi ekasya dve rūpe yujyete virodhāt  tatra ‘vijñānam ānandam brahmaiti bhāva rūpayoḥ ānanda brahmaṇoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt advaita vighātaḥ syāt etad  dharmaḥ  api dharmiṇaḥ  na bhinnaḥ bhede gavāśvavat dharma dharmi bhāva anupapatteḥ tad asat  abhede api dharmi rūpavat tad anupapatteḥ tasmāt kathañcid bhinnaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ca ātyantika bheda abhāva śrutiḥ ‘ekam eva advitīyamiti na yujyate evam yaḥ  api ekasya rūpa dvayam pratipadyate tasmāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  duḥkha abhāva upādhiḥ eva ānanda śabdaḥ yathā sthūla abhāva ādi upādhayaḥ ‘a sthūlam anaṇva hrasvam aitya ādayaḥ śabdāḥ na ca vijñāna ānandayoḥ eka tvam eva śabda dvaya prayoga vaiyarthyāt  katham ca aparyāya śabda abhidheya eka tvam tasmāt duḥkha uparama eva ānanda śabdasya brahmaṇi artha iti atra ucyate viśiṣṭasya āhlāda ātmanaḥ prakāśasya cāndramasasya iva śabda dvayena pratipādanāt na doṣaḥ yathā ca prakṛṣṭaḥ prakāśaḥ savitā iti na ca prakṛṣṭa prakāśa śabdayoḥ paryāya tvam atha ca eka eva abhyām artha viśeṣaḥ pratipādyate prakāśa viśeṣaḥ na hi prakarṣaḥ  anyaḥ prakāśa rūpāt sa vitari na prakāśa rūpaḥ  vā prakarṣāt  api tu prakāśa bhedaḥ śabda dvaya upāyaḥ pratīyate tathā ‘vijñānam ānandam brahmaiti ānanda bhedaḥ  vijñāna bhedaḥ  vā brahma rūpam iti śabda dvayena avagamyate parama tām api asya kecid sādhana pāratantrya lakṣaṇāyāḥ kṣayitā lakṣaṇāyāḥ ca duḥkha tāyā abhāvāt manyante tad api yathāśabdam pratipatteḥ śabda pramāṇake arthe na anumanyante na hi svarūpataḥ para ma tā saṃbhave virodhisaṃsargāt upacaritā sā yuktā bhavitum tasmāt ātma prakāśa prakṛṣṭa ātma svabhāvam eva brahma iti yuktam evam ca laukika ānanda etasya mātrā iti yujyate avacchedāt  duḥkha nivṛttau tu duryojam etad  itas ca ānanda svabhāva ātmā para prema āspada tvāt  śrūyate hi para prema āspada tvam ‘tat etad preyaḥ putrātiti pratīyate ca tathā hi sarvasya iyam ātma āśīḥ kṛmeḥ api ‘mā na bhūvam bhūyāsamiti sā ca priye avakalpate premā ca sukha ātmani na duḥkhe na ubhaya rūpa rahite dveṣāt upekṣaṇāt ca anye tu suṣupte ‘sukham aham asvāpsamiti parāmarśāt ātmani sukha anubhavam āhuḥ na hi ananubhave parāmarśa evam syāt  suṣupta abhyupagamaḥ ca na ca anyathā anubhave sukham iti parāmarśaḥ na ca tatra ātmanaḥ  anyat anubhavanīyam asti tathā ca aharahar brahma loka avāptiḥ śrūyate tatra anya āhuḥ duḥkha uparamāt api tathā parāmarśa siddheḥ na ekāntataḥ sukhitva siddhiḥ tān pratyāhuḥ anyathā abhāve avagate duḥkha uparama nimittaḥ sukha śabda iti yujyate anyathā mukhya artha tā eva yuktā tatra āhuḥ ubhayathā vyapadeśasya darśanāt upapatteḥ ca na vyapadeśa mātrāt artha siddhiḥ iti alam ati vistareṇa atra kecid  bhoga vyavasthānāt  mukta saṃsāri vibhāga upapatteḥ ca dṛś śakteḥ ca arthavat tvāt  sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt  dṛśyena ca draṣṭuḥ anumānāt  dṛśyasya ca sukha duḥkha moha bhedavat śabda ādi vibhāga upalabdheḥ ekatva śrutiḥ jāti deśa kāla vibhāga abhāva nimitta upacārāt manyante ‘ātmā eva idam sarvamiti ca tādarthya nimitta upacārāt tān pratyucyate ekam iti ‘indraḥ  māyābhiḥ puru rūpa īyateiti vyaktam eva nānā rūpa avagamaḥ  māyā nibandhanaḥ  darśitaḥ tatra katham eka tvam upacaritam iti vaktum śakyam tathā vyaktaḥ  nānā tva niṣedhaḥ ‘na iha nānā asti kiñcanaiti nānātva darśana nindā ca ‘mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnotiiti bheda darśanasya ca abhāvaḥ bheda dṛṣṭiḥ iva bhramāt  ‘ya iha na anā iva paśyatiiti iva śabdena prakāśitaḥ  na upacarita ekatve avakalpate kāmam upacāra ādaḥ tu eka tvam na tu bhāvikasya nānātvasya nivṛttiḥ sā api upacāreṇa eva ucyata iti ced  na prayojana abhāvāt sati nimitte prayojane ca upacāraḥ na ca nānātva nivṛtti upacāre prayojanam paśyāmaḥ viparyayāt ca abhyudayāya niḥśreyasāya vā nānā tva nivṛttiḥ upacaryeta sā hi sādhya sādhana ādi vibhāgam nivartayantī sarvatra ca ātmā abhimānam āvirbhāvayantī tad virodhinī syāt  tathā hi sarvatas  nivṛttasya niḥśreyasam iti avisaṃvādaḥ (corret tet  api saṃvādaḥ edition) tathā ‘ekam eva advitīyam aiti avadhāraṇa ādvitīya śabdābhyām tasya eva arthasya punar punar abhidhānāt sarva prakāra bheda nivṛtti para tā śruteḥ lakṣyate abhyāse hi bhūyas tvam arthasya bhavati yathā ‘ahaḥ darśanīyā ahaḥ darśanīyāiti na nyūna tvam api dūrata eva upacarita tvam yad tu bhoga vyavasthānāt iti tatra ucyate kalpitāt api bhedāt bhoga vyavasthā siddheḥ asāram etad  tathā hi ekasmin= api ātmani sarva gate śarīra parimāṇe aṇu parimāṇe vā kalpita bheda nibandhanā bhoga vyavasthā dṛśyate pāde me vedanā śirasi me vedanā iti na hi pādasya śirasaḥ  vā vedanayā abhisaṃbandhaḥ ajña tvāt  śarīra parimāṇa ātma vādinaḥ  api na avayavā eva vedanā bhājaḥ ātmanaḥ tad viraha prasaṅgāt  syāt etad  aikātmye tadvat eva deha antara bhoga anusandhānam syāt  anyat idānīm etad  asti tāvat bhoga vyavasthā api ca tatra api na pradeśaḥ pradeśa antara vedanām anusaṃdadhāti tathā iha api na jīvaḥ  jīva antara vedanām anu saṃdadhāti iti samānam tathā maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādiṣu sukha ādīnām varṇa saṃsthāna bheda vyavasthānam upalabhyate bheda abhāve api evam ca mukta saṃsāri vibhāgaḥ  api upapannaḥ tathā hi ekaḥ  api ātmā pradeśaiḥ sukha duḥkha ādibhiḥ yujyamānaḥ tatra baddha iva itaratra mukta iva ca gamyate yathā malīmase darpaṇa tale malīm asam mukham viśuddhe viśuddham darpaṇa rahitam ca gamyamānam tad upādhi doṣa asaṃpṛktam syāt etad  kalpanā pratipattuḥ pratyayasya dharmaḥ  na vastu vyavasthāpayitum alam na khalu pratipattuḥ pratyayam anu viparivartante vastūni na ca upacaritāt kāryam upapadyate na hi upacarita agni bhāvaḥ  māṇavakaḥ  dahati udāhṛtā tu vyavasthā satyam vibhramaḥ  hi saḥ atra api vibhrama tvam na daṇḍa vāritam kalpitaḥ  api ca ahidaṃśaḥ  maraṇa kāryāya kalpate pratisūryakaḥ ca prakāśa kāryāya yad api dṛśyena eva draṣṭuḥ anumānāt draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ bhedaḥ dṛśyasya ca sukha ādi bheda upalabdheḥ na anātvam iti tad api asat na draṣṭarya prakāśe yatas  dṛśyasya siddhiḥ asti iti uktam dṛśya bheda upalabdhiḥ ca na asti pramāṇasya anavacchedaka tvāt iti vakṣyate dṛś śakteḥ ca arthavat tvam sva ātma upayogāt na ca sva ātmani vṛtti virodhaḥ pradīpavat pramāṇa phalavat ca iti uktam api ca eka tva eva ayam draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ  avakalpate draṣṭuḥ eva cit ātmanaḥ tathā tathā vipariṇāmāt vivartanāt vā nānātve tu vivitkasvabhāvayoḥ asaṃsṛṣṭa paraspara svarūpayoḥ asambaddhayoḥ kīdṛśaḥ  draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ na hi cityā saṃsṛṣṭam cetitam iti yujyate ekāntaḥkaraṇa saṃkrāntau= asti eva sambandha iti ced  na citeḥ śuddha tvāt apariṇāmāda pratisaṃkramāt ca dṛśyā buddhiḥ citi sannidheḥ tad chāyayā vivartata iti ced  atha kā iyam tad śāyatā atada ātmanaḥ tad avabhāsaḥ na tarhi paramārtha taḥ  dṛśyam dṛśyate paramārthataḥ ca adṛśyamānam draṣṭṛ vī atiriktam asti iti durbhaṇam yaḥ  api manyate dṛśya tayā eva dṛśyam vyavasthāpyate na sambandhena darśanam ca ‘idam aiti parāgrūpa viṣayam sa vaktavyaḥ satyam parāgrūpa viṣayam tad tu ekasya eva ātmanaḥ tathā tathā vipariṇāmāt vivartanāt vā darpaṇa tala iva ātmanaḥ tathā hi darpaṇa tala stham ātmānam vibhaktam iva ātmanaḥ pratyeti citeḥ tu vibhaktam asaṃsṛṣṭam tayā cetyata iti duravagamam evam ca draṣṭuḥ avyatirekaḥ  dṛśyasyāmnāyate ‘a ātmani vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavatiiti tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam ekam iti kṣaṇika jñāna ātma vādinaḥ tu sa vāsana kleśa samucchedāt jñāna uparama lakṣaṇām eva brahma prāptim āhuḥ tathā ca śrūyate ‘na pretya saṃjñā astiiti anye tu samucchinna sakala vāsana tvāt vidhūta viṣaya ākāra upaplava viśuddha jñāna utpāda lakṣaṇām anādi nidhana tve hi na apaneyam na upaneyam vā kiñcid asti iti tad arthāni śāstrāṇi tad arthāḥ ca pravṛttayaḥ  vyarthāḥ syuḥ tathā hi vidyā svabhāvam ced  na kiñcid nivartavyam avāptavyam vā syāt  avidyāyāḥ  abhāvāt vidyāyāḥ ca bhāvāt  avidyā svabhāvam ced  tasya nitya tve pūrva svabhāva tyāgāt svabhāva antara anāpatteḥ ca evam ubhaya svabhāva tve api vidyāyāḥ prāpta tvāt avidyāyāḥ ca ucchettum aśakya tvāt tān pratyāha amṛtam ajam iti na ca śāstrāṇām mukti arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam avidyāyāḥ  nivartya tvāt  sarva pravādeṣu ca anādiḥ api avidyā ucchedya abhyupagamyate na brūmaḥ  anādeḥ na uccheda iti kim tu nityasya brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvasya atha avidyā na brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ artha antaram brahmaṇa āpadyeta na vā syāt  tatra kim nivartyam atha matam agrahaṇam avidyā sā katham artha antaram syāt  na ca anivartyā sarva pramāṇa vyāpārāṇām agrahaṇa nivṛtti artha tvāt tad api ayuktam tattva agrahaṇa ātmikayā vidyayā nivartyate sā ca nityā brahmaṇi na ca brahmaṇaḥ  anyaḥ  asti yasya tattva agrahaṇam brahmaṇi prayatnalabhyayā vidyayā nivartyeta brahmaṇi tu yugapad grahaṇa agrahaṇe vipratiṣiddhe avipratiṣedhe vā na kadācid avidyā nivartyeta yasya tu viparyaya grahaṇam avidyā tasya brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ ced sa nityaḥ katham nivartyeta asvabhāvaḥ ced artha antaram āpadyeta kasya ca tad iti vācyam brahmaṇaḥ  anyasya abhāvāt  brahmaṇa eva iti ced  vipratiṣedhaḥ tasya vidyā svarūpa tvāt avipratiṣedhe vā kena nivṛttiḥ atra ucyate na avidyā brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ na artha antaram na atyantam asatī na api satī evam eva iyam avidyā māyā mithyā avabhāsa iti ucyate svabhāvaḥ ced kasyacid  anyaḥ  ananyaḥ  vā parama artha eva iti na avidyā atyanta asattve khapuṣpa sadṛśī na vyavahāra aṅgam tasmāt anirvacanīyā sarva pravādibhiḥ ca ittham iyam āstheyā tathā hi śūnya vādinā sattve yathārtha darśanam na avidyā kha puṣpa tulya tve na vyavahāra aṅgam vijñāna mātra vādinaḥ  api yathā avabhāsam jñāna sadbhāve na artha apahnavaḥ nīla pīta ādeḥ jñeya ākārasya bahis avabhāsān apahnavāt  atyanta asattve bahis avabhāsa ayogāt  kha puṣpavat  bāhya artha vādinām api anitya ādiṣu nitya ādi khyātayaḥ rajata ādi vibhrāntayaḥ ca avabhāsamāna rūpa sadbhāve na avidyā tvam aśnu vīran na atyanta asattve tad nibandhanaḥ kaścana vyavahāraḥ syāt  syāt etad  avabhāsamānam rūpam mā bhūt  avabhāsaḥ tu san= ā iva sa ca avidyā iti gīyate na etad sāram avabhāsamāne asati tad avabhāsaḥ  api satyataḥ  durnirūpaḥ avabhāsa mātram tu syāt  tad avabhāsa iti api bhrāntiḥ eva tasmāt na avidyā satī na api asati iti ata eva ca asyā nivṛttiḥ adṛḍha svabhāvāyāḥ māyā mātra tvāt anyathā svabhāve dṛḍham vyavasthitāyāḥ katham anyathātvam svabhāva hānāt  śūnya tve svayam nivṛtta tvāt  evam ca na advaita hānam na nivartanīyasya abhāvaḥ  vā yad tu kasya avidyā iti jīvānām iti brūmaḥ nanu na jīvā brahmaṇaḥ  bhidyante evam hi āha ‘anena jīvena ātma anupraviśyaiti satyam paramārthataḥ kalpanayā tu bhidyante kasya punar  kalpanā bhedikā na tāvat  brahmaṇaḥ tasya vidyā ātmanaḥ kalpanā śūnyatvāt  na api jīvānām kalpanāyāḥ prāk  tad abhāvāt itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt  kalpanā adhīnaḥ  hi jīva vibhāgaḥ jīva āśrayā kalpanā iti atra kecid āhuḥ vastu siddhau= eva doṣaḥ na asiddham vastu vastu antara niṣpattaye alam na māyā mātre na hi māyāyām kācid anupapattiḥ anupapadyamāna arthā eva hi māyā upapadyamāna artha tve yathā artha bhāvāt na māyā syāt  anye tu anādi tvāt ubhayoḥ avidyā jīvayoḥ bīja aṅkura santānayoḥ iva na itaretara āśrayam aprakḷptim āvahati iti varṇayanti tathā ca uktam avidyā upādānava ādibhiḥ ‘anādira prayojanā ca avidyāiti tatra anādi tvā anna itaretara āśraya tva doṣaḥ aprayojana tvāt na bheda prapañca sarga prayojana paryanuyoga avakāśaḥ yad eke paryanuyuñjate ‘prayojanam anuddiśya na mandaḥ api pravartateiti tatra parasya brahmaṇaḥ prapañca sarga prayojanam vācyam na tāvat para anugrahaḥ prāk  sargāt anugrāhyāṇām abhāvāt duḥkha uttara tvāt ca sargasya na ātma artha krīḍā ādiḥ āpta kāma tvāt iti tasya avidyā nibandhana tve sarge na avakāśaḥ na hi avidyā prayojanam apekṣya pravartate na hi gandharvanagara ādi vibhramāḥ samuddiṣṭa prayojanā bhavanti tathā ‘puruṣasya viśuddhasya na aśuddhā vikṛtiḥ bhavetiti api prayuktam avidyā nibandhane sarga vibhāge api ca kṛtārthānām āpta kāmānām eva krīḍā ādi pravṛttiḥ ullāsāt  prārthanā parikṛṣṭa cetasām tu rati virahiṇām anabhimatā eva krīḍā bhavati na ca vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇya doṣaḥ na hi māyā kārasya vividham prapañcam darśayataḥ  aṅga sākalya vaikalya vibhāgena rāga dveṣa vibhāgaḥ citrapusta ādi kṛtām vā vikala avikala ādi bhedena citrāṇi tāni tāni kurvatām bālānām ca mṛṇmaya ādibhiḥ pratikṛti bhedaiḥ vicitraiḥ krīḍatām na teṣu kiñcid vaiṣamyam nairghṛṇyam vā karma āśaya anurodhena ca vidadhataḥ  vaicitryam na doṣa iti ācāryāḥ na ca anīśvara tva doṣaḥ na hi sevā bheda anurodhena phala bheda pradaḥ prabhuḥ aprabhuḥ bhavati tathā śuddhasya api aśuddhaḥ  vikāraḥ na hi prakṛti vikārayoḥ atyantam availakṣaṇyam prakṛti vikāra bhāva eva na syāt  dravāṇām cāpām karaka ādiḥ kaṭhinaḥ  vikāraḥ tathā acetanasya gomayasya cetanaḥ vṛścika ityādi bahuvidham prakṛti vikāra vailakṣaṇyam utprekṣitavyam iti alam ati prasaṅgena nanu jīvā api brahma tattva avyatirekāt viśuddha svabhāvāḥ tad katham teṣu avidyā vakāśaḥ vārtam etad  na ca tāvat bimbāt avadātāt pratibimbam kṛpāṇa ādiṣu bhinnam atha ca tatra śyāma tā ādiḥśuddhiḥ avakāśam labhate vibhramaḥ sa iti ced  samānam etad jīvānām api aśuddhiḥ vibhramaḥ anyathā duravāpa eva viśuddhiḥ syāt iti uktam syāt etad  kṛpāṇa ādayaḥ  mukhe vibhrānti hetavaḥ tathā iha api vibhrama hetuḥ vācyaḥ anādau vibhrame hetu anveṣaṇam asāmpratam iva tathā ca ‘svapna ādivat avidyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ tasya kiṅkṛtāiti pratyuktam nanu svābhāvikī ana ādiḥ avidyā nirhetuḥ sā katham ucchidyeta sarva śāstrāṇi eva tāvat naisargikyā avidyāyāḥ  ucchedāya prasthitāni api ca pārthivānām aṇūnām śyāma tāna ādiḥ pāka jena varṇena nivartyate nanu svābhāvikam api kiñcid vilakṣaṇa pratyaya upanipātāt nivartatām aikātmya vādinaḥ tu anāgantuka arthasya tad abhāvāt kutaḥ nivṛttiḥ na khalu ātma svabhāva eva vidyā avidyā nivartikā avidyāyāḥ tayā saha vṛtteḥ avirodhāt  virodhe vā nitya nivṛtteḥ nityam uktam jagat syāt  na ca vidyā antaram āgantukam virodhi nivartakam aikātmya vāde vyatiriktasya tasya ayogāt āgantukasya brahma svabhāva tva anupapatteḥ ca tad uktam ‘svābhāvikīm avidyām tu na ucchettum kaścid arhati vilakṣaṇa upapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikam kvacid  na tu aikātmya abhyupāyānām hetuḥ asti vilakṣaṇaḥiti atra ucyate uktam etad jīvānām avidyā kaluṣita tvam na brahmaṇaḥ tad hi sadā viśuddha nitya prakāśam anāgantuka artham anyathā brahma bhūyam gatasya api na avidyā nivarteta tatra anirmokṣaḥ atha brahmā eva saṃsarati brahmā eva mucyate eka m uktau sarva mukti prasaṅgaḥ yatas  bheda darśanena brahmā eva saṃsarati abheda darśanena ca mucyate teṣām ca nisarga ja avidyā kaluṣāṇām vilakṣaṇa pratyaya vidyā udayena upapadyate avidyā nivṛttiḥ na hi jīveṣu nisarga jā vidyā asti avidyā eva hi naisargikī tasyāḥ  āgantukyā vidyayā pravilayaḥ avyatireke api ca brahmaṇaḥ  jīvānām bimba pratibimbavat vidyā avidyā vyavasthā vyākhyātā kena punar upāyena avidyā nivartate śravaṇa manana dhyāna abhyāsaiḥ brahmacarya ādibhiḥ ca sādhana bhedaiḥ śāstra uktaiḥ katham yaḥ  ayam śravaṇa manana pūrva kaḥ  dhyāna abhyāsaḥ pratiṣiddha akhila bheda prapañce ‘sa eṣa na iti na iti aātmani sa vyaktam eva bheda darśana pratiyogī tad nivartayati sa ca sāmānyena bheda darśanam pravilāpayan= ātmanā api pravilīyate na ca śrotṛ śravaṇa śrotavya ādi vibhāga parihāṇyā vibhāga antara nivṛtti viṣayāḥ śravaṇa ādayaḥ api tu sāmānyena tathā ca tasmin= api pravilīne svacchaḥ pariśuddhaḥ  asya ātmā prakāśate yathā rajaḥ samparka kaluṣitam udakam dravya viśeṣa cūrṇa rajaḥ prakṣiptam rajontarāṇi saṃharat su ayam api saṃhriyamāṇam su acchām svarūpa avasthām upanayati evam eva śravaṇa ādibhiḥ bheda darśane pravilīyamāne viśeṣa abhāvāt tad gate ca bhede svacche pariśuddhe svarūpe jīvaḥ  avatiṣṭhate avidyayā eva tu brahmaṇaḥ  jīvaḥ  vibhaktaḥ tad nivṛttau brahma svarūpam eva bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi bhede tad ākāśam pariśuddham parama ākāśam eva bhavati syāt etad  katham bhedena eva bhedaḥ pratisaṃhriyate bheda pratipakṣa tvāt  yathā rajasā rajaḥ iti uktam vyaktam eva bheda atīta brahmaṇi śravaṇa manana dhyāna abhyāsānām bheda darśana pratipakṣa tvam avidyā anubandhe api yathā payaḥ payaḥ  jarayati svayam ca jīryati yathā ca viṣam viṣa antaram śamayati svayam ca śāmyati yathā uktam ‘vidyām ca avidyām ca yaḥ tad veda ubhayam saha avidyayā mṛtyum tīrtvā vidyayā amṛtam aśnuteetad uktam bhavati vidyā avidye dve api upāya upeya bhāvāt sahite na avidyām antareṇa vidyā udayaḥ  asti sādhyā tarhi tathā ca kṛtaka tvāt anitya tvam ata āha avidyayā mṛtyum iti eṣaḥ  arthaḥ na avidyā vidyāyāḥ sādhanam kim tu avidyayā śravaṇa ādi lakṣaṇayā api avidyā eva nivartate mṛtyuḥ iti avidyā eva ucyate tasyām nivṛttāyām vidyā rūpa upalakṣitam amṛtam aśnute svarūpa avasthānam sphaṭika maṇiḥ iva upādhi āśraya nibandhana uparāga tyāgāt antareṇa prayatna antaram vidyā svarūpe avatiṣṭhata iti anyaḥ  arthaḥ na avidyā vidyā rahitā asti tathā hi bheda darśanam api na prakāśa śūnyam tad abhāve na bhedaḥ prakāśeta tasmāt para eva prakāśaḥ tathā tathā prakāśate yathā uktam ‘tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhātiiti kim tu avidyā anubaddhaḥ yathā uktam ‘sarvam darśana m anyūnam avikalpam vikalpitam iva tu ayam āntaraḥ puruṣaḥ  abhimanyatetathā na vidyā aikātmya śravaṇa ādi lakṣaṇā vinā avidyayā śrotṛ śravaṇa ādi vibhāga anubaddha tvāt tatra avidyayā eva vidyā pratyāsannayā vibhāga darśanam avidyām tīrtvā vidyā lakṣaṇe nitye svarūpe avatiṣṭhate pratibimba kaluṣitam iva udakam tad nivṛttau syāt etad  aikātmye vibhāgasya asatya tvāt tad adhiṣṭhāna śravaṇa ādayaḥ  api asatyāḥ katham kasmaicid kāryāya syuḥ asatyāt ca satya pratipattiḥ mithyā eva yathā dhūma iti mithyā gṛhītāt bāṣpāt iti ucyate na ayam niyamaḥ asatyam na kasmaicid kāryāya bhavati iti bhavati hi māyā prīteḥ bhayasya ca nimittam asatyam ca satya pratipatteḥ yathā rekhā gavayaḥ  lipi akṣarāṇi ca syāt etad  svarūpeṇa idam satyam na śūnyam aikātmya vādinaḥ tu sva rūpeṇa api upāyānām asatya tā ucyate santu sva rūpeṇa satyāḥ yena tu rūpeṇa pratipādakāḥ tad asatyam kārya upayoga rahitā svarūpa satyatā vyarthā api ca abheda darśana upāyā api na sva rūpeṇa mithyā yatas  brahma eva eṣām svarūpam tatra brahma eva avidyā anubaddham brahma prāpti upāyaḥ yathā rekhā ādayaḥ ‘ka kāraḥ  ayam gavayaḥ  ayam aitya vidyamāna rūpeṇa eva varṇa ādīnām bodhakāḥ yaḥ  api manyate na rekhā gavayaḥ  gavayatvena gavaya antarāṇām pratipatti hetuḥ na rekhā varṇa tvena kim tu sādṛśyāt  etad sadṛśaḥ  gavaya iti rekhā ca samayāt  īdṛśīm rekhām dṛṣṭvā ayam varṇaḥ smartavya iti tasya loka virodhaḥ tathā hi bālā hi rekhāsu varṇa tvena eva vyutpādyante loke abhedena ca vyapadeśaḥ ‘ayam gavayaḥ aitya ākhyātuḥ pratipattuḥ ca ‘gavayaḥ ayam mayā dṛṣṭaḥiti tathā asatyāt pratibimbāt ca adṛṣṭasya pratibimba hetoḥ viśiṣṭa deśa avasthasya anumānam na mṛṣā śabdāt ca nityāt asatya dīrgha ādi vibhāga bhājaḥ  artha bheda pratipattiḥ na mithyā tathā mithyā ahidaṃśaḥ  maraṇa hetuḥ tatas ca maraṇa mūrcchā ādi anumānam na vitatham kāla ādi bheda yuktāt satya ahi daṃśāt iva yasya eva kṣaṇika jñānam ātmā tasya eva tu upaneya apaneyā sambhavān mokṣa śostrāṇām mukti arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam kṣaṇikasya svarasena eva nirvāṇāt  anādheya atiśaya tvāt ca ekasmin kṣaṇe viśeṣa aviśeṣa vibhāga abhāvāt kṣaṇasya abhedya tvāt  yadi matam santatau= upaneyam apaneyam ca samasti iti tad asat  kartā bhoktā ca saṃsārī na ca santatiḥ avastu tvāt kartrī bhoktrī vā katham vāsataḥ  mukti bandhau atha matam na atyantam asatī santatiḥ na api satī kalpanayā tu satī tad vimokṣāya śāstrāṇi pravṛttayaḥ ca iti kalpitaḥ tarhi saṃsarati vimucyate ca kalpita viṣayau ca saṃsāra vimokṣau= api kalpi tau= eva tad etad asmābhiḥ ucyamānam kim na bhavataḥ  abhimatam uktam etad  kalpita viṣayau= eva saṃsāra mokṣau na parasmin parama arthe api ca abhyupagamya api kṣaṇikam vijñānam anādi nidhanāyā eva santateḥ mukti saṃsārau= abhyupetau tathā hi santateḥ anādi tvāt saṃsārasya avastu tvāt ca na utpādaḥ na ucchedaḥ avastu tvāt antyakṣaṇa anupapatteḥ ca sa hi antyaḥ kṣaṇaḥ kiñcid kāryam ārabheta vā na vā ārambhe na antya iti tad abhāva at na ucchedaḥ anārambhe sarva śakti virahāt asat lakṣaṇāt tasya asattvam tasmin= asati sarve api anena eva krameṇa asantaḥ santāninaḥ syuḥ tad abhāve santāna eva na asti kasya ucchedaḥ atha ārabhata eva kāryam antyaḥ santāna antare sārvajñe sati hetu phala bhāve katham santāna antaram na hetu phala bhāvāt anyat eka santateḥ vyavasthāpakam na hetu phala bhāva mātrāt eka santati vyavasthā api tu upādāna hetu phala bhāvāt na ca sārvajñasya jñānasya cara makṣaṇa upādānam ālambana pratyayaḥ hi saḥ samanantara pratyayaḥ ca upādānam sva santati patita samanantara pratyaya janyam ca sārvajñam jñānam ālambana pratyayaḥ asya cara makṣaṇaḥ yadi tulya jātīyam upādānam na mukta citta sārvajña jñānayoḥ tulya jātīya tā na asti yaḥ  api manyate vilakṣaṇa kārye santati uccheda iti tasya rūpa jñāna prabandhe viṣaya antara vijñānāt nirvāṇa prasaṅgaḥ katham cit tulya tā āyām anirvāṇam iti alam ati prasaṅgena kecid tu vijñāna guṇam avijñāna svabhāvam ātma tattvam icchantaḥ samutkhāta sakala viśeṣa guṇe svarūpe tasya sthitim brahma prāptim āhuḥ sā hi tasya avasthā deha indriya ādi upādhibhiḥ akṛta avacchedā bṛhatī brahma iti gīyate jñāna svabhāva tve ca sarva gatasya deha indriya nirapekṣasya nitya tvāt jñāna svarūpasya sannihita vividha jñeya bhedasya bṛhattaraḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt  atha na vijānāti kiñcid  na tarhi jñāna svarūpaḥ sa karmakaḥ  hi jānātyarthaḥ  na asati karma sambandhe yujyate tān pratyāha vijñānam iti kutas  śrūyate hi ‘satyam jñānam anantam brahma‘vijñānam ānandamityādi na ca ukta doṣaḥ yathā dāha kaḥ  api vahniḥ upanītam dāhyam dahati na anupanītam adāhyam ca yathā ca sphaṭika darpaṇa ādayaḥ su acchāḥ prakāśa svabhāvā api yad eva upanidhīyate yogyam ca tad chāyā āpattyā tad eva darśayanti evam ayam puruṣaḥ  bhoga āyatana śarīra sthaḥ  bhoga sādhana indriya upanītān śabda ādīn bhuṅkte tad chāyā āpattyā nitya caitanyaḥ  api atas ca na sarvasya sarva darśi tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca muktau bāhya viṣaya upabhogaḥ syāt etad  sarva gatasya sarvam eva viṣaya tvena vartate tatra kim upaneyam ucyate yasya api ajñasya ātmanaḥ  jñānam manaḥ saṃyoga ādi janyam tasya api sarva manobhiḥ sarva ātmanām saṃyogāt katham upabhoga vyavasthā manaḥ saṃyoga mukhena sarve hi tad viṣayā viṣaya tve asya vartante atha asya karma nibandhana tvāt upabhogasya karma nimittā vyavasthā sā citi rūpa ātma vādinaḥ  api na daṇḍa vāritā api ca asya abheda darśana pariniṣpattyā sarvasmin= ātma bhāvam āpanne dṛśya abhāvāt eva na darśanam dṛś svabhāvasya api dagdhuḥ iva vahneḥ dāhya abhāvāt na dāhaḥ prakāśasya iva ca prakāśya abhāvāt na prakāśaka tā tad uktam ‘na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyate avināśi tvāt  na tu tad  dvitīyam asti tatas  anyat vibhaktam yad paśyet‘yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūtityādi vijñāna ādi viśeṣa guṇa nivṛtti lakṣaṇā ca muktiḥ uccheda pakṣān na bhidyate na hi sataḥ  api ātyantikaḥ  darśana abhāvaḥ  abhāvāt viśiṣyate kaḥ ca sarvatas  preyasa ātmanaḥ  abhāvam abhikāṅkṣeditya puruṣa arthaḥ  mokṣaḥ syāt  syāt etad  vividha duḥkha upaśama tvāt ātma ucchedaḥ  api puruṣeṇa arthyate dṛśyante hi tīvra pāpa roga grastāḥ sva ucchedāya yatamānāḥ satyam pravṛddha gada unmūlita nikhila sukhā duḥkha mayīm iva mūrtim udvahantaḥ na tu evam saṃsāriṇaḥ  vividha vicitra deva ādi ānanda bhāginaḥ tatra yathā vividha duḥkha uparama tvāt puruṣa artha tvam tathā vividha sukha uparama tvāt apuruṣa artha tvam api yasya tu nirmṛṣṭa nikhila duḥkha anuṣaṅgā parama ānanda saṃvedana avasthā tasya eva aikāntikam puruṣa artha tvam iti alam ati prasaṅgena akṣaram iti śabda ātma tām āha viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya lakṣaṇāt  apariṇāmi tvam vā pariṇāme pūrva dharma nivṛtteḥ kṣaraṇasya bhāvāt  tad vyudāsena katham tāvat śabda ātma tā ‘param ca aparam ca brahma yadā uṅkāraḥ aitya ādi śrutibhyaḥ na ca idam abhidheya apekṣam kāra pratyaya antasya śabda svarūpa paratvāt avarṇāt api varṇa samudāyāt paraḥ kāra pratyayaḥ  dṛśyate ‘eva kāraḥ kimarthaḥ‘kim arthaḥ cakāraḥiti nanu idam anyathā eva vyācakṣate sarva viśeṣa atigasya brahmaṇa upāsitum aśakyatvāt pratīkā upadeśaḥ  ayam asmin= ālambane brahma upāsitavyam yathā devatāyāḥ sākṣāt pūjā sambhavāt tad lāñchane dāruṇī aśmani vā pūjā vidhānam tad buddhyā tathā dhyātā devatā sā prasīdati iti anena vā abhidhānena tad dhyeyam praṇavasya tad abhidhāna tvāt  ucyate ‘om iti ātmānam dhyāyatha‘om iti yuñjīta aiti yatra yoga aṅga tā śrūyate tatra evam yatra tu yuñjīta iti ādeḥ aśravaṇāt tādātmya eva paryavasyati vākyam tatra na ittham yathā ‘om iti brahma om iti idam sarvamiti atra hi sarva vāc anugamena tad atyāgāt oṅkāraḥ  vācaḥ tattvam iti darśayitvā vāc rūpa atyāgāt ca rūpa prapañcasya ‘oṅkāra eva idam sarvam aiti upasaṃharati yatra api ‘etena eva param puruṣam abhidhyāyītaiti śravaṇam tad api sarva ātma bhāva pratipādana pūrvakam na ca sarva ātma bhāva aupacārikaḥ stuti artha iti yuktam mukhya artha tve api avirodhāt sarvasya hi pratyakṣa ādi anavaseyam śāstra gamyam idam rūpam na viruddhyate na hi pramāṇa antareṇa anavagamaḥ pramāṇa antarasya viṣayam apaharati ‘tasmāt vidvāniti ca sārvātma vida eva tena dhyāna upadeśaḥ na ca tad anyatas  tasmāt anantaram eva vākyam tatra paryavasitam tatas  adhigata sārvātmyasya sataḥ  dhyāna upadeśaḥ atha vā ‘vāc eva viśvā bhuvanāni jajñe vāc eva idam bubhuje vāc uvāca aiti ādau vācaḥ sārvātmyam śrūyate tathā vāc sūkte vācaḥ sarva ātma tvam sarva īśi tvam ca pradarśitam ‘aham rudrebhiḥ vasubhiḥ carāmiiti vācā eva yathā ātmani pratibuddhena vāmadevena ‘aham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ caiti api ca prakṛti rūpa anvitā vikārāḥ vāc rūpa anvitam ca jagat  atas  vācaḥ  vipariṇāmaḥ  vivartaḥ  vā avasīyate katham tad anugamaḥ tad uparāga vijñāna vedanīya tvāt tathā hi dhūmāt atra agniḥ iti pratipatteḥ vyadhikaraṇa tayā vyaktam vailakṣaṇyam śabdāt artha avagamasya saṃvedyate sarveṇa itas ca etad evam yaḥ tu śabdayoḥ viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāvaḥ  avagamyate ‘nīlam utpalamiti artha gata eva asau anyathā yathā ‘u ūrdhva tve kāka nilayanāt sthāṇuḥ aiti paraspara vyavacchinnābhyām arthābhyām artha antara pratītiḥ tathā syāt  api ca dhūma iva śabde pratipatti hetau na tādrūpyeṇa niścayaḥ syāt  na ca dhūmāt pramāṇa antarāt vā agnau niścayaḥ  dhūma rūpa anukārī bhavati bhavati tu pramāṇa antarāt api artheṣu niścayaḥ śabda rūpa parāmarśī tad darśanāt śabdāt api pratipattau tathā pratipattiḥ na tu ā anantarya nimittā bhrāntiḥ iti adhyavasyāmaḥ bālānām api ca yā iyam anya parihāreṇa stana ādau pravṛttiḥ sā na ‘idam aitya niścinvatām bhavitum arhati na aniścite sthāṇau puruṣe vā anyatara nibandhanā pravṛttiḥ na ca niścayaḥ śabda anurāga śūnya iti teṣām api pūrva janma śabda bhāvanā bhājām vāc rūpa uparaktam eva jñānam niścīyate tathā ca tad rūpa upagrāhyam jagat tad vivarta iti pratīmaḥ api ca santi arthā vyāvahārikāḥ yeṣām na śabda vivartāt anyat tattvam tad sāmānyāt itare api tathā avasātavyāḥ yathā ‘kuryāt  na kuryātiti vidhi niṣedhau vākya arthaḥ samūhaḥ asantaḥ ca alāta cakra śaśa viṣāṇa ādayaḥ tatra na tāvat vidhi niṣedhau bhūte pravṛtti nivṛttī na ca vartamāne na bhaviṣyantyau apākṣīt pacati pakṣyati iti aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt kārye iti ced  na kāla traya atirekeṇa kāryatvasya anirūpaṇāt  tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛtti anuguṇam avastukam pratibhā mātram vidhi niṣedhaḥ ca syātām na ca anālambanā jñāna svabhāva tvāt pratibhā yuktā na ca sā śabda rūpa parāmarśa vikalā tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛttyā anuguṇyena śabda tattvam eva tathā tathā avabhāsata iti sāmpratam evam vākya arthaḥ saṃsargaḥ  na saṃsargi vyatirekeṇa kaścid  na saṃsargya saṃsargi rūpa atiriktaḥ na jñeya śūnyam jñānam na vikalpa pratyayaḥ vāc rūpa uparāga rahita iti vāc tattvam eva tathā tathā vivartata iti nyāyyam evam samūhe vanāt au= asatsu ca alāta cakra ādiṣu yojanīyam api ca yadi api ṣaḍja ādiṣu gavā ādiṣu ca prāk  śabdāt jñānam asti tathā api na tādṛś  yādṛś  śabda niveśāt uttarasmin kāle aviviktā hi prāk  pratipattiḥ sphuṭatarā vivekavatī paścāt  tathā ca gopāla avi pālāt ayaḥ  viveka jñāna siddhaye saṃjñām niveśayanti evam ca śabda saṃsparśe arthe bodha utkarṣa darśanāt tad pratihāre ca saṃcetitānām api asaṃcetita kalpa tvāt pathi gacchataḥ tṛṇa ādīnām apakarṣāt vāc rūpa adhīnam eva citaḥ citi tvam vāc śaktiḥ eva vā citiḥ tad pratisaṃhāre api sūkṣmā vāc śaktiḥ iti eke sarvathā vāc rūpa adhīnaḥ  jñeya bodha iti sarvam jñeyam vāc rūpa anvitam gamyata iti tad vikāraḥ tad vivartaḥ vā mṛda iva ghaṭa ādayaḥ candramasa iva jala taraṅga candramasa iti anye tu mṛd ādi dṛṣṭānta darśanāt pariṇāmitām brahmaṇaḥ  manyante tad apākriyate akṣaram iti kutas  ‘dhruvaḥ‘nityaḥ aiti tatra tatra śruteḥ atha matam pariṇāmi tve api tattva avighātān na nitya tā vyāhanyate yathā uktam ‘yasmin vikriyamāṇe api tattvam na vihanyate tad api nityamiti satyam tathā api tu yad viśuddham ātma rūpam tasya abhāvāt sarva ātmanā pariṇatau= anitya tvam eka deśa pariṇatau sāvayava tvāt nitya tvam eka tvam ca vyāhanyete tad etad viśuddha tvam nitya tvam eka tvam ca ākāśa kalpe brahmaṇi avakalpate kalpita avacchede akalpita avacchedam api ākāśam anavacchinnam asti eva atha kalpita eka deśa pariṇāmaḥ sa kalpanayā eva iti suṣṭhu uktam akṣaram iti kecid  ‘sarva gandhaḥ sarva rasaḥ aityādi śruteḥ sarva ātma tām brahmaṇa upāgaman evam ca viṣaya upabhoga upapatteḥ prakāśa svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ  viṣayāḥ yuktam yad prakāśeran anya tve tu jaḍānām prakāśanam asambhāvanīyam iti tān pratyāha asarvam iti kutas  ‘a sthūlam anaṇva hrasvamiti sarva bheda uparāga pratiṣedhāt sarva bheda aviyogāt ca anirmokṣaḥ na hi svabhāvāt viyojayitum vastu śakyam vahniḥ iva auṣṇyāt  atha api kathañcid viyojyeta tathā api bheda prapañca prabandhasya anucchedāt viyoga abhāvāt nitya saṃsāritā syāt  sarvathā aśanāyā pipāsā ādi prapañcaḥ  asya ātmā tad prapañcasya ca ucchedaḥ  na iṣyate tatra ekātmya vādinaḥ  anirmokṣaḥ ātma bheda vādinaḥ tu kasyacid ucchinnaḥ kasyacid na iti mukta saṃsāri vibhāgaḥ tasmāt na prapañca ātmakam brahma avidyā vikrīḍitam eva prapañca iti sāmpratam yadi tarhi avidyā krīḍitam eva prapañcaḥ prapañca śūnya tā tarhi parama arthaḥ sā eva astu brahma parama artha tvāt tathā ca prapañca niṣedhena eva tad rūpam śrāvyate ‘sa eṣa na iti na iti‘a sthūlam anaṇva hrasvamiti ca tatra āha sarvam iti etad uktam bhavati brahmaṇaḥ  na sarva ātma tā sarvam tu brahma ātmakam brahma rūpeṇa rūpavat  na tu śūnyam eva nitya mukti prasaṅgena tad artha upadeśa pravṛtti vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt  nitya mukti tve api avidyā nibandhanaḥ saṃsāraḥ iti ced  yadi grahaṇa abhāvaḥ  avidyā katham tarhi tad nibandhanaḥ saṃsāraḥ muktau= api tasya tulya tvāt  tadvat eva na kiñcid prakāśeta atha ayathārtha grahaṇam avidyā na tarhi sarva śūnyatā ‘tena idam pūrṇam puruṣeṇa sarvamiti śruteḥ ‘ātmā eva idam sarvamiti ca sarvasmin= ātma upadeśāt ‘katham asataḥ sat jāyetaiti ca svayam śūnyatāyāḥ  niṣedhāt  bhāvaḥ hi yathāvat aprakāśamānaḥ  adhyasta avidyamāna rūpaḥ prakāśate śūnye tu kva adhyāsaḥ kim prakāśa tām iti nirbīja tā eva syāt  ‘vijñānam ānandamiti rūpa upadeśāt ca na sarva abhāva mātram brahma api tu sarvasya ātmā iti kecid tu kevalasya sukhasya adarśanāt duḥkha āvinā abhāvāt na asti avasthā duḥkha saṃsparśa viviktā iti manyante na hi kaścid jantuḥ sukhī ā iva upalabhyate duḥkhī ā iva vā duḥkha vata eva tu sukham sukha tve avatiṣṭhate tāpavata eva candana saṃsparśaḥ sukham tatra āha abhayam iti sarva bhaya vinirmuktā hi brahma avasthā na ca atra alpīyān api kleśaḥ asakṛt abhaya śruteḥ ‘abhayam vai brahmaityādi tathā hi na svābhāvikam bhayam brahmaṇi ānanda rūpeṇa virodhāt  na āgantukam hetumat  dvitīya abhāvāt tad uktam ‘dvitīyāt vai bhayam bhavatiiti na ca duḥkha nivṛtti rūpam sukham yena duḥkhitasya eva sukham sukha tve avatiṣṭheta iti prapañcitam etad purastāt  aparaḥ prakāraḥ iha kecid muktā abhimatānām api punarāvṛtti bhayam manyante iha hi vijñāna ātmānaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  vibhaktāḥ syuḥ avibhaktā vā svatas  brahmaṇā eva vā vibhajyeran bhoga artham krīḍā artham vibhūti khyāpana artham vā svabhāvāt vā % avidyā nibandhanaḥ  vā tad vibhāgaḥ vijñāna ātmāna eva vā brahma śabda abhidheyāḥ na anyat brahma % teṣām karma avidyā nibandhanaḥ saṃsāraḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ paraspara yogya tā nibandhanaḥ  vā % tatra yogyatā nibandhana tve yogyatāyā anapāyāt punarāvṛtti bhayam apracyutam atha kṛta kārya tvāt na punarāvṛttiḥ sakṛt śabda ādi upalabdhau na punar tad upalabdhiḥ syāt  atha ananta vikārā prakṛtiḥ sarva ātmanā upalabdhau nivartate avikṛta rūpa antara upalabdhaye ca pravartata eva ānantyāt eva tarhi na sarva ātmanā upalabdhiḥ saṃbhavati iti guṇa puruṣa anyatā ākhyātimataḥ  api punarāvṛttiḥ saṃbhāvyeta avidyā pūrva karma nibandhana tve api anādau saṃsāre ananta tvāt karmaṇā ām aniyata vipāka kāla tvāt ca pratisarga avasthāyāḥ  iva mukti avasthāyāḥ  api pratyudāvṛtti bhayam na vyāvartate avidyā nibandhana tve api tasyāḥ  nirhetu tvāt niṣprayojana tvāt ca pravṛtteḥ tathā eva punar  punar  pravṛttiḥ kena vāryate tathā ca suṣupte brahma prāpteḥ pratyudāvṛttiḥ dṛśyate svatantre tu brahmaṇi vibhaktānām jīvānām deha indriya upabhoga hetau= avibhaktānām vā vibhajya bhoga ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ na punar deha ādi bhedaḥ  na sambhāvyate svatantraḥ  hi krīḍayā svātantrya khyāpanena vā svabhāvena vā punar badhnīyāt laukika iva īśvaraḥ atha eṣa karma apekṣaḥ na karmasvasya svātantryam tathā api karmaṇām ānantyāt vipāka kāla niyama abhāvāt ca kalpa śata atikrame api prāpta vipāka kālebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ punar bandhaḥ sambhāvyate yatas  na eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ na hi asya prāyaṇam eva abhivyañjakam api tu deśa kāla ādayaḥ  api tathā hi ekasmin= api dehe krameṇa karma phala bhogaḥ  dṛśyate viruddha jāti bhoga nimittānām ca karmaṇām yugapad āvāpa gamana anupapatteḥ garbha mṛtyūnām ca akarmaṇām vimukti prasaṅgāt  (ṃ=  bh vimukti prasaṅgaḥ edition) tatra ucyate abhayam iti parā hi iyam kṣema prāptiḥ śrūyate na asyām punar saṃsāra bhayam asti na tāvat karma nimittaḥ punar saṃsāraḥ vidyayā prāyaścittena iva akṛta bhogānām anantānām api karmaṇām prakṣayāt  uktam hi ‘jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathāiti tathā ‘kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇiiti athavā vidyayā avidyā nivṛttau pravilīna eva % kartṛ karma phala pravibhāgaḥ tasya kutas  sambhavaḥ na api avidyā nimittaḥ tad pravṛtti hetoḥ abhāvāt  anādiḥ hi avidyā anādi tvāt eva na hetum apekṣate prāc abhāve hi hetu vyāpāraḥ asati prāc abhāve kadā hetuḥ vyāpriyeta na hi sataḥ  hetu kṛtyam asti vidyayā tu ucchinnā prāk asatī pravartamānā na akasmāt pravartitum arhati suṣupte tu vikṣepa mātram nivṛttam tad saṃskāraḥ  agrahaṇam ca na eva nivṛtte anyathā na turīyāt bhidyeta vikṣepa mātra abhāvāt tu brahma prāpti abhidhānam tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam abhayam iti kena punar  pramāṇena asya arthasya samadhigamaḥ na tāvat pratyakṣeṇa tasya etad viparīta bheda viṣaya tvāt na api anumānena tad pūrvaka tvāt na upamānena sādṛśya viṣaya tvāt tasya ca bheda adhiṣṭhāna tvāt  arthāpattiḥ tu viparyaye na bhedam antareṇa kaścid vyavahāra upapadyate yatas  abhedaḥ  api hi pramātṛ ādi vibhāgāt ṛte duravagamaḥ abhāvaḥ  api na bhāva rūpa tattva avagamāya alam na api prapañca abhāva avagamāya pratyakṣa ādiṣu satsu tad asaṃbhavāt āgamaḥ  api na tāvat āpta praṇetṛ kaḥ  atra kramate pramāṇa antara adhigata gocara tvāt na api svatantraḥ vidhi niṣedha rūpa tvāt  tayoḥ ca sthite tattve asaṃbhavāt  na api tad anapekṣam vyavasthita vastu viṣayam eva prāmāṇyam bhūta anuvāda tve pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt lokāt ca śabda sāmarthya adhigamaḥ tatra kārya para tayā eva kārya an vayiṣu artheṣu padāni prayujyante tathā arthavat tvāt na hi pravṛtti nivṛtti śūnyasya vacasaḥ kaścid arthaḥ api ca na bhūta anuvādāt vacasaḥ sambandha anugamaḥ api tu pravartakāt  pravṛttyā hi anumāya artha pratyayam tatra śabdasya sāmarthya pratītiḥ (@ pratīteḥ edition) tathā ca na pravṛtti sambandha rahiteṣu artheṣu śabdānām śaktiḥ gamyate tathā satya nava gata sāmarthyāḥ śabdā bhūte arthe katham tad avagamayeyuḥ api ca pramāṇa antara avasitaḥ ced saḥ arthaḥ na śabdasya tatra prāmāṇyam atha anavasitaḥ natarām apadārtha tve vākya viṣaya tva asambhavāt  padārtha eva hi viśiṣṭa tayā vākya arthībhavati atyanta aparidṛṣṭaḥ tu padāt anavagamyamānaḥ padārtha saṃsarga ātmake vākya arthe na guṇa tvena pradhāna tvena vā anupraveśam arhati api ca pralīna nikhila avacchedam tattvam agocara eva pratipatteḥ sarvā hi pratipattiḥ ‘evam na evamiti vyavacchedena pravartate anyathā na kaścid pratipannaḥ syāt  sarva viśeṣa pratyasta maye tu katham pratipattiḥ syāt iti atra āha āmnāyataḥ prasiddhim ca kavayaḥ  asya pracakṣate bheda prapañca vilaya dvāreṇa ca nirūpaṇām bhūta artha vādi tve api apauruṣeyasya na sa apekṣa tvam iti vakṣyate na ca kārya niṣṭhāni eva loke vacāṃsi tathā hi priya ākhyānāni ‘diṣṭyā vardhase putraḥ te jātaḥiti na pravṛttaye nivṛttaye vā dṛśyante ca sukha utpādana prayojanāni na ca sukhī bhava iti tatra pravṛttiḥ upadiśyate vastu sāmarthyāt eva tad siddheḥ upadeśasya anapekṣaṇāt  atha matam asti tāvat tatra pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ vacasaḥ ca tatra tātparyam satyam utpattyā tātparyam na pratipattyā pratipattiḥ tu bhūta artha niṣṭhā eva na ca bhūta artha paryavasitasya eva śabdasya prayojanavat tve pravṛtti avadhiḥ vyāpāraḥ kalpayitum śakyate api ca upāye vā apravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ pravartyate ajñāta upāya tvāt vā upeye prāc apravṛtta upāya prajñāpana dvāreṇa tatra iha na tāvat upāye putra janmani tasya niṣpanna tvāt  na upeye sukhe tad artha vyāpāra antara abhāvāt tathā durjana vacanāni apriya ākhyānāni viṣāda prayojanāni na pravṛttim nivṛttim vā upadiśanti pūrveṇa eva nyāyena tathā rajju veṣṭitasya sarpa veṣṭitam ātmānam manyamānasya bhaya nivṛttaye tattva ākhyānam dṛśyate na tu tatra ‘mā bhaiṣīḥiti niyogaḥ tatra hi niyogaḥ  bhavati yatra niyoga artham pratibudhya puruṣaḥ  buddhi pūrvam niyoga sāmarthyāt icchayā vā punar  pravartate nivartate vā iha tu tattva pratipatti mātrāt niyoga icchā anapekṣasya hetu abhāvāt eva tasya bhaya nivṛttiḥ na ca bhaya nivṛttau puruṣa artha tvāt svayaṃpravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ  niyojyaḥ na api tad upāye tattva pratipattau ‘rajjuḥ na sarpaḥiti śabdāt eva tad utpatteḥ śabda artha pratipatti uttara kālasya ca vyāpārasya vidhi nibandhana tvāt  tathā dūra deśa vṛttānta ākhyānāni pṛṣṭavatām kutūhalinām autsukya nivṛtti arthāni bhūta artha paryavasitāni na hānāya upādānāya vā yatra api (api ca yatra api edition) bhūta artha pratipattau hānam upādānam vā saṃbhavati ‘eṣa pratirodhakavān adhvā nidhimān eṣa bhū bhāgaḥiti tatra api hāna upādānayoḥ śabdaḥ  vyāpriyate bhūta artha upakṣayāt śabdāt bhūtam artham pratipadya tasya pramāṇa antara avagatām upakāra hetu tām apakāra hetu tām vā saṃsmṛtya icchayā pravartate dveṣeṇa nivartate vā nanu prayoktā buddhi pūrva kārī śrotuḥ pravṛtti artham nivṛtti artham vā vacanam prayuṅkte tathā ca pravṛtti nivṛtti paryavasitam eva idam hi tatra prayoktavyam na prayujyate ‘na gantavyam anena adhvanātathā ‘gṛhāṇa itaḥ nidhimiti na etad sāram bhūta artha paryavasitasya api vacasaḥ  bhūta artha avagama mukhena pravṛtti nivṛtti aṅga bhāvaḥ  yatas  na vyāhanyate pratyakṣa ādīnām iva bhūta artha pramā pari samāpta vyāpṛtayaḥ pratyakṣādayaḥ  mātrayā api agocarīkṛta pravṛtti nivṛttayaḥ na pravṛtti nivṛtti aṅga bhāvam jahati tathā śabdaḥ  api iti na kiñcid praduṣyati prayoktṛ abhisaṃhite pravṛtti nivṛttī iti ced  na prayoktṛ abhisaṃdhānāt śabda artha tvam api tu sāmarthyāt  anyathā nidhi prāpti dvārikā nānāvidha puruṣa artha avāptiḥ api tasya abhisaṃhitā iti śabda arthaḥ syāt  yadā ca pravṛttim nivṛttim vā abhisaṃdhāya kiñcid pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ jijñāsyate tadā abhisaṃhite api pravṛtti nivṛttī na pratyakṣa ādi prameye tadā abhisaṃhite api pravṛtti nivṛttī na śabda arthau itas ca etad evam (itaḥ ca tad evam edition) yad kasyacid upādāna buddhiḥ anyasya upekṣā śabda artha tve hi sarveṣām upādāna buddhiḥ eva syāt  na ca pravartaka vākya vyavahārāt eva sambandha avagamaḥ yena pravṛtti parata eva avagamyeta anyathā api darśanāt  ‘devadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyām odanam pacati aitya vyutpanna kāṣṭha śabda arthaḥ  vyutpanna itara padārthaḥ  vyutpanna vibhakti arthaḥ ca yad pacati arthe karaṇam paśyati tasya kāṣṭha prātipadikā artha tām pratipadyate tathā harṣa viṣāda āśvāsa prayojanebhyaḥ tattva ākhyānebhyaḥ  harṣa ādi nimitteṣu bhavati vyutpattiḥ yathā eva hi pravṛtti viśeṣa darśanāt viśiṣṭa pravṛtti pratyayaḥ tad nimitta pratyayaḥ vā anumīyate hetu antara abhāvāt śabda anantaryāt śabdasya tatra sāmarthyam kalpyate tathā harṣa ādi upalabdheḥ harṣa ādi nimitta pratyaya anumānam śabdān antaryāt ca śabdasya tatra sāmarthya kalpanā pramāṇa antareṇa ca putra janmanaḥ  harṣa nimittasya tasya avagata tvāt anyasya abhāvāt  ‘putraḥ te jātaḥ aiti idam vākyam āptena tatra putra janmani prayuktam iti pratipadyate putra janma eva ca asmāt vākyāt anena pratītam iti avadhārayati tad evam prayoga pratyayābhyām asmin= arthe vākyasya sāmarthyam pratipadyate bhavatu vā loke sarva vacasām pravartaka tā tatas ca sambandha avagamaḥ tathā api idam vicāryam kim vidhāyaka pada vyatirekiṇām padānām sva artha mātra para tā āhosvit kārya artha saṃsarga para tā uta padārtha mātra saṃsarga para tā iti tatra sva artha mātra paryavasāne vākya artha pratyaya abhāvaḥ prayoga vaiyarthyam ca syāt  tasmāt anya artha vyatiṣaṅga para tā tāvatā prayoga pratyayayoḥ upapattau na viśeṣa vyatiṣaṅge pramāṇam asti yaḥ  hi viśeṣa vyatiṣaṅgam kalpayati kalpayati asau= artha antara vyatiṣaṅgam tathā ca vinā api kāryeṇa padārthānām paraspara saṃsargāt viśiṣṭa bhūta artha pratyaya siddhiḥ avaśyam ca etad evam vijñeyam anyathā loke vivakṣā para tvāt padārtha anvayasya tad abhāvāt vede veda artha pratītiḥ na syāt  api ca sarveṣām kārya anvayitve parasparam padārthānām anabhisambandhaḥ tatra na viśiṣṭa padārtha viṣayaḥ  niyogaḥ pratīyeta eka padārtha sādhya eva syāt  atha na viniyoga pratyarthī niyogaḥ viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvāt  pūrvaḥ tarhi viniyogaḥ paścāt niyogaḥ kim atas  asti niyoga atirikta artha anvaye api padasya sāmarthyam niyoga anapekṣam ca paraspara anvitānām iyoga anvayāt na ca niyoga ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ saṃsarga iti pratipādayiṣyate anadhigatam api ramāṇa antareṇa anadhigata sambandham ca sva śabdena śakyam śabdena nirūpayitum viśeṣa pratiṣedha mukhena viśeṣa śabdānām nañaḥ ca yathāyatham arthaiḥ vidita saṅgati tvāt tathā ca ittham eva tad upadiśyate ‘a sthūlam aiti sarva viśeṣa atigam etad kathayati bheda prapañca vilaya dvāreṇa iti etad ca vakṣyata iti anyaḥ  arthaḥ yad uktam pratyasta mita sakala viśeṣam tattvam pratipatteḥ eva aviṣaya iti tatra ucyate viśeṣa nivṛttyā eva tad śabdena buddhau nidhīyate suvarṇa tattvavat na hi suvarṇa tattvam piṇḍa rucaka ādi saṃsthāna bheda upaplava rahitam dṛśyate na ca ta eva suvarṇa tattvam tad parityāge api bhāvāt saṃsthāna antare atha ca adṛṣṭa saṃsthāna bheda upaplava vivekam api buddhyā bheda apoha dvāreṇa svayam pratīyate parasmai ca pratipādyate sa eṣa pratipatti kramaḥ śrutyā eva darśitaḥ ‘sa eṣa na iti na itiiti tathā anyaiḥ ‘satyam ākṛti saṃhāre yad ante vyavatiṣṭhatetathā aparaiḥ ‘adhyāra upāpavādābhyām niṣprapañcam prapañcyateiti idam idānīm vicāryate kim kṛtsna āmnāyaḥ  bheda prapañca vilaya mukhena brahma nirūpayati āhosvit kaścid asya eka deśaḥ tatra kecid āhuḥ sarvatra eva āmnāye kvacid kasyacid bhedasya pravilayaḥ  gamyate yathā ‘svarga kāmaḥ  yajetaiti śarīra ātma bhāvasya pravilayaḥ atra hi deha vyatirikta svarga upabhoga samarthaḥ  adhikārī gamyate tena deha ātma bhāva pravilayaḥ tathā ‘gaḥ dohanena paśu kāmasya praṇayet aiti adhikṛta adhikārāt adhikāri bheda pravilayaḥ tathā vidhi niṣedha codanāsu api naisargi kīṇām rāga ādi nibandhanānām pravṛttīnām pravilayaḥ niṣedheṣu sākṣāt  vidhiṣu pravṛtti antar niyogena loke api anabhipretāt pathaḥ sākṣāt vā nivāraṇam pathi antara upadeśena vā evam ca rāga ādi nibandhana naisargika pravṛtti bheda vilaya dvāreṇa dṛṣṭena eva karma vidhaya ātma jñāna adhikāra upayoginaḥ tathā hi śāntasya dāntasya samāhitasya ca ātmani darśanam upadiśyate śakyam ca na hi viṣayaiḥ ākṛṣyamāṇaḥ tad upāya pravṛtti kṛta cetāḥ śaknoti ātmani samādhātum naisargikībhyaḥ tu pravṛttibhya uparataḥ  niyata mānasa ātma darśanena adhikriyate sāmarthyāt  anye (ṃ=  ā anye tu edition) manyante anavāpta kāmaḥ kāma upahata manā na parama advaita darśana yogyaḥ karmabhiḥ tu kṛta kāma nibarhaṇaḥ sahasra saṃvatsara paryantaiḥ prājāpatyāt padāt parama advaitam ātmānam pratipadyata iti ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ anayoḥ kṛtsna āmnāya ātma jñāna eka paryavasāyī anyeṣām darśanam pṛthakkāryā eva santaḥ karma vidhaya ātma jñāna adhikāram avatārayanti puruṣam anapākṛta ṛṇa trayasya tatra anadhikārāt  ‘ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtya manaḥ  mokṣe niveśayetiti anye tu saṃyoga pṛthaktvena sarva karmaṇām eva ātma jñāna adhikāra anupraveśam āhuḥ ‘vividiṣanti yajñena aiti śruteḥ ‘yena kenacana yajeta api darvīhomena anupahata manā eva bhavatiiti ca anye tu puruṣa saṃskāra tayā ātma jñāna adhikāra saṃsparśam karmaṇām varṇayanti ‘mahāyajñaiḥ ca yajñaiḥ ca brāhmī iyam kriyate tanuḥ‘yasya ete catvāriṃśat saṃskārā aṣṭau= ātma guṇāḥiti ca anye tu etad eva viparītam varṇayanti ātma jñānam eva kartṛ saṃskāra tayā karma adhikāra anupraveśī iti anye tu paraspara virodhinoḥ karma ātma jñānayoḥ dvaita advaita viṣaya tvena asaṃbandha eva iti manyante tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ na hi karma ādi vidhayaḥ sva vākya samadhigata svarga ādi kāryāḥ kārya antaram apekṣante na api ātma jñāna vidhiḥ yathā udita brahmacarya ādi sādhana nirākāṅkṣaḥ karma vidhīn apekṣate tatra kuta eka adhikāra tvam yadi manyeta anavagata kāryā (atha anavagata@ edition) eva karma ādi vidhayaḥ svarga ādīnām guṇa tvena saṃbandhāt iti svarga kāma adhikaraṇam asmai vyācakṣīta api ca sarva vidhi niṣedhānām nāma rūpa pravilaya kārya apavargi tve jantūnām abhyudaya vinipātā akarma nimittā ākasmikāḥ syuḥ tathā apavargaḥ  api syāt iti vaiyarthyam śāstrasya api atha svarga ādi kārya dvāreṇa karma vidhīnām jñāna adhikāra anupraveśitā mārga grāma gamana upadeśānām iva abhimata nagara gamana upadeśa anupraveśi tvam tad asat  yuktam mārga grāma prāpteḥ anabhimata deśa prāpti upadeśa anupraveśi tvam na hi mārga grāma upadeśeṣu puruṣa artha prāptiḥ atas  sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt yatra puruṣa artha prāptiḥ tam anupraviśanti na tu evam karma vidhiṣu puruṣa arthasya alābhaḥ svarga ādīnām puruṣeṇa arthyamāna tvāt  tatra ca naiḥ ākāṅkṣye katham anya anupraveśaḥ atha matam yadā upacchandya nīyata uttarottara grāma guṇa upadarśanena abhipretam deśam tadā pūrva grāma upadeśāḥ prāpta abhimata kāryā upadeśa antara anupraveśinaḥ ca iti yuktam tatra api pramāṇa antareṇa vaktuḥ abhiprāya adhigamāt  pramāṇa antareṇa hi tatra idam adhigatam etad deśa prāpta avidamasya samīhitam vaktuḥ saṃpadyate tasmāt idam asya vivakṣitam iti na tu śabda vṛtti mātra anusāreṇa (śabda pravṛtti mātrā@ ṃs ā śabda vṛtta mātrā@ edition) itas ca etad evam yad pratigrāmam vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca satyām artha prāptau pramāṇa antareṇa anadhigate para deśa prāpti abhiprāye pūrva upadeśān pūrva arthān eva pārśva sthāḥ pratipattāraḥ pratipadyante para deśa upadeśam ca sva artha niṣṭham yadi api vastu sthityā pūrva upadeśa arthāḥ para upakāriṇaḥ tathā api na śabdasya tātparyam dravya arjana ādi vidheḥ iva kratu vidhi artha upakāre api śabda vṛtta anusāreṇa ca iha tātparyam pramāṇa antara abhāvāt iti api ca adhva grāma upadeśānām tad paratva adhyavasāyena eva tatra gamanam artha prāptiḥ ca tatra para deśa prāpti para tāyām tu na niyogataḥ tatra gamanam mārga antareṇa api tad prāpteḥ vivakṣita tvāt gacchet  na ca niyogataḥ  artha prāptiḥ anya pareṣu prayojana śruteḥ api artha vāda tvāt tad iha yadi vidhi niṣedhāḥ kārya antara parāḥ na svarga ādi kāryāḥ na khalu svarga ādi kāryam prayāja ādi kārya tulyam yena kārya antaram anupatet  katham ca dṛṣṭena eva ātma jñāna adhikāra upakāriṇa iti vaktavyam yadi tāvat rāga ādi ākṣipta dṛṣṭa artha pravṛtti nirodhena bhavatu pratiṣedhānām evaṃbhāvaḥ karma vidhayaḥ tu katham nirundhanti iti vācyam na hi te parisaṃkhyāyakāḥ na ca niyāmakāḥ atyantam aprāpta artha tvāt prāpta arthaḥ  hi vidhiḥ anya nivṛtti phalaḥ  vijñāyate na ca tulya kārya tvena virodhena nivṛttiḥ aniyata kālaphalā hi naiyogikyaḥ pravṛttayaḥ  adṛṣṭa arthāḥ dṛṣṭa arthāḥ tu rāga ādi ākṣiptāḥ svābhāvikyaḥ na ca sa aṅgrahaṇyāḥ sevāyāḥ ca grāma upāya tve kaścid virodhaḥ etāvati pramāṇa tvāt śāstrasya tatra yugapad krameṇa vā phala bhūma arthinaḥ sevāsa aṅgrahaṇyau= anutiṣṭhataḥ kaḥ  virodhaḥ api ca sakala dṛṣṭa artha pravṛtti nirodhe niyoga niṣṭhā api pravṛttayaḥ  nirudhyeran anārjita dhanasya sādhana vikalasya tāsām asambhavāt  api ca tulye kāma upāya tve dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha pravṛttyoḥ na na viśeṣaḥ  rāga ādi ākṣipta tve tathā hi ‘svarga kāmaḥ aiti rāga ādi ākṣipta pravṛtti anuvādena viśeṣa vidhānam tathā ca prapañca abhiniveśe tulye kena viśeṣeṇa eka ātma anuguṇyam bhajate tad virodhinī aparā kāma ākṣepaḥ  hi aviśiṣṭaḥ  manasaḥ atha kāma upāya tvam eva na manyeta varṇitam āka smika tvam uktaḥ ca nyāyaḥ pratyuddhriyeta tulya kārya nibandhana tvāt ca virodha ādyā nirodha āśaṅkā sā dūratas  nirasta avakāśā syāt  atha kāma prāptyā karma vidhayaḥ kāmān pravilāpayantaḥ  jñāna adhikāra anuguṇāḥ yathā uktam ayadā sarve pramucyate kāmā ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ atha martyaḥ  amṛtaḥ  bhavati atra brahma samaśnuteiti tad api asat yatas  na kāma prāptyā kāma pravilayaḥ api tu doṣa paribhāvanābhuvā prasaṅkhyānena kalayā api ced kāmaiḥ manaḥ saṃspṛśyate hriyata eva hāribhiḥ uktam hi ‘na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati‘bhoga abhyāsam anu vivardhante rāgāḥ kauśalāni ca indriyāṇāmiti ca anupāya tvāt api tāvat ayam kāmebhyaḥ  vinivarteta nikhila kleśa upaśama rūpam ca ātma jñānam saṃśrayeta karma vidhi nidarśita vividha upāyaḥ tu tān eva prakṛta hāriṇaḥ  bhogān abhiniviśeta tad pravilaya rūpāca ātma jñānāt udvijeta śrutaḥ  api hi ātmani ānandaḥ  ananubhūtaḥ  na anubhūta viṣaya nibandhana ānanda abhilāṣam mandīkartum api utsahate prāk eva ucchettum tasmāt prasaṃkhyānam eva ekaḥ kāma nibarhaṇa upāyaḥ karma vidhayaḥ tu viparyaya hetavaḥ yad api sarvatra eva āmnāye kvacid kasyacid bhedasya vilayaḥ yathā ‘svarga kāmaḥ  yajetaiti śarīra ātma tva pravilaya iti tad api asat anidaṃpara tvāt  na hi idam vacanam deha vyatirikta ātma tattva avabodha param atha anya parāt api arthāt evam avasīyata iti tad api hastini dṛṣṭe tad padena tasya anumānam iva sākṣāt hi ‘a sthūlam aiti upakramya deha indriya vilayaḥ  darśitaḥ arthāt ca kāma ādi grantheḥ kāṭhinyam vaidikam syāt iti dvitīyaḥ  api kalpaḥ  varṇitāt eva kāmānām kāma nibarhaṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt sva kārya nirākāṅkṣāṇām ca anya anupraveśe pramāṇa bhāvāt asamañjasaḥ eka adhikāra tve tu samuccayaḥ sarva karmaṇām syāt  sa ca aśakya iti ye api viparyayeṇa jñāna karmaṇoḥ eka adhikāra tvam āhuḥ taiḥ api jñānasya karma sambandhe pramāṇam vaktavyam na tāvat  ‘brīhīn prokṣatiiti yathā tatra hi prakaraṇāt prakṛta karma apūrva lakṣaṇa aparaḥ  brīhi śabdaḥ sva svarūpa ānarthakyāt prakṛta apūrva sambandham bodhayati na api yathā ‘yasya parṇa mayī juhūḥ bhavatiiti tatra hi juhvādi avyabhicarita karma sambandham asati api prakaraṇe karma upasthāpayati tatra vākyena eva sambandhaḥ ātma jñānam tu na prakaraṇe śrutam na api ātma avyabhicarita karma sambandhaḥ tena asya karma sambandhaḥ durvacaḥ tathā ca ajñāte pārārthye yā nāma phala śrutiḥ na sārtha vādinī bhavati iti pṛthak adhikāra tvam atha matam vartamāna apadeśāt ‘na sa (ca edition) punar āvartate aiti kāma upabandha abhāvāt phalam vipariṇamayya kalpayitavyam tad ca tad ākāṅkṣāyām satyām na tu dṛṣṭe sati tad ākāṅkṣā asti ca ātma jñāna vidheḥ dṛṣṭa phalam deha antara upabhogya phaleṣu karmasu pravṛttiḥ tasmāt svādhyāya adhyayana vidhivat ātma jñāna vidhiḥ svādhyāya adhyayana vidhiḥ hi dṛṣṭa karma avabodha nirākāṅkṣaḥ  na artha vādataḥ phalam prārthayate tathā ātma jñāna vidhiḥ api iti na adhikāra antaram tad api asat yatas  ayam anya eva aupaniṣadaḥ puruṣaḥ  vedānteṣu jijñāsyate na ca tad jñānam karma pravṛtti hetuḥ na hi tasya kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tve evam hi āha ‘na tad aśnāti kiñcana‘anaśnan= anyaḥ abhicāka śītiiti yaḥ tu karmaṇām kartā bhoktā ca sa eva sarva pratyakṣa siddhaḥ na śabda prameyaḥ nanu jīva paramātmanoḥ eka tvam eva evam hi āha ‘anena jīvena ātmanāiti satyam tasya eva tu jīvasya evam avidyā anubandham pratyakṣa avaseyam rūpam tad ca karma pravṛtti hetuḥ na ca tad śabdam apekṣate yad tu svayaṃprakāśam sarva vibhāga śūnyam tad śabdāt jñātum iṣyate tad ca karma pravṛtti virodhi tad jñānasya katham karma pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭam prayojanam syāt  tathā hi brahma ānandam ekam advayam ātmānam vijānataḥ kimartham katham vā pravṛttiḥ syāt  āpta kāma tvāt sādhana ādi upāya abhāvāt ca syāt etad  aupaniṣada puruṣa jñānam eva karma aṅga tvena coditam ‘yat eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayā upaniṣadā tad eva vīryavattaram bhavatiiti tathā ‘yaḥ  vā etad akṣaram gārgya viditvā asmin= loke juhoti aiti upakramya yāga ādi phalasya antavat tā darśanena brahma vidyāyāḥ tādarthyam darśitam ‘tam vidyā karmaṇī samanvārabheteiti ca vidyā karmaṇoḥ sāhityam darśitam pūrvam tāvat prakṛta udgītha viṣayam ‘om iti etad akṣara mudgīthamiti upakramāt  pareṇa api karma nindayā akṣara jñāna stutiḥ vidyā karmaṇoḥ ca samanvārambhaḥ  bhedena vidyāvantam vidyā an vārabhate karmavantam karma iti tasmāt evam api na karma jñānayoḥ eka adhikāra tvam iti ye api virodhāt asambandha eva karma jñānayoḥ ‘dvaita viṣayam karma advaita viṣayam jñānam aiti manyante teṣām anutpāda eva advaita jñānasya prasajyate pramāṇa ādi vibhāgā dvaita pratipattyoḥ virodhāt  atha upāya upeyayoḥ ayaugapadyāt avirodhaḥ pralīyata eva advaita pratipattau sarvaḥ  vibhāgaḥ na ca virodhaḥ  anupāya tvam vā upāyasya pūrva kāla tvāt  tadā ca tasya apralīna tvāt bheda eva ca abheda pratipattau= upāyaḥ na tarhi karmabhiḥ api virodhaḥ upāya tvāt eva syāt etad  asādhya tvāt brahmaṇaḥ  na karmaṇām upayogaḥ  vidyate śrūyate ca ‘nāsti akṛtaḥ kṛtenaiti na ca jñāna utpattau= upayogaḥ jñānasya pramāṇa adhīna tvāt  na ca jñāna sahakārīṇi karmāṇi jñānasya sādhya antara abhāvāt na tasya mokṣaḥ sādhyaḥ anitya tva prasaṅgāt  atha bandha hetu vicchedaḥ sādhya iti tasmin vicchinne tad abhāvāt mucyate kaḥ punar bandha hetuḥ anādya vidyā na tarhi pṛthak ta d vicchedaḥ sādhyaḥ yatas  vidyā udaya eva avidyā vyāvṛttiḥ syāt etad  bhavatu agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa avidyā vyāvṛttiḥ vidyā utpādaḥ yatas  bhāva eva abhāva vyāvṛttiḥ na ca vidyā utpāda eva viparyāsa jñāna vyāvṛttiḥ na khalu bhāva antaram bhāva antara vyāvṛttiḥ na ca paraspara abhāva ātmānaḥ  bhāvāḥ abhāva tva prasaṅgāt  yadi manyeta tattva agrahaṇa nimittaḥ  viparyāsaḥ  nimitta nivṛttau svayam eva nivartiṣyate tad ca na na khalva grahaṇam abhāvaḥ kasyacid nimittam mūrcchā ādiṣu prasaṅgāt  kim tarhi nimittam ‘anādira prayojanā ca avidyāiti uktam tatra ca hetu anuyogaḥ  niravakāśaḥ viparyāsa tad saṃskārayoḥ ca paraspara hetu phala bhāvena vyavasthānāt na doṣaḥ atas  viparyaya jñānasya nivṛttiḥ vidyayā sādhyeti tatra jñānasya sahakārī apekṣā syāt  etad ca vārtam na khalu śuktikā ādiṣu viparyāsa pura ssaram samupajāta samyak jñānāḥ tad nivṛttaye pṛthak  prayatante sahakāri vā anyat apekṣante yatas  virodhi bhāva antara utpāda eva pūrva pradhvaṃsaḥ na śūnyam anyathā na pradhvaṃsaḥ  hetumān syāt  virodhinī ca vidyā viparyaya jñānasya tad utpattau viparyāsaḥ  naṣṭa eva bhavati atha ucyeta karmāṇi bandha hetavaḥ tad kṣayaḥ  jñānāt sahakāri savyapekṣāt iti tad ca pramṛṣṭa aśeṣa viśeṣa viśuddha jñāna udaye kutas  sambhavaḥ tathā ca viparyāsa saṃśayābhyām tulyavat prasaṃkhyātāni karmāṇi abhidyante hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvareiti atha vijñāna vaimalyāya anya apekṣā sā api mudhā saṃśaya viparyāsayoḥ jñāna malayoḥ pramāṇa uttha vijñāne asaṃbhavāt  atha matam śābda jñānāt anyat api pratyakṣam jñānam iṣyate vigalita vibhāga udgrāham sarva vikalpa atītam tasya hi brahma gocaraḥ na śābdasya vibhakta padārtha saṃsarga udgrāhiṇaḥ tad utpattau karma upāsana ādi apekṣā iti kaḥ punar asya viśeṣaḥ yena tad arthyate spaṣṭa ābha tvam na tasya upayogaḥ jñānam hi jñeya abhivyāptaye śābda jñāne ca utpanna āptam eva jñeyam pramiteḥ pratyakṣa paratvāt tatra ca naiḥ ākāṅkṣyāt tad arthyata iti ced  etad adhigate prameye kim anyat ākāṅkṣyeta pramāṇa antaram iti ced na prameya siddhi artha tvāt tad ākāṅkṣāyāḥ punar  siddhi artham iti ced na pūrvasmāt api asakṛt tad siddheḥ siddhasya ca siddhi apekṣāyām na hetuḥ asti upāya antara sadbhāvaḥ ced  upāya antaram tarhi apekṣeta prameye tu naiḥ ākāṅkṣyam eva prīti viśeṣaḥ ced  sa pūrva pramāṇa jāt api darśanāt sidhyati na tad siddhi artham pramāṇa antaram pratyakṣa dṛṣṭam api itaraiḥ tad sambhavāt jijñāsyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt niścāyaka tvam itareṣām api pramāṇa bhāvāt  hāna ādi yogya viṣayam pratyakṣam sannikṛṣṭa artha tvāt na itarāṇi iti ced  sannikarṣa hetuḥ tarhi apekṣya tām na pramāṇam siddha tvāt pramāyāḥ prakṛte ca prameye na eṣa viśeṣaḥ  asti sāmānya viṣayāḥ śabda ādayaḥ viśeṣa viṣayam pratyakṣam iti ced  anadhigata eva tarhi śabdena pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ bāḍham uktam etad  na śābdasya jñānasya viṣayaḥ  brahma iti yadi tarhi na śabdena adhigatam brahma katham tasmin= upāsanā pravartatām na ca anyasmin= upāsyamāne anyat sākṣāt bhavati kasya ca rūpasya sākṣātkaraṇāya yajña ādi vidhānam śabda upadarśita niratiśaya ānanda apahata pāpma ādi rūpa brahma svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ sākṣātkaraṇāya yajña ādi vidhiḥ upapadyate avidita puruṣa artha rūpe tad viparīta rūpe nirvicikitsāt pramāṇāt prakaṭa tām prāpte na aparam apekṣyam asti nanu avagate api ‘tattva m asiiti śabdāt brahma ātma bhāve prāk iva sāṃsārika dharma darśāt tad nivṛttaye bhavati anya apekṣā na etad sāram katham khalu avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ  vidita ātma yāthā tathyaḥ  mithyā darśana nimittaiḥ dharmaiḥ yujyate śrūyate ca ‘brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatiiti na ca brahmaṇi apahata pāpmani teṣām avakāśaḥ tathā ‘a ātmānam ced vijānīyāt ayam asmi iti pūruṣaḥ kim icchan kasya kāmāya śarīram anusañjvarettathā ‘a śarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥiti mithyā abhimāna nimittaḥ śarīra sambandhaḥ tasmin yāthātathya darśanāt nivṛtte aśarīra tvam tatra priya apriyayoḥ asambandha ākhyāyate tasmāt na avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ prāk iva sāṃsārika dharma bhāj  yaḥ tu tathā na asau= avagata brahma ātma bhāva iti atra ucyate niścite api pramāṇāt tattve sarvatra mithyā avabhāsā nivartante hetu viśeṣāt anuvartante api yathā dvi candra diś viparyāsa ādaya āpta vacana viniścita diś candra tattvānām tathā nirvicikitsā dāmnāyāt avagata ātma tattvasya anādi mithyā darśana abhyāsa upacita balavat saṃskāra sāmarthyāt mithyā avabhāsa anuvṛttiḥ tad nivṛttaye asti anyat apekṣyam tad ca tattva darśana abhyāsaḥ  loka siddhaḥ yajña ādayaḥ ca śabda pramāṇakāḥ abhyāsaḥ  hi saṃskāram draḍhayan pūrva saṃskāram pratibadhya sva kāryam santanoti yajña ādayaḥ ca kena api adṛṣṭena prakāreṇa śreyaḥ paripanthi kaluṣa nibarhaṇa dvāreṇa iti anye nityānām karmaṇām durita kṣaya artha tvāt syāt etad  anuvartantām mithyā avabhāsāḥ pramāṇāt tu niścayaḥ yathātattvam yathā niścayam ca vyavahāraḥ tasmānāvagata ātma tattvasya kācana śubha aśubhā vā pravṛttiḥ upapadyate ucyate jāte api tattva darśane anāhite ca paṭau saṃskāre draḍhiyasi ca mithyā darśana je saṃskāre niścayā api mithyārthā bhavanti yathā diś mūḍhasya ananusaṃhita āpta vacasaḥ prāk iva pravṛtti darśanāt  tathā pramita rajju bhāvāyā api rajjvāḥ pramāṇa ananu sandhāne sarpa bhrāntyā bhaya darśanam tasmāt jāte api pramāṇāt tattva darśane anādi mithyā darśana abhyāsa pariniṣpannasya draḍhīyasaḥ saṃskārasya abhibhavāya ucchedāya vā tattva darśana abhyāsam manyante tathā ca ‘mantavyaḥ  nididhyāsitavyaḥiti ucyate śama dama brahmacarya yajña ādi sādhana vidhānam ca anyathā kaḥ tad upadeśa arthaḥ syāt etad  brahmacarya ādi sādhana karaṇāt eva āmnāyāt tattva vijñānam tad asat  śabda mātrāt pratipatteḥ utpatteḥ na hi prāk  sādhana viśeṣebhyaḥ tattva pratipatti para āmnāyaḥ  avācakaḥ na api aniścāyakaḥ aśeṣa āśaṅkā nirmokṣāt anyathā tad upadiṣṭeṣu sādhaneṣu api durlabhā pratipattiḥ api ca anyathā niścaye api raṅga gatā bharata ādayaḥ  mithyā avabhāsena śoka bhaya ādi hetavaḥ niścite api guḍasya mādhurye tatra mithyā tikta avabhāsaḥ  avitatha iva duḥkhayati avitathasya iva tasya api dhūtkṛtya tyāgāt  tasmāt tad nivṛttaye viniścita brahma ātma bhāvena api sādhanāni apekṣyāṇi yathā eva pramāṇāt tattva abhivyaktau na mukteḥ kārya tā tathā abhivyakti viśeṣe api sādhanebhyaḥ śrutayaḥ tu abhyāsa pariniṣpatti avasthā viṣayāḥ śabda sādhana jñāna apekṣā vā bhavantu tad hetu tvāt uttarasya iti alam ati vistareṇa yad api pṛthakkāryā eva karma vidhayaḥ  jñāna adhikāram avatārayanti apākṛta ṛṇa trayasya tatra adhikārāt tad api na niyogataḥ āśrama vikalpasya smaraṇāt  ‘tassya āśrama vikalpam eke‘yam icchet tamavasetiti ‘yadi vetarathā brahmacaryāt eva pravrajetiti śravaṇāt  ‘etat ha sma vai tad pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ  agnihotram na juhavāñcakriretathā ‘kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥtathā ‘kimarthā vayam adhyeṣyāmahe kimarthā vayam yakṣyāmaheiti karma tyāga darśanāt  pratipannaga arhasthyasya ātma vidyayā eva kṛtakṛtyatām manvānasya ṛṇa apākaraṇam pratyanādṛtasya vihita akaraṇa nimittasya pāpmanaḥ  vidyā udaya pratibandhṛ tvam darśayati ‘ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtyaiti idam tu yuktam kārya antara nirākāṅkṣāṇām api karmaṇām saṃyoga pṛthaktvāt  ‘tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti yajñenaiti vidyā aṅga bhāvaḥ saḥ  api utpatti artha tayā na prayāja ādivat kāya upayogena vidyāyāḥ kārya antara abhāvāt  saṃskāra pakṣaḥ  vā smṛteḥ saṃskṛtasya hi vidyā utpatteḥ tad uktam ‘vihita tvāt ca āśrama karmā apiiti nanu dṛṣṭa utpāya eva vidyā utpādaḥ tatra dṛṣṭā eva iti kartavya tāpekṣyatām śama dama ādi sādhana viśeṣaḥ citta vikṣepasya vihantrī sama hita cittasya ābhasataḥ  jñāna prasāda utpatteḥ na tu yajña ādayaḥ taiḥ vinā api abhyāsena tad sambhavāt satyam tathā ca ūrdhvaretasām ca āśramiṇām vinā api taiḥ viśuddha vidyā udaya iṣyate kim tu kāla kṛtaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sādhana viśeṣāt hi sā kṣipram kṣiprataram ca vyajyate tad abhāve cireṇa ciratareṇa ca tad uktam ‘sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśvavateṣaḥ  arthaḥ ‘yajñena dānena aiti śravaṇāt karmāṇi apekṣyante vidyāyām abhyāsa labhyāyām api yathā antareṇa api aśvam grāma prāptau siddyantyām śaighryāya akleśāya vā aśvaḥ  apekṣyate nanu vidyā rūpam brahmā eva na vidyā brahmaṇaḥ  anyā tad ca nityam akāryam tatra katham kiñcid apekṣyeta ucyate yathā upadhāna tirohita rūpa sphaṭika maṇiḥ upadha avakarṣaṇam svarūpa abhivyaktaye apekṣate tathā iha api draṣṭavyam na hi sphaṭika maṇeḥ pūrvarūpam vinaṣṭam upadhāna sannidheḥ tad apagame vā anyat utpannam na hi akasmāt aneka visabhā ga kṣaṇa vyavahitasya pūrva sabhā ga kṣaṇasya utpattiḥ sambhavati na hi agni vigame aṅgārebhyaḥ punar  kāṣṭha santati pravṛttiḥ tasmāt yathā eva akāryam sphaṭika rūpam upadhāna avakarṣaṇam apekṣate tathā ātma rūpam api syat etad  jñānam tatra sa apekṣam tad ca sphaṭikāt bhinnam kāryam puruṣa prayatnaḥ  hi tatra jñāna arthaḥ kim punar jñānam sva rūpeṇa eva arthitam āhosvit artha svabhāva siddhaye na tāvat svarūpeṇa arthena vyavahārat  na vijñāna mātra nibandhanaḥ  vyavahāraḥ mithyājñānena api prasaṅgāt  atha artha svabhāya jñānam arthyeta tad arthaḥ  vyāpāraḥ tena arthitaḥ  bhavati na ca jñānāt arthe kaścid vikāraḥ tayoḥ asaṃbandhāt yogya deśa tāyāḥ sarvatra bhāvāt  sarva pratipad tṛṇām ca vidita tva prasaṅgāt  dhvasta anāgateṣu ca tad asaṃbhavāt tasmāt yathā atirohitam api tirohitam iva abhivyajyata iva prayatna apekṣam tathā ātma tattvam api atirohitam tirohitam iva prayatnāt abhivyajyata iva iti puṣkalam saṃhṛta akhila bhedaḥ  atas  sāmānya ātmā sa varṇitaḥ hema iva pārihārya ādi bheda saṃhāra sūcitam yatas ca viśeṣa pratyasta mukhena tad nirūpaṇam atas  anyaiḥ brahma vidyā abhiyuktaiḥ sāmānya rūpam brahma nirūpitam ‘sa eva mahān aja ātmā sattā lakṣaṇaḥtathā ‘sattā eva sarva bheda yoniḥ prakṛtiḥ parāiti yathā suvarṇa tattvam kaṭaka aṅgulīya ādi viśeṣa upasaṃhāreṇa nirūpyamāṇam tad sāmānyam iti ye vā ‘nirviśeṣam na sāmānyam bhavet śaśa viṣāṇavat aiti abhāvam āhuḥ tān pratyucyate saṃhṛta akhila bheda iti yadi tāvat asāmānya tvam sādhyate siddha sādhanam viśeṣāṇām abhāve keṣāṃ tad sāmanyam sāmanyam tu uktam brahma vādibhiḥ viśeṣa pratyasta mukhena nirūpaṇāt upacārataḥ atha abhāva eva sādhyaḥ viśeṣaiḥ eva asya nirviśeṣaiḥ vyabhicāra iti iti śrīmat maṇḍana miśra viracitāyām brahma siddhau brahmakāṇḍaḥ samāptaḥ editiā ūn auriginally bhrahma and tharka kāṇḍas ṭere togetheḥ  Vacaspati doeḥ  na ut knoṭ this division tarkakāṇḍaḥ nanu pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ vyāvṛttānām bhāva svabhāvānām avagamāt na ekasmin= advaye śabdaḥ pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt grāva plavana ādi arthavacaḥvat  ucyate āhuḥ vidhātṛ pratyakṣam na niṣeddhṛ vipaścitaḥ na ekatva āgamaḥ tena pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate nanu pramāṇa antara para tantrāṇām puruṣa vacasām tad virodha ādi uktam apramāṇa tvam svatantrasya tvāmnāyasya anapekṣita pramāṇa antara pravṛtteḥ tad virodhe api kasmāt apramāṇa tvam āmnāya virodhāt eva tu pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇa tāyāḥ kim iti na cyavante tulye anapekṣa tve na viśeṣa hetuḥ asti tatra vṛthā pramāṇa antara virodha parihāra pariśrama iti tatra kecid āhuḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodhe āmnāyasya daurbalyam sa apekṣa tvat tathā hi svarūpa siddhi artham eva tāvat pratyakṣa ādīni āmnāyaḥ  apekṣate tathā ca teṣām prāmāṇyam anumantavyam tad apabādhane svarūpasya eva tāvat asiddheḥ na tu evam āmnāye pratyakṣa ādīnām kācid apekṣā dṛṣṭa vyabhicāra tvāt ca śabdasya pratyakṣasya ca adṛṣṭa vyabhicārāt  api ca sa avakāśa anavakāśayoḥ anavakāśam balavat  anavakāśāḥ ca pratyakṣa ādayaḥ sa avakāśaḥ tu śabdaḥ  gauṇena arthena tathā hi śakyam eka tvam abheda śrutīnām upacaritam avakāśaḥ  varṇayitum avivakṣita arthānām vā vedāntānām japa upayogaḥ  avakāśaḥ upaniṣadaḥ  vedāntā iti varṇitam kim ca vyākula tvāt āmnāyasya avyākula tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām karma vidhayaḥ  hi bheda āśrayā abheda āśrayāḥ ca vedāntāḥ paraspara parāhatā asatī api pramāṇa antara virodhe durlabha prāmāṇyāḥ kim punar avyāhata pratiṣṭhita prāmāṇya ādi virodhe tasmāt idam avirodhāya prayatyata iti mukhya tvāt ca mukhyā hi pratyakṣa ādayaḥ jātasya jantoḥ apara kāla āmnāyaḥ sa taiḥ pratiṣṭhita arthaiḥ apahṛta viṣayaḥ kalpanīya arthaḥ  bādhyate tad anusāreṇa vā artha kalpanām arhati arthataḥ  api ca mukhya tā pratyakṣa ādīnām pada padārtha vibhāga adhīna āmnāya artha paricchedaḥ sa ca pratyakṣa ādiṣu āpatate atas  avirodhāya prayatyata iti anye manyante tulya bala tve api pratyakṣa ādīnām āmnāyasya ca vastuni vikalpānupapatteḥ virodhe saṃśayaḥ syāt  tena avirodha upapādyata iti anyat darśanam āmnāya eva balavān= tad virodhe ‘paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam prakṛti vat‘pūrva ābādhena na utpattiḥ uttarasya hi sidhyatiiti tathā hi sarvasya nisarga jaḥ pratyakṣa ādi nibandhanaḥ kila vibhakta vastu paricchedaḥ tad apekṣaḥ tu tad pūrva kaḥ anisarga jaḥ kasyacid eva agantuḥ advaita avagamaḥ sa pūrvam anupamṛdya udetum aśaknuvan= tad apabādha ātmā udīyate itas ca saṃbhavat vicitra vibhrama hetu tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām vigalita nikhila doṣa āśaṅka tvāt ca āmnāyasya puruṣa āśrayāṇām hi doṣāṇām śabde puruṣa abhāve asaṃbhavāt  śakyaḥ  hi āmnāyāt eva anādiḥ avidyā saṃskāraḥ  vibhrama hetuḥ pratyakṣa ādiṣu saṃbhāvayitum niścetum ca deha ātmā abhimāna iva na tu evam apauruṣeye śabde kācid doṣa āśaṅkā satyām vā pramāṇam eva na syāt  pratyakṣa ādīnām tu vyāvahārikam prāmāṇyam avidyā saṃskārsya sthemnā vyavahāra viparyaya abhāvāt yatra ca vyavahāra viparyayaḥ  na tatra prāmāṇyam śabde tu saṃbhāvita doṣe na tattva āvedanena prāmāṇyam na vyavahāra aviparyayeṇa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt doṣebhyaḥ  vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna darśanāt ca pratyakṣa ādīnām tu vyavahāre saṃvādān na śakyate vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna hetuḥ doṣaḥ kalpayitum vyavahāra viparyayāt hi sa kalpyeta tattva darśanasya tu vedānta janmanaḥ pratipakṣa tvāt tattva pratihati mātra hetuḥ eva anādiḥ avidya anubandhaḥ kalpyate tatas  doṣa anubandhaḥ prāmāṇyam ca iti na virodhaḥ śabdaḥ tu saṃbhāvita doṣaḥ  durlabha prāmāṇya eva syāt  dṛśyate hi doṣebhyaḥ  vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna utpattiḥ tatra doṣa āśaṅkayā vyavahāra visaṃvādasya śaṅkita tvāt tattva pratighātasya ca na tattva āvedana lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam na vyavahāra avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇam iti tasmāt śabdasya prāmāṇya abhyupagame pramāṇa antara virodhe api tasya eva balavat tvam iti sāṃpratam yad tu pratyakṣa ādi apekṣaṇāt iti tatra ucyate na pramitau= apekṣāvattā śabdasya pratyakṣa ādiṣu kim tu sva rūpa siddhau anyathā pramāṇam eva na syāt  tathā ca sva kārye apekṣa tvāt na pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ  hīyate pratyakṣādayaḥ  pi sva rūpa siddhau na anya anapekṣāḥ kārye hi sa apekṣa tvam sāmarthyam apakarṣati iti yad tva iteṣām prāmāṇyam anumātavyam iti kaḥ  vānyathā āha vyavahāra avisaṃvādi lakṣaṇam tu tad  na tattva āvedana lakṣaṇam vyāvahārika prāmāṇya upetebhyaḥ pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ siddhāt āmnāyāt tattva darśanam tad virodhāt teṣu tattva darśana aṃśam eva apabādhate na vyavahāra avisaṃvāda aṃśam dṛṣṭam ca hetu tvena apekṣitāyāḥ  api pūrvasyāḥ pratipatteḥ parasyāḥ pratipatteḥ balīyaḥ tvam yathā dūra stheṣu vanaspatiṣu hasti pratipattibhyaḥ  vanaspati pratipatteḥ apekṣitā hi hasti pratipattayaḥ  vyakta vanaspati pratipattyā hetu tvena na tasyāḥ  indriya artha saṃnikarṣa mātrāt janma āpāte abhāvāt  na ca deśa viśeṣāt  tad deśa sthasya eva utpatteḥ tasmāt puras vartiṣu vanaspatiṣu praṇihita manasaḥ prācya viparyāsa anugatam ati saṃskāra saciva indriya ādi saṃyoga kāri tā sā iti mantavyam evam eka ādi saṃkhyā buddhi apāyā viṃśati ādi buddhayaḥ api udāhāryāḥ evam ca yad eke varṇayanti svayam eva vyāhatā vedānta artha pratipattiḥ nābhedaḥ  bhedam antareṇa śakyaḥ  avasātum bheda upāyā hi tasya pratipattiḥ tatra abhedaḥ samākṣipta bheda eva pratāyata iti vyāghātaḥ tad apāstam yata upāyam ākṣipati pratipattiḥ na upāyasya parama artha tām mithyājñānāt api tattva pratipatteḥ vyāvahārikam ca bhedasya satya tvam iṣṭam eva iti vyabhicāra darśanam ca duṣṭa hetu janmanoḥ śabda pratyakṣayoḥ samānam itarayoḥ api tulyam avyabhicāri tvam tathā anavakāśa tvam api yadi khalu ekam advayam vedānta arthaḥ kaḥ teṣām anyaḥ avakāśaḥ atha aupacārika tvam eka tvam tad arthaḥ  avivakṣita artha tā vā japa upayoginām tatra virodha eva na asti iti bala abala cintā na avatarati tad kutas  sa avakāśa tvena daurbalyam katham ca mukhyam artham ati laṅghya upacaritaḥ  avakāśaḥ katham vautpattike śabdasya artham prati śeṣa bhāve ‘dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam‘a viśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaḥ aiti ca avivakṣita artha tā pramāṇa antara virodhāt iti ced  vārtam etad  na pramāṇasya pramāṇa antara apekṣam prāmāṇyam yena tad virodhe svarasam jahyāt  tad apekṣa tve hi tad anuguṇa tayā varteta nirapekṣasya kaḥ pramāṇa antara anusaraṇe hetuḥ laukikāḥ tu śabdāḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣam sva artham abhidadhati iti yuktā teṣām tad anusāriṇī vṛttiḥ tulye tu anapekṣa tve kim iti na viparyayaḥ ubhayoḥ vā vyāghātāt aprāmāṇyam ‘paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam aiti vā rajata jñānasya iva pūrvasya bādhaḥ na khalu rajata jñāna virodhāt śukti jñānam anya viṣayam aviṣayam vā katham tarhi vede guṇa vādaḥ yatra śrautaiḥ arthaiḥ pramāṇa artha niṣpatteḥ asambhavaḥ tatra dvitīyasyaapi vṛtteḥ śabdānām pravṛtti darśanāt tayā pramāṇa viṣaya lābhaḥ yatra tu śabdāḥ svarasena labhante viṣayam tatra na pramāṇa antara virodhāt apāvartante na hi eṣām pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ  arthaḥ  yena tad vaśāt apāvarteran atha matam ubhaya anugrahāt evam kalpyate evam hi śabdaḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ ca anugṛhītā bhavanti anyathā pratyakṣādayaḥ  atyantam apabādhitāḥ (ṃ=  ā @meva bādhitāḥ edition) syuḥ na etad sāram pramāṇa sāmarthya anusāreṇa prameye kācid kalpanā syāt  pramāṇe tu svarasa siddham parityajya kalpanāyām na nibandhanam asti tasmāt pramāṇa anusāreṇa vikalpa samuccaya vyavasthāḥ kalpyante na ubhaya anugrahāt na ubhayam anugṛhītavyam iti pramāṇam asti te eva pramāṇe iti ced  yadi matam na pramāṇasya pramāṇa antarāt anugrāhya tvam api tu svata eva pramāṇa tvāt eva hi tasya tena artha vyavasthāpanā yathā tarhi tatas  arthaḥ  avagamyate tathā vyavasthāpanīyaḥ evam tad anugṛhītam bhavati anyathā bādhitam syāt  apramāṇikā ca artha vyavasthā tatas  svarasena apratīteḥ anyasya ca abhāvāt  itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt ca prāmāṇyāt siddhāt artha antare pratītiḥ prāmāṇya ani athā anupapattyā kalpanīyā tad pratīteḥ ca prāmāṇyam svarasa labhye tu arthe pratītita eva prāmāṇyam iti na itaretara āśraya tā tasmāt virodhe bādha eva pūrvasya pramāṇa anusārī tathā pratīteḥ na uttarasya viṣaya antara kalpanā na khalu rajata jñāna anugrahāya śukti śakala jñānasya gocaraḥ  aparaḥ kalpyate na ca pratyakṣa ādīnām ananya gati tvāt anavakāśa tvam yā khalu rajata ādi vibhramāṇām gatiḥ sā teṣām api yadi teṣām upacaritaḥ kalpitaḥ  vā viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām api tathā atha asattvāt tasya āviṣayā avidyamāna arthāḥ pratyakṣādayaḥ  api evam tasmāt avivakṣita artha tvam upacarita artha tvam vā gatiḥ ubhayoḥ aviśiṣṭā etena idam api parākṛtam yad āhuḥ śabdasya pramāṇa antara virodhe dṛṣṭam upacarita artha tvam avivakṣita artha tvam vā loke tasmāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhe vedāntānām tathā abhāva iti pratyakṣa ādiṣu api tathā darśanāt iti yad tu mukhya tvāt pratiṣṭhita arthaiḥ apahata viṣaya āmnāya iti ata eva bādhakaḥ śukti jñānavat na ca tad anusāreṇa artha kalpanām arhati anapekṣa tvāt  na tad adhīnam asya pramāṇa tvam na taiḥ saṃbhūyakāri tvam nāmnā ayasya pratyakṣa ādīnām ca eka vākya bhāvaḥ paraspara anapekṣaḥ  hi ubhayatra buddhi utpādaḥ tatra para balīyaḥ tvam nyāyyam yathā uktam ‘pūrvāt para balīyaḥ tvam tatra nāma pratīyatām anyonya nirapekṣāṇām yatra janma dhiyām bhavetyatra tu eka vākya tayā saṃbhūyakāri tvam tatra anupajāta virodhitayā sva rasa vṛttyā mukhye sthite prathamayā vṛttyā tad eka vākya tvam pratipattum aśaknuvanti tad apekṣita artha samarpaṇa anupapatteḥ para padāni dvitīyayā vṛttyā pūrva apekṣitam artham samarpayanti eka vākyatā sāmarthyāt iti mukhya balīyaḥ tvam yad tu vyākula tvāt iti tatra ucyate syāt vyākula tvam yadi karma vidhayaḥ  bheda pratipādana parāḥ syuḥ te tu siddham bhedam upāśritya ‘idam anena ittham sādhayetiti puruṣa hita anuśāsana pradhānāḥ syāt etad  asati bhede aṃśa traya pratyastamayāt kutaḥ hita anuśāsanam ucyate yathā khalu śyena ādiṣu ‘na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāniiti pratiṣedhāt sādhya aṃśa pratyasta maye api anuśāsanam evam sarvatra sarva aṃśa pratyasta maye api tathā hi niṣiddha anartha udayā katham hiṃsā sādhyā syāt  atha bhavati kasya cit tīvra krodha ākrānta svānta tayā samuddhata dhvānta tiraskṛta viveka vijñānasya anartham api artha tvena paśyataḥ śāstra upadeśam atikrāmataḥ tathā jyotiṣṭoma ādiṣu nisarga jā avidyā upadarśitā
