apratibuddhānām trayaḥ  api aṃśāḥ tān upāśritya teṣām anuśāsanam pratibuddhāḥ tu karma vidhibhiḥ na anuśiṣyante yathā śyena ādi vidhibhiḥ apajita krodha arātayaḥ tad evam vyavahāra siddha bheda āśrayeṣu karma vidhiṣu yadi api bheda pratītiḥ asti tathā api teṣām atatparatvān na tatra prāmāṇyam vṛttānteṣu iva arthavāda padānām tathā ca kutas taiḥ vedāntānām parāhatiḥ vedāntaiḥ vā teṣām api ca pratyakṣa ādiṣu eva parāhatiḥ upalabhyate bādhya bādhaka bhāva darśanāt rajata śukti śakala ādi jñāneṣu bheda abheda pratīteḥ ca sarvatra tad evam balavat tve api āmnāyasya yaḥ  nāma manda dhīḥ laukika vacasām pratyakṣa ādi virodha upacarita artha tva darśanāt lokavat vede api śabda vṛttam iti manyate yaḥ  vā nirūḍha nibiḍa tayā bheda darśana andhakārasya pratyakṣa ādīnām eva balavat tvam manyate loka vacasām ca taiḥ bādha darśanāt  tad pratibodhanāya virodhaḥ  nirasyate na hi yaḥ  nāma manda viṣeṇa vṛścikena daṣṭaḥ  mriyate na asau na cikitsyata iti tatra pratyakṣe trayaḥ kalpāḥ vastu svarūpa vidhiḥ vastu antarasya vyavacchedaḥ ubhayam vetti ubhayasmin= api traividhyam yaugapadyam vyavaccheda pūrva kaḥ  vidhiḥ vidhi pūrva kaḥ  vyavaccheda iti tatra vastu antara vyavacchede ubhayasmin vā bhedaḥ pratyakṣa gocara iti bhavati virodhaḥ sva rūpa vidhi mātre tu kasyacid vyavacchedena śūnye na bhedaḥ pramāṇa arthaḥ na hi vyavacchedāt ṛte bheda siddhiḥ vidhi mātra vyāpāram ca pratyakṣam atas  na virodhaḥ katham iti ucyate labdha rūpe kvacid kiñcittādṛś  eva niṣidhyate vidhānam antareṇa atas  na viṣedhasya saṃbhavaḥ na tāvat vyavaccheda mātram pratyakṣa vyāpāraḥ na yugapad ubhayam na vyavaccheda pūrvakam vidhānam yatas  siddhe viṣaye siddha rūpam eva niṣidhyate ‘nedam iha‘nāya mayam aiti siddhe bhū tale siddhaḥ  ghaṭaḥ gavi vā aśvaḥ na pratiṣedhyāt pratiṣedha viṣayāt ca vinā pratiṣedhaḥ  avakalpate katham tarhi atyanta āsatām pradhāna kha puṣpa ādīnām pratiṣedhaḥ na hi tatra kvacid deśe kāle vā niṣedhaḥ ātyantika tvāt  na api kutaścid siddhi atyanta asattvāt tatra kecid āhuḥ kha puṣpa ādiṣu tāvat siddheṣu kha ādiṣu tadvidhāḥ puṣpādayaḥ  niṣidhyante ‘pradhānam na asti aiti jagat kāraṇe sukha duḥkha moha ātma tā vibhakta kārya tva ādīni nivāryante anye tu kutaścid nimittāt  buddhau labdha rūpāṇām bahis niṣedhaḥ kriyata iti varṇayanti anyathā daiva niṣiddhe kaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  aprāpta rūpe prāpta rūpe vā katham atyantāya pratiṣedhaḥ api ca anapekṣita viṣaya niṣedhye vyavacchede śūnyatā pramāṇa arthaḥ syāt  na bhedaḥ sarvasya sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa niṣedhāt  yaḥ tu bhedāya vyavacchedaḥ sa bhedyayoḥ siddhim apekṣate na ca sā vidhāna ādṛta iti prāk vidhānam eṣitavyam vidhi pūrvaka eva ca niṣedhaḥ  aṅgīkriyata iti na api vidhi pūvakaḥ  vyavacchedaḥ yatas  kramaḥ saṃgacchate yuktyā na eka vijñāna karmaṇoḥ na saṃnihita jam tad ca tad anyāmarśi jāyate na khalu eka pramāṇa jñāna vyāpārau santau vidhi vyavacchedau kramavantau yujyete kṣaṇika tvāt  kramavatoḥ hi vyāpārayoḥ paścāt tanaḥ na tad vyāpāraḥ syāt  vyavadhānāt  api ca janma eva buddheḥ vyāpāraḥ  artha avagraha rūpāyāḥ sā ced arha vidhāna rūpa udayā vidheḥ eva asyā vyāpāraḥ yaugapadyasya niṣedhāt  utpannāyāḥ ca punar anutpatteḥ api ca saṃnihita artha ālambanam pratyakṣam na asaṃnihitam artham avabhāsayitum arhati na ca anavabhāsamāna rūpam vyavacchettum paryāpnoti anavabhāsamāne hi tatra vyavacchedye vyavaccheda mātram syāt  na vyavacchedaḥ kasyacid  sarvasya vā syāt  tasmāt na anavabhāsamāne vyavacchedye vyavacchedaḥ na ca saṃnihita artha avalambane pratyakṣe asaṃnihita avabhāsaḥ  yuktaḥ katham idānīm bādhakam pratyakṣam tatra hi pūrva artha niṣedha puraḥsaraḥ  anya vidhiḥ eka jñāne abhyupeyate asaṃnihita niṣedhya avabhāsaḥ ca tasmāt na eṣa niyamaḥ yatas  pūrvaḥ niṣedhaḥ eka jñāna vyāpāre ca kramaḥ pratyakṣeṇa ca asaṃnihita artha avabhāsaḥ na etad sāram tatra api pūrva vijñāna vihite rajata ādau ‘idamiti ca saṃnihita artha sāmānye niṣedhaḥ  vidhi pūrva eva śuktikā vidhiḥ tu virodhi niṣedha pūrva ucyate vidhi pūrva tā ca niyamena niṣedhasya ucyate na vidheḥ niṣedha pūrvaka tā niṣidhyate na ca tatra eka jñānasya kramavat vyāpāra tā ubhaya rūpasya utpatteḥ pūrva jñāna prāpita tvāt ca viṣaya vyavacchedyayoḥ na asaṃbhavaḥ pūrva jñāna avabhāsite ca vyavacchedye vyavacchedasya vṛtteḥ na asaṃnihita artha avabhāsa prasaṅgaḥ pūrva apekṣasya tasya utpatteḥ pūrva apekṣayā eva ca tad  dvi rūpam udeti anyathā eka rūpam eva udīyāt api ca sarva vyavaccheda an apākurvataḥ kaḥ  vyavacchedaḥ  abhimataḥ yena pratyavasthīyeta siddhaḥ sa loka iti ced  ayam vā kim na loka siddhaḥ na aśvaḥ  gauḥ na gauḥ aśva iti yad tu matam eka vidhiḥ eva anya vyavacchedaḥ tathā hi darśanam yathā eva tad ākāratayā tad rūpam vidadhāti tathā tad eka ākāra pratiniyamāt ‘tat eva na anyatiti anyat vyavacchinatti tad sāmarthya prabhāvitau ca ‘idam na idam aiti vikalpau bhāva abhāva vyavahāram pravartayataḥ na hi eka ākāra pratiniyatāt ananya saṃsargiṇaḥ  jñānāt anyaḥ  anya vyavacchedaḥ tatra ucyate vidhānam eva na ekasya vyavacchedaḥ  anya gocaraḥ mā sma bhūt aviśeṣeṇa mā na bhūt eka dhī juṣām na eka pratiniyamaḥ  anya abhāva niścaya nimittam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti asya itarasya ca aviśeṣeṇa vyavaccheda prasaṅgāt  tad pratiniyamaḥ  hi tatas  anyasya asaṃsargaḥ tathā ca asaṃsargāt vyavacchede tasya dṛśya adṛśyayoḥ aviśeṣāt ubhayoḥ vyavacchedaḥ syāt  atha matam bhavati eva tathā hi yāvantaḥ  asya anātmāna stān aviśeṣeṇa tad ātma niyamāt darśanam apākaroti tathā ca na asya anya ātmānaḥ tad deśa kālāḥ tu bhaveyuḥ rūpa ādivat avirodhāt  tatra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ viśeṣaḥ tad deśa kāla vyavaccheda avadhāraṇāya saṃbhavati hi anupalabhyaḥ tad deśa kālaḥ  anātma anupalabhyamānaḥ  api anya upalabdhau itaravat  anyathā na tulya upalambha yogyatas  syāt  satyam asti ayam vibhāgaḥ na tu idānīm darśana pratiniyamasya sāmarthyam tathā hi pratiniyatam api tatra deśe kāle ca rūpe darśanam tayoḥ yathā rūpa vidhi mātra upakṣayāt na rasam vyavacchinatti tathā bhū bhāga darśana niyamaḥ  api bhū bhāga vidhi mātra vyāpāra tvāt na ghaṭa dṛśyam api vyavacchindyāt  vyavacchede vā sarvasya vyavacchedaḥ tasmāt  dṛśya vyavacchede api hetu antaram upāsyam na darśana pratiniyama mātram tathā ca ātmā antara vyavacchedaḥ  api na tatas  siddhim upāśnute kāmam vidheḥ vidheyā sattva vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt tad abhāvaḥ  vyavacchidyeta na ātma antara sat tā tad deśa kālayoḥ iva anupalabhya sattā na ekasya bahava ātmāna iti ced  anyatas tarhi virodhāt vyavacchedaḥ na darśana niyamāt  asati ca vyavacchede kutaḥ bahu tvam kutaḥ vā virodha itaretara āśrayam vā tasmāt na eka vidhiḥ anya vyavacchedaḥ api ca eka niyamāt anya vyavacchede citra ādiṣu nīla ādīnām eka darśana bhājām bhedaḥ  na sidhyet  eka jñāna saṃsargāt ekatra jñānasya aniyamāt  nanu prakṛtyā eva bhinnā bhāvāḥ tān= tadvidhān vidadhadeva darśanam parasparataḥ  vyāvartayati na hi vyāvṛttiḥ anyā vyāvṛttimataḥ tatra vyāvṛttimat vidhau sā api vidhīyata eva yad prakṛtiḥ khalu yaḥ padārthaḥ sa tayā eva prakṛtyā vidheyaḥ anyathā na tasya vidhiḥ syāt  vyāvṛtta svabhāvāḥ ca bhāvā yathāyatham darśaneṣu nirbhāsante tasmāt tathā eva vidhīyanta iti atra api asaṃspṛṣṭa nirbhāsanāt asaṃspṛṣṭa svabhāva tve dṛśyayoḥ aviśeṣeṇa vyavacchedaḥ tad avasthaḥ api ca na bhedaḥ  vastunaḥ  rūpam tad abhāva prasaṅgataḥ arūpeṇa ca bhinna tvam vastunaḥ  na avakalpate na vyāvṛttiḥ vastu svabhāvaḥ sā khalu eka aneka adhiṣṭhānā pratijñāyate prajñāyate ca tathā ca tasyāḥ  ekasyaaneka vṛtteḥ vastu svabhāva tve vastūnām api bhedaḥ  na syāt  na ekasmāt abhinna svabhāvam bhinnam yujyate tadvat eva atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣa iti artha antaram eva vyāvṛttiḥ āsthīyate tathā api vyāvṛtteḥrūpa tvāt svarūpeṇa na bhāvā vyāvṛttāḥ syuḥ aparaḥ kalpaḥ bhedaḥ parasparān ātma svabhāvaḥ sa ced vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ vastūnām abhāva prasaṅgaḥ abhāva ātmaka tva pratijñānāt  aparaḥ prakāraḥ bhedaḥ ced vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ na ekam kiñcana vastu syāt  bhedena ekatvasya virodhāt  paramāṇuḥ api bhedāt aneka ātmaka iti na ekaḥ tathā ca tad samuccaya rūpaḥ  anekaḥ  api asiātmā na avakalpate tatra ekatva aneka tvayoḥ anupapatteḥ tṛtīya prakāra asaṃbhavāt ca vastunaḥ  niḥsvabhāva tva prasaṅgaḥ anyā vyākhyā dvitīya ardhasya vyatireka avyatireka vikalpe pratyavatiṣṭhate vastu gata eṣa vibhāgaḥ tad svabhāva tvam anya tvam ca iti na avastuni vikalpa viracita śarīre bhede avatāram arhati tathā hi tattva anya tva abhyām anirvacanīyaḥ anādi vikalpa vāsanā upādāna vikalpa paridarśita śarīraḥ ‘ayam asmāt bhinnaḥ ayamanayoḥ bhedaḥiti vyavahāram pravartayati na bhedaḥ  nāma kiñcid vastu yasya tattvam anya tvam vā kiñcid vicāryeta tatra idam punar upatiṣṭhate arūpeṇa ca bhinna tvam vastunaḥ  na avakalpate yadi tarhi arūpaḥ  niḥsvabhāvaḥ  bhedaḥ na hi vastu sthityā asti vikalpaiḥ eva kevalam upadarśyate na tarhi vastunaḥ  bhinna tvam paramārtha taḥ  bheda abhāvāt na hi kalpitena svabhāvena pāramārthikī tadvat tā yujyate kalpitā eva syāt  tad etad asmābhiḥ ucyamānam kim iti bhavān na anumanyate vayam api etad eva brūmaḥ na bhedaḥ  bhāvataḥ asti anādya vidyā vilasitam etad iti yad uktam bheda ātma tve vastuna eka vastu abhāvaḥ tad bhāvāditarasya api iti vastu abhāvaḥ tatra āhuḥ para apekṣam vastunaḥ  bheda svabhāvam brūmaḥ na ātma apekṣam yena virodhāt eka vastu abhāvaḥ syāt  sva rūpeṇa tu ekam vastu para apekṣayā bhinnam iti tatra ucyate pauruṣeyīm apekṣām ca na hi vastu anuvartate na apekṣā nāma kaścid vastu dharmaḥ yena vastūni vyavasthāpyeran na khalu sva hetu prāpita udayeṣu svabhāva vyavasthiteṣu vastuṣu svabhāva sthitaye vastu antara apekṣā yujyate tatra puruṣa pratyaya dharmaḥ  ayam na ca puruṣa pratyaya anuvidhāyīni vastūni sva hetubhyaḥ sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ atas  na tad anusāreṇa vastu rūpam vyavatiṣṭhate vyavasthita vastu svarūpa anusāreṇa eva tasya vyavasthā nyāyyā tad pūrvaka tvāt paraspara apekṣāyām ca vastu svabhāva sthitau= itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt  athavā yad uktam ekasmāt bhedāt avyatiredāt vastunaḥ  bheda abhāva prasaṅga iti tatra āhuḥ na bheda ekaḥ rūpa virodhāt  ekatve ca tad nimittam vastūnām eka tvam syāt  tasmāt pratibhāvam bhedaḥ  bhidyate katham tarhi aneka āśraya tvam apekṣātaḥ tathā hi pratiyogi apekṣam tasya svarūpam vyavasthitam tathā ca yathāyatham bhedaiḥ pratiyogi apekṣaiḥ ātma bhūtaiḥ bhinnāḥ sarve bhāvā iti tatra ucyate pauruṣeyīm iti puruṣaḥ  hi ekam artham gṛhītvā param apekṣate kārya artham sva hetubhyaḥ tu pratilabdha avikala svabhāvānām bhāvānām bhāva antareṣu kimartha apekṣā nanu svabhāva sthitaye nānāvidhā hi bhāva svabhāvāḥ tatra kaścid pratiyogi apekṣayā eva vyavatiṣṭhate vastu tattve yathā ayam eva bhedaḥ na tarhi hetubhyaḥ  bhāvasya avikala ātma lābhaḥ bheda ākhyasya rūpasya pratiyogi apekṣa tvāt  hetu antarāt ca pratiyoginaḥ saṃpadyamānaḥ paścāt bhedaḥ  na svabhāvaḥ syāt  syāt etad  avikala rūpa eva bhāvaḥ hetubhyaḥ  jāyate tatra bheda ākhyam rūpam pratiyogi apekṣam na anapekṣam kadācid ittasya tadvidha tvāt tena tadvidhena eva saha jāyata iti na vikala rūpa prādurbhāvaḥ tatra ucyate bhavatu tadvidhasya prādurbhāvaḥ apekṣā arthaḥ tu vaktavyaḥ yasya hi yatra kiñcid  āyatate tad  tad apekṣata iti ucyate na anyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sa apekṣa nirapekṣayoḥ vyapasthāpakaḥ  nirūpyate tatra na tāvat utpattiḥ pratiyoginī āyatate sva hetubhyaḥ  avikalasya utpatteḥ na artha kriyā tad asaṃnidhāne api tasya artha kriyā darśanāt  pratītiḥ ced  tathā hi na anapekṣya pratiyoginam bhedaḥ pratīyata iti na tarhi bheda svabhāvaḥ sa apekṣaḥ tasmin= avasthite vastu sthiti uttara kālā pratītiḥ artha antaram eva pratiyoginam apekṣate yathā vyavasthita anapekṣa svabhāvā rūpa ādayaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi apekṣāyām pratītau na sa apekṣa svabhāvāḥ kathyate itaretara āśrayāt ca na pratītiḥ api paraspara āyattau= akalpate na ca vastu mātrāt anavagṛhīta bhedāt bheda siddhiḥ ekasmin= api tad prasaṅgāt  tasmāt pauruṣeyīm apekṣāyām na vastu anuvarttate atas  na vastu svabhāva iti arthaḥ anyā vyākhyā na bhedaḥ  vastunaḥ  rūpam āpekṣikaḥ hi pratīyate na ca apekṣāyām puruṣa pratyayam vastu anuvartate vyavasthita vastu pūrvaka tvāt iti katham tarthi pitṛ ādayaḥ na hi te apekṣayā vinā na ca kha puṣpa gandharvanagara ādi tulyāḥ avisaṃvādi vyavahāra aṅga tayā loka siddha tvāt  ucyate bhedaḥ  api evam kim na loka siddhaḥ api ca pitṛ ādi viṣaye apekṣā janana ādi prabhāvitā eka kriyā viśeṣeṇa vyapekṣā hrasva dīrghayoḥ vyavasthite eva janya janaka śaktī pitṛ putra śabdayoḥ abhidheye te tu samāna janana vyāpāra viṣaye tau= āskandataḥ svabhāva bhedāt  atas  yena samāna tvam tatra apekṣā etad uktam bhavati śabda arthaḥ tatra sa apekṣaḥ na vastu apekṣā hetuḥ ca tatra sādhāraṇī kriyā vidyate vyavasthitayoḥ api vastunoḥ bhāva bhede tvayam vastu tattva gataḥ  vicāraḥ na ca apekṣā hetuḥ kaścid upalabhyate hrasva dīrghayoḥ api eka jātīyāyām kriyāyām deśa vyāptau nyūna adhika bhāvāt evam draṣṭavyam yadi tarhi kārya bhedāt api apekṣā hanta! artha kriyā bhedāt eva bhāvānām paraspara apekṣaḥ  bhedaḥ setsyati kim ca asatyām api darśanāt bheda siddhau vidhi mātra vyāpāra tvāt kārya bhedāt eva kāraṇa bhedam anumimīmahe na ekatve kārya bhedaḥ kalpate kāraṇa svabhāva apekṣa tvāt kārya bhedasya tad jananaḥ ced asya (tad jananam ced asya edition) svabhāvaḥ na anya jananaḥ tasmāt kārya antarasya anyatas  janma iti tad idam bhedena eva bheda prasādhanam na ati caturaśram api ca artha kriyā kṛte bhede rūpa bhedaḥ  na labhyate dāha pāka vibhāgena kṛśānuḥ na hi bhedavān na artha kriyā bhedāt bhāvānām paraspara apekṣaḥ  rūpa bhedaḥ pratīyate na api anumātum śakyate vyapadeśa bheda mātram tu syāt  ekasmin= api vahnau dāha pāka ādi kārya bheda dṛṣṭeḥ atha matam rūpa ādi samūhaḥ  vahniḥ tatra rūpāt prakāśaḥ sparśāt dāha iti kāmam dāha pākau tu sparśāt eva tau ca loke pratīti bhedau sati api saṃyogi dravya vikriyā sāmānye karma ca ekam saṃyoga vibhāga saṃskārāṇām hetuḥ ātmā ca icchā ādīnām sattva ādayaḥ ca pratyekam abhedāt lāghava prakāśa ādīnām rūpādayaḥ  jñāna viśeṣāṇām sajātī yakṣaṇānām ca iti utprekṣitavyam nanu na artha kriyā bheda mātrāt bhedam brūmaḥ api tu tatra asaṃbhāvinyā adṛṣṭāyāḥ yathā cakṣuṣi sati api adṛṣṭāyāḥ ca badhire tatra asaṃbhāvinyāḥ śabda buddheḥ indriya bhedaḥ paraspara asaṃbhavi kāryāḥ ca prāyeṇa bhāvāḥ anya kāryasya anyatra adarśanāt  atha kārya asaṃbhavaḥ katham pratyetavyaḥ nanu uktam tatra adarśanāt  na tarhi asaṃbhavaḥ yasya khalva dvayam jagat tasya kārya jātam ekatra eva dṛśyata iti katham adarśanam tatra siddhe bhede tatra adarśanam tatra adarśanāt ca bheda siddhiḥ iti ita retara āśrayāt na bheda anumānam atha matam adṛṣṭasya darśanāt iti tad asat  ekasmāt api kramavatām kāryāṇām darśanāt  syāt etad  ekāntataḥ  abhede kārya darśana adarśane na yukte viśeṣa abhāvāt na tarhi kārya bhedaḥ  abhedam apabādhate tad anupamardena viśeṣa mātra anumānam syāt  tad ca kalpanā viṣayam na eva avajānīmahe vastu sataḥ tasya ayogāt tattva anya tvayoḥ asaṃbhavāt yaḥ tu kṣaṇika vādī tattvam eva viśeṣasya na manyate tasya asati kāraṇa svabhāva abhede katham tulya svabhāva kārya utpādaḥ atha niranvaya vināśānām api kalpanā viṣayāt abhedāt kāryasya tulya tā hanta! tarhi bhedāt eva kalpanā viṣayāt kārya bheda siddheḥ mudhā kāraṇa bheda kalpanā atha kārya abhede na (atha na kārya abhedena edition) kāraṇa svabhāva abhedaḥ  apekṣyeta bhinna svabhāvebhyaḥ sahakāribhya eka kārya utpatteḥ yathā cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ  rūpa vijñānasya (rūpa ādi jñānasya ṃs ā ṃs ch rūpa ādi jñānasya edition) yathā tarhi kārya svabhāva abhedāya na kāraṇa svabhāva abhedaḥ  apekṣyate tathā tad bhedāya kāraṇa bhedaḥ  api na apekṣitavyaḥ api ca aneka kāraṇa janye api ekasmin kārye kāraṇa vyāpāra viṣaya bhedaḥ tena eva varṇitaḥ yathā rūpa jñānasya cakṣuṣaḥ  rūpa grahaṇa niyamaḥ samanantara jñānāt upalambha ātma tā viṣayāt tad ākāra tā iti yadi ca kārya tulya tvam na hetu sāmya kṛtam na kāryāt hetu anumānam syāt  bhinna jātīyāt api tulya jātīya utpatti saṃbhavāt hetu abhedaḥ ced na kārya abheda upayujyate kaḥ tulya jātīyāt vijātīyasya janma nivārayet  tatra yathā vyāvahārikāt abhedāt kārya abhedaḥ tathā vyāvahārikāt bhedāt kārya bheda iti na viśeṣaḥ syāt etad  kalpitaḥ ced bhedaḥ kārya bhedāya prabhuḥ na tarhi kalpitaḥ na hi anyat parama artha sataḥ  lakṣaṇam artha kriyā sāmarthyāt  tulyam idam abhede api yaḥ  api manyate yugapad viruddha artha kriyā darśanāt bheda a= agatiḥ tathā hi janana maraṇa vṛddhi kṣaya sthāna gamana śoka harṣa ādi vividha viruddha dharma samupetam ekadā viśvam upalabhyate tad bhedavat iti gamyate tasya api idam eva uttaram āvṛttyā dāha pāka vibhāgena iti katham idam tāvat ayam praṣṭavyaḥ kaḥ  viruddha arthaḥ yadi ekatra asaṃbhavaḥ saḥ  asiddhaḥ atha paraspara vyavacchinna ātma tā janana ādayaḥ ca paraspara rūpa nivṛtti ātmāna iti na tarhi ataḥ bheda siddhiḥ ekasmin= api vahnau dagdhṛ tva paktṛ tva darśanāt  na hi paraspara vyavacchedam antareṇa nānā tvam dharmāṇām tatas ced bhedaḥ na aneka dharmakam ekam kiñcid syāt  atha paraspara abhāva ātma tā eva virodhaḥ na ekasmin sa eva bhavati na ca bhavati iti tatas  bheda avasāyaḥ tad asat  na hi evam dharmau= eva kutas tayoḥ virodhāt bheda avagatiḥ kha puṣpa ādiṣu ca ubhaya abhāvāt ubhaya prasaṅgaḥ atha vadhya ghātaka bhāvaḥ  (vadhya ghātuka@ edition) virodhaḥ harṣaḥ śokam hanti śokaḥ ca tam evam itareṣu api tatra api na ajāta ekaḥ  anyam nāśayati na anya adhikaraṇam tasmāt eka adhikaraṇaḥ  bhūtvā nāśayati iti vācyam evam ca tayoḥ eka adhikaraṇa tva darśanāt na tad darśanena adhikaraṇa bheda anumānam avyabhicāram atha bhāva rūpa tad vyavaccheda ātmānaḥ  dharmā virodhinaḥ nitya tva anitya tva mūrta tva amūrta tva ādayaḥ tad saṃbandhāt bheda gatiḥ tad api na yatas  na avaśyam yaḥ  yatra bhavati sa tam vyāpnoti na hi ratha ādayaḥ tad saṃyogāt ayaḥ  vā nabhaḥ  vyaśnuvate anyān vā saṃyoginaḥ pṛthivī ādīn avacchinna tvāt  evam avacchinnā dharmā anavacchinnam anantam artham āśrayantaḥ  api na vyaśnuvate atas  na ekasmin= api bhāva abhāva virodhaḥ yaḥ tu manyeta artha kriyā bhedaḥ  artha kriyā vyavasthā tatas  bheda adhigamaḥ ekatve hi na vyavasthā yujyate tathā ca payasaḥ  api tailam tilebhyaḥ ca dadhi syāt  tathā ekasmin jāyamāne sarvam jāyeta naśyati ca naśyet  anyathā bheda eva śabda antareṇa uktaḥ syāt  tad uktam saha utpatti vināśau sarvam ca sarvatra upayujyeta iti tasya āpi idam eva uttaram dāha pāka vibhāgena iti yadi kārya nānā tvam vyavasthā na tayā tilānām payasaḥ ca bhedam pratipadyate atha payasaḥ  dadhnaḥ janma na anyata iti vyavasthā na anya tvam siddhayā vyavasthayā pramitsitam tad lakṣaṇam anupraveṣṭum arhati tasyāḥ  asiddhi prasaṅgāt  tasmāt dadhi janana śaktiḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca vyavasthā tatas  bhedaḥ na hi eka viṣaya ekasya śakti aśaktī yujyete iti sa ca ayam virodhi dharma yogaḥ  bheda hetuḥ anantaram eva nirāsi yathā khalu dīrgha kālāḥ padārthā mita kālaiḥ dharmaiḥ saṃbadhyamānāḥ tad dharmāṇaḥ  atad dharmāṇaḥ ca na virodha pada bhājaḥ tathā parimita deśaiḥ vipula deśā anantāḥ ca katham anantasya antavān dharma iti ced  vyatireke anivarcanīya tve vā na asti asaṃbhāvanā avakāśaḥ avyatireke api dīrgha kālasya iva mita kālaḥ yaḥ  api dīrgha kālam artham na pratipadyate tam pratīdam punar  paṭhitavyam dāha pāka vibhāgena iti ekaḥ  api vahniḥ kiñcid eva dahati pacati ca tathā ca dāhakaḥ ca ādāhakaḥ ca na bhidyate tathā na dāha antarāṇi pāka antarāṇi vā karoti tasmin= eva dāhye pākye ca tathā bīja ādayaḥ pratyekam samarthā api na aṅkura antarāṇi janayanti na api sāmagrī tathā ca janakatvam ajanaka tvam iti atha ekasmin= eva janaka śaktiḥ anyam pradhvastam āgāminam vā ekam kim na janayati atha tatra eva eṣām sāmarthyam na anyatra tulya jātīye api kutas  tasya eva utpatteḥ kārya gamya tvāt ca sāmarthyasya tathā ca na śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ ca iti virodhaḥ abhede api tarhi payasaḥ tilānām dadhnaḥ anutpattau na virodhaḥ tathā hi yasya tāvat dadhnaḥ payasaḥ  janma na tasya tilebhyaḥ  anutpattiḥ yena śakti aśakti virodhāt  bhedaḥ syāt  kutas  tilānām payasaḥ  abhedāt  atha dadhi antarasya anutpatteḥ virodhaḥ tad ca na anyatra aśakteḥ tatra eva śakteḥ bīja ādīnām iva na hi samartham iti eva kāraṇam sarvam tulya jātīyam janayati ekasmāt eva sarva tulya jātīya kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt  atha matam artha kriyāsu bhedena viniyogāt bheda madhyavasyāmaḥ dadhne hi payaḥ  viniyujyate na sikatā iti tad api anaikāntikam ekatve api bhedena viniyoga darśanāt  tad eva artha vastu sahakāri sametam viniyujyate na kevalam atha matam bhinnam eva tad  sahakāri sannidhāna upādhi bhedāt aupādhikaḥ tarhi pratyaya mātra niveśī bhedaḥ na paramārthataḥ tathābhūtaḥ ca bhāva bhedaḥ  hi anujñāyata eva yaḥ  api kṣaṇika tvena bhedam āha tasya api bhedasya tulya tvāt sarvam sarvatra viniyujyate na vā kiñcid kvacid  adṛṣṭa sāmarthya tvāt  atha kalpanā viṣayāt abhedāt tad siddhiḥ parasya api tādṛśāt bhedāt iti na viśeṣa iti uktam yaḥ  api ekasya ubhayam pratijānīte bhedam abhedam ca tena ekatra api viruddha dharma āveśam abhyupayatā durlabha eva dadhnaḥ janakatvā janaka tvābhyām tila payasoḥ vibhāga iti tad evam ekasya eva eṣa mahimā bheda saṃpādana asahaḥ vahneḥ iva yadā bhāva bheda kalpaḥ tadā mudhā ekatra kriyā bheda upalabdheḥ asaṃbhavasya ca asiddheḥ adṛṣṭa darśanasya ca abheda bādhane sāmarthya abhāvāt viśeṣa mātra hetu tvāt tasya ca tattva anya tvābhyām anirvācyasya kalpanā āspada tvāt abhedāt iva ca tādṛśāt  kārya abhedasya bhedāt api tadvidhāt bhedasya upapatteḥ virodhasya ca anaikāntika tvāt asiddha tvāt vā vyavasthāyāḥ ca viniyoga bhedasya ca anaikāntika tvāt  abhedāt iva ca kalpitāt bhedāt tad siddheḥ bheda abhedayoḥ ca ekatra samavāye śakti aśaktyoḥ viniyoga aviniyogayoḥ ca eka samavāya saṃbhavāt ekasya eva eṣa kaḥ  api acintyaḥ sāmarthya atiśayaḥ  nikhila bheda prapañca saṃpādanāyai prabhuḥ pāvakasya iva pāka ploṣa ādi pravibhāga nimittam yadā upapadyate tadā bheda kalpanamakāraṇam ekasmāt api tad siddheḥ iti pūrva upasaṃhāraḥ tad etad ṛcā abhyanūktam ‘etāvānasya mahimāiti etad parimāṇam asya sāmarthyam yad ekaḥ  api ‘sahasra śīrṣāiti ‘yat bhūtam yad ca bhavyamiti pūrvarc dvaya nirdiṣṭa vividha viruddha abhimata dharma kārya vyavahāra āśrayaḥ katham iti ‘ataḥ apratyakṣa abhimatāt  ‘puruṣa eva idam sarvam aiti vā adṛṣṭa nirdiṣṭāt  ‘uta amṛta tvasya aiti vā deva manuṣya loka bhedena prapañcāt ekā ekasmāt samastāt ca vṛddhataraḥ puruṣaḥ tena asmin parimitānām viruddha abhimatānām api anante na samāveśaḥ  na yujyate tad eva jyāyaḥ tvam darśayati ‘pādaḥ  asya viśvāiti kṛtsnaḥ  api tāvat bhūta prapañcaḥ  asya kanīyān bhāga iti kim punar  pratyekam tathā hi ‘tri pāt aiva aparimitam anantam maraṇa ādi bhūta prapañca dharma śūnyam rūpam ‘di vi apradyota avasthāyām vartate pramoda avasthāyām vā sūrya maṇḍale dyusthāne vā tatra hi tad upāsyam tad hi tasya upalabdhi sthānam iti tatra iti ucyate aparaḥ kalpaḥ kalpite api kārya bheda ādi avasthāyā vā kāraṇa bhede kim iti na kārya antaram kim iti vā na saṃkaraḥ viparītā vā vyavasthā bhede api payasaḥ tilebhya eva tailam na sikatābhyaḥ bhinā api ca eka kāryāḥ cakṣuḥ āloka ādayaḥ śara śṛṅga ādayaḥ ca bhede api ca tilebhyaḥ tailam payasaḥ  dadhi na tu payasaḥ tailam tilebhyaḥ  dadhi yadi matam acintyebhyaḥ  bhāva sāmarthyebhyaḥ acintya anupapattitaḥ  bhāva sāmarthyāni ‘kasmāt  kathamiti kārya darśana unneya vyavasthāni tebhyaḥ kāryasya bhedaḥ vyavasthā na viparyayaḥ ca iti yadi evam ekasya eva saḥ  astu sāmarthya atiśayaḥ yad anekam vyavasthitam aviparītam ca kāryam tanmātreṇa tad siddheḥ aprāmāṇikā bhāvānām bhāva kalpanā iti syāt etad  vahneḥ api śakti bheda nibandhanaḥ kārya bhedaḥ tad na ekasmāt anekam kāryam tatra yadi vahniḥ api kāraṇam katham na ekasmāt anekam kāryam atha śaktīnām eva kāraṇa tvam abhipraiti tatra ucyate yathā eva bhinna śaktīnām abhinnam rūpam āśrayaḥ tathā nānā kriyā hetu rūpam kim na abhyupeyate ekasya aneka kārya yoga virodhāt śakti bhedaḥ kalpyate yadi ca ekasya aneka saṃbandha virodhaḥ katham nānā bhūtābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ ekaḥ saṃbadhyate tatra yathā ekasya artha svabhāvasya nānā śakti yogaḥ tathā nānā kārya yogaḥ  api kim na anujñāyate atha nānā kārya yoge virodhaḥ na nānā śakti yoge viśeṣa hetuḥ vācyaḥ api ca śaktīnām avyatirekāt ekam aneka ātmakam iṣṭam tatra ekatvam sva āśraya samavāyinā aneka tvena ca virudhyate kārya gatena tu āśraya antara samavāyinā virudhyata iti su bhāṣitam! atha artha antara tvam eva śaktīnām āśraya arthaḥ  vācyaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ ced  na bhinna tve rūpa avibhāga lakṣaṇaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ bheda eva na syāt  na nairantaryam tad śakti dravya saṃyuktasya dravya antarasya api tad śakti tva prasaṅgāt  na hi dravyasya anantaram tad śakteḥ vyavahitam bhavati na hi cakṣuḥ dravyasya anantaram rūpasya na anantaram vibhu tvāt ca ākāśa ādīnām sarva artha śakti vyavadhāna abhāvāt sarva śakti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt upakāra viśeṣāt kutaścit āśrayaḥ tatra yathā bhinnāsu śaktiṣu tad bhedāt upakārān bhinnānekaḥ  artha svabhāvaḥ karoti tathā kāryāṇi api iti kasmāt na iṣyate evam tāvat na anumāne api bheda adhigamaḥ na artha apattyā ca ye tu manyante satyam etad  na pratyakṣam bheda adhigamāya alam itaretara abhāva aṃśaḥ  hi bhāvānām bhedaḥ na saḥ  akṣa gocaraḥ ‘bhāva aṃśena eva saṃyogaḥ  yogya tvāt indriyasya hitathā ca na liṅga gamyaḥ  api adṛṣṭa saṃgati tvāt  arthāpattiḥ api kārya vyavasthā hetukā syāt  sā asiddhe bhede vyavasthāyāḥ  (ṃ=  ch kārya vyavasthāyāḥ  edition) eva anupapatteḥ tatra ayuktā tasmāt sat upalambha hetubhyaḥ pramāṇa antaram eva abhāvāya upāsanīyam vidhāyakāt vā pramāṇa antaram eva vyavacchedakam abhāva ākhyam tad nibandhanā hi bhāvānām asaṃkīrṇa tā (@ma saṃkīrṇa svabhāva tā edition) yad avocan ‘vastu asaṃkara siddhiḥ ca tad prāmāṇya samāśrayāiti tān pratyucyate anyonya saṃśrayāt bhedaḥ  na pramā antara sādhanaḥ na asmin= ayam na ayam ayam iti bhedāt vinā na dhīḥ na khalu yad vyavacchidyate yatas ca vyavacchidyate tayoḥ apratipattau vyavaccheda gatiḥ na anapekṣita viṣaya niṣedhyaḥ  niṣedhaḥ  asti san vā śūnyatām āpādayet  na bhedam iti uktam teṣām api vacaḥ ‘gṛhītvā vastu sadbhāvam smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam mānasam na astita ajñānam jāyate akṣa an apekṣayātayoḥ ca pratipattiḥ yadi na asaṃkīrṇa svabhāvayoḥ api tu vastu mātra tvena vyavacchedya vyavaccheda a= adhi vibhāga abhāvāt na niṣedha saṃbhavaḥ  artha mātre hi avibhāge viṣaya tvena apekṣite na niṣedhyam niṣedhya tvena apekṣite na viṣaya viśeṣaḥ tatra atyantāya niṣedhaḥ syāt  sa ca na siddha tvena asiddhatvena vā yujyata iti uktam kasyacid tāvat kutaścid (kasyacid kutaścid ṃs ch kasyacid kutaścid ca edition) bheda pratipattau sarvasya sarvatas  bheda gatiḥ syāt  aviśeṣāt  tasmāt anena asaṃkīrṇa svabhāvena bhinnau= eva pratipadya viṣaya niṣedhyau ‘nedam iha‘nāya mayamiti vyavacchedaḥ pratipattavyaḥ saṃbhavān niyamāt ca na ca anyathā pratiyogi tvam sāmānya upalabdhau ca sthāṇau puruṣasya abhāva(ṃ=  ā puruṣa abhāva@ edition) pratipatti abhāvāt tathā ca siddha viṣaya niṣedhya aṅgīkaraṇena vyavaccheda mātra vidhāyinya bhāva pratipattiḥ pratyātmam upalakṣyate tathā ca itaretara āśraya tvam asaṃkara pūrvam abhāva jñānam tatas ca asaṃkara siddhiḥ iti api ca na pramāṇa anutpāda mātrāt abhāva jñānam suṣupta ādau= anutpatteḥ tasmāt satsu pramāṇa kāraṇeṣu pramāṇa an utpādaḥ  abhāva jñāna hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ na ca tasya svarūpa bhedaḥ kaścid  yena sāmarthya atiśayāt cakṣuḥ ādivat bodhakaḥ kim tu na antarīyaka tvāt na antareṇa prameya abhāvam satsu pramāṇa hetuṣu pramāṇa an utpādaḥ asatsu tu sati api prameye tad abhāvāt syāt iti tathā ca liṅgavat jñāna apekṣaḥ pratipatteḥ janakaḥ sa ca yadi vastu antara jñānam na asiddhe vastu bhede sidhyati jñeya bheda anumeyaḥ  hi jñeya anumeyānām jñānānām bhedaḥ tathā ca vastu bheda siddhi pūrvikā eva abhāvāt bhedau= agatiḥ iti itaretara āśraya tvam atha ātmanaḥ  apariṇāmaḥ na sa stimita avasthā sarva apratipattau kasyacid abhāvasya anavagateḥ tasmāt sati api vastu antara jñāna rūpa pariṇāme tad jñāna rūpa pariṇāma abhāvaḥ  abhāva jñāna hetuḥ na ca eṣa viśeṣaḥ prāk vastu bheda siddheḥ sidhyati iti tad eva itaretara āśraya tvam ye tu āhuḥ darśanāt eva bhāvānām bhedaḥ sidhyati tathā hi nirvikalpasya pratyakṣasya sāmānya viṣaya tvam apākurvata uktam ‘tatyuktam pratidravyam bhinna rūpa upalambhanātiti yaḥ tu saṃyogāt samavāyāt vā saṃkaraḥ saḥ  abhāva ākhyena pramāṇena apanīyata iti te prāk eva pratyuktāḥ ye api vidhāyaka pratyakṣa puraḥsaram pratyakṣa antaram eva vastu grahaṇa pratiyogi smaraṇa iti kartavyatā anugṛhīta akṣa pratilabdha janma vyavacchedakam manyante yathā eva sa vikalpasya vastu grahaṇasya paścāt janma śabda smaraṇa vyavadhiḥ ca na ca anaindriyaka tvam itikartavya tā viśeṣa anugṛhītāt indriyāt tad utpatteḥ evam na asti iti api jñānasya iti bruvantaḥ tān pratīdam eva vaktavyam anyonya saṃśrayāt bhedaḥ  na pramā antara sādhanaḥ pratyakṣa antara sādhana iti arthaḥ ‘ayam asau na bhavatiiti jñānam pratyakṣam vā pramāṇa antaram vā sarvathā viṣaya niṣedhya vibhāgāt ṛte na niṣedha saṃbhava iti kim ca mīyamāna eka rūpeṣu na niṣedhaḥ  avakāśavān api ca sat mātra rūpe sarvatra pratīyamāne tad svabhāveṣu vastuṣu na itara abhimata itara abhimata pramāṇa anutpādaḥ sat svabhāva tvāt tayoḥ ‘sa t aiti ca sarvatra pramāṇa sadbhāvāt  pramāṇa abhāvāt ca itaretara abhāva jñānam iti nanu na arthānām kiñcid abhinnam rūpam pratyabhijñānāt hi tad avagamyate (tad avagamyeta ṃs ā tad gamyeta edition) na ca artha mātram dṛṣṭavataḥ  artha antare sa eva ayam iti pratyabhijñā asti yathā ekām gām dṛṣṭavataḥ  gavā antare sat śabda pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ tu pācaka ādivat yoga nibandhanā pramāṇa viṣayaḥ  hi ‘saniti ucyate na etad sāram na ced abhinna rūpa pratipattiḥ nirviṣaya tvam eva pramāṇasya āpadyeta yatas  na vyavacchedam antareṇa bheda pratītiḥ na vyavacchedaḥ kevalaḥ na vidhi sahitaḥ na vidheḥ paścāt pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ na vidhiḥ eva vyavaccheda iti varṇitam tatra yadi ekam api na gamyate nirviṣayatā eva syāt  apratyabhijñānam ca yadi gaḥ vailakṣaṇyāt ucyeta sati api sat mātra rūpa anugame gavā antare api tad na syāt  devadatta vailakṣaṇyāt  na hi yādṛśaḥ  devadattasya punar darśane ekatva pratyayaḥ tādṛśaḥ  gavā antare atha asti tatra tāvat pūrvā para anusandhānam na tu sataḥ sat antare kim ca bhoḥ anusandhānāt eka tvam na abhinna rūpa saṃvidaḥ na idānīm abhinna deśa kālaḥ  artha  ekaḥ syāt  deśa kāla bhede hi saḥ  ayam iti pūrva apara anusaṃdhānam gaḥ maṇḍale ca mahiṣa maṇḍala vilakṣaṇe deśa bhede api abhinna rūpa anugatāt prathamāt eva nirvikalpakāt pratyayāt eka artha pratipattiḥ iṣyate na ca tatra kāla bheda abhāvāt saḥ ayam iti avamarśaḥ yathā uktam nirvikalpaka bodhe api dvi ātmakasya api vastunaḥ grahaṇam lakṣaṇa ākhyeyam jñātrā śuddham tu gṛhyate na ca yathā maṇikam dṛṣṭavataḥ  maṇikā antare anusandhiḥ tathā śarāvam dṛṣṭvā tatra mṛd jātiḥ api apahnūyeta atha asti tatra api na tu yathā maṇikā antare sāmānya rūpāṇām bhūyastvāt utkaṭaḥ alpa sāmānya anugamāt sat antare api tathā eva syāt  vistareṇa ca etad upariṣṭāt abhidhāsyata iti alam ati prasaṅgena bheda abheda avabhāse dve vijñāne ced parīkṣyatām yadi matam vidyete tāvat anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta ābhe dve vijñāne na hi tayoḥ abhāve anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta vyavahāra saṃbhavaḥ na ca vijñāna rūpāt anyaḥ  artha vyavasthā hetuḥ tasya ahetu tve abhedaḥ  api na sidhyet  na etad sāram na hi vijñānam iti eva artham (@m iti eva artha tattvam edition) vyavasthāpayati tad api hi parīkṣyam yuktyā virudhyate na iti pramāṇa uttham na iti na khalu alāta cakra ādi vijñānebhyaḥ  artha tattva vyavasthā syāt etad  na pratyakṣam yuktyā apabādhyate satyam pratyakṣa tā eva bheda jñānasya na iti āveditam yathā kṣepīyassarva todij saṃyoga kāritasya alāta cakra jñānasya tad  sat api apramāṇa uttham pratyakṣa sarūpam svapna dṛśya alāta cakra ādi jñānavat na tattva avagama nimittam nanu uktena prakāreṇa pramāṇāt anyatas  api bheda jñānasya udayaḥ na saṃbhavati kaḥ  vānyathā āha na hi paramārtha taḥ  bheda avagamaḥ  asti yadi syāt  katham bhedaḥ  apahnūyeta apahnave vā katham tad avagamaḥ na avagamyam asti avagamyate ca iti durghaṭam kim tarhi idam avidyā vibhramaḥ yathā avabhāsam vedya sadbhāve ca na vibhramaḥ kim tu samyak jñānam asataḥ  ca avagamaḥ  anupapannaḥ tasmāt na paramārthataḥ sattvena nirucyate na api asattvena loke siddha tvāt sarva pravādeṣu iti uktam api ca jñāna dvaye asmin= catasraḥ kalpanāḥ saṃbhavanti jñāna bhedāt sāmānya vyakti vibhāgena vastu dvayam yathā āhuḥ saṃsarga vādinaḥ ekam vā sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam vastu yathā āhuḥ anekānta vādinaḥ viśeṣā eva vā vastūni teṣām ātyantika bheda niścaya asāmarthyāt tad upādānaḥ tad viṣaya eva abhedaḥ kalpanā jñāna gocaraḥ dṛṣṭā hi bhinneṣu abheda kalpanā ‘vanamiti yathā āhuḥ ātyantika bheda vādinaḥ abhedaḥ  vā parama arthaḥ tasya anavacchinnasya anantasya tathā niścetum aśakteḥ anādi tvāt ca avidyāyāḥ tad upādānāḥ tad viṣayā bheda parikalpanāḥ dṛṣṭā hi taraṅga bhedāt abhinne candramasi bheda kalpanā tad na aparīkṣya tattva niścayaḥ tatra parīkṣāyām na tāvat dvayam aikātmya prakhyānān avakalpanāt  samavāya kṛtam tad ced na bhedasya aparicyuteḥ na tāvat dve vastunī sāmānya viśeṣau prakhyā bhedāt  samāna adhikaraṇa tvena hi ime prakhye jāyete ‘san ghaṭaḥ gauḥ svastimatīiti na vyadhikaraṇa tvena yathā nīla pīta prakhye yathā vā ‘daṇḍaḥ  devadattaḥiti na api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena yathā ‘daṇḍī aiti saṃbandhasya apratibhāsanāt na ca vastu bheda viṣaya tve sāmānādhikaraṇyam avakalpate sati api saṃbandhe saṃbandhi dvayam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvena dvābhyām ekayā vā buddhyā gṛhyate na tu paraspara ātma tvena paraspara ātma tvena ca iha pratipattiḥ pratyātma vedanīyā vipratipatteḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ  bhede na anyathā vipratipadyeran sāmānya pratyakṣe ca viśeṣa pratyakṣa abhimānāt anyathā dhūma dṛṣṭau= iva agnau parokṣa abhimānaḥ syāt  syāt etad  na saṃbandha mātrāt bheda pratipattiḥ api tu saṃbandha viśeṣāt samavāyāt sa hi vastu saṃśleṣa ātmakaḥ tad na samavāye api tābhyām rūpa bhedasya anapāyāt anyathā bheda abhāvāt asaṃbandhāt tathā ca na aikātmyena prakhyā yujyate asti ca iyam atas tayā viruddhaḥ prakhyā bhedaḥ  na vastu bheda vyavasthāyai prabhavati svayam vā vyāhata tvāt  eka adhikaraṇa tvena utpatteḥ (eka adhikaraṇa tvena upapatteḥ edition) nanu bhede api paraspara ātma tvena pratipatteḥ nimittam samavāyaḥ tasya khalu eṣa sāmarthya atiśayaḥ yena bhedavatām arthānām bhedam tirodadhāti tathā ca te abhedena prakāśante atra ucyate bheda antardhāna sāmarthyam tasya bhede api ced matam hanta ekasya eva tad kim na yad evam avabhāsate samavāya sāmarthyāt ced bhedavatā urabhedavatā urabheda avabhāsaḥ hanta ekasya eva vastunaḥ sāmarthya viśeṣāt nānā avabhāsaḥ  abhyupeyatām vyarthā vastu bheda kalpanā na hi asti viśeṣaḥ yatas  bhinnayoḥ abheda prakāśa saṃbhavaḥ na ekasya nānā avabhāsa saṃbhava iti nanu jvalana ayaḥ guḍa ādiṣu dṛṣṭam evaṃvidham saṃsargasya sāmarthyam tatra darśanāt saṃbhavī saṃsargāt bhedavat sva bheda avabhāsaḥ na ekasmin nāna avabhāsaḥ adarśanāt  ucyate dṛṣṭaḥ saṃsarga dharmaḥ  ayam yadi ekam api vai tathā nānā avabhāsate citram rūpam ekam tathā matiḥ dṛṣṭam khalu ekam api vividha avabhāsam yathā citram rūpam tad hi khalu na nīla ādi samāhāra mātram teṣām avayava samavāye rūpa antara anabhyupagame ca avayavinaḥ  nīrūpa tva prasaṅgāt  na ca nīrūpa tvam eva āvayavinaḥ rūpa saṃskāra abhāve hi na sa cākṣuṣaḥ syāt  na ca rūpi samavāyāt saṃkhyā karma ādivat cākṣuṣa tvam evam hi uktam ‘mahati aneka dravya samavāyāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥiti sarvaḥ ca ittham avayavī nīrūpaḥ syāt  atha na arūpaḥ pratīyata iti na ayam prasaṅgaḥ citraḥ  api tathā iti na arūpaḥ tad ca asya rūpam nīla pīta ādi nirbhāsaḥ tathā nagara trailokya ādi buddhayaḥ vividha viṣaya ākārā nirbhāsante bheda abhāve api iti viṣaya ākāra jñāna vādinaḥ  manyante na ca eka buddhi tattva avyatirekāt viṣaya ākārāḥ parasparataḥ  api vyāvartante prāk eva buddheḥ syāt etad  citram api rūpam saṃsargāt eva eka artha samaveta samavāya lakṣaṇāt tathā avabhāsate tad asat  yatas  na ca saṃbandhi saṃbandhaḥ saṃsargaḥ  vyavadhānataḥ saṃśleṣaḥ  hi saṃsargaḥ tatas ca paraspara rūpa avabhāsaḥ sa ca avyavadhāne yujyate na tu sva āśrayābhyām vyavadhāne avayava avayavi rūpayoḥ eka vyavadhāne api asaṃśleṣaḥ kim u dvaya vyavadhāne kim ca vyavahāre para upādhau sarvā dhīḥ vyāvahārikī ayathārthā yadā bhāva bheda kalpaḥ tadā mudhā yasya khalu ‘śuklaḥ  gauḥityādi buddhayaḥ vyavahāra aṅga bhūtā dravyeṣu guṇa jāti upādhi nibandhanāḥ tasya etā na yathāvastu jāti guṇa dravyāṇām anyonyam artha antara tvāt  tathā ca na vastu nibandhanaḥ  vyavahāraḥ buddhyā anupadarśitasya avyavahāra aṅgavāt buddhi upadarśitasya ca tathā abhāvāt evam ca pratyaya viracitena eva ayam arthena vyāvṛttaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  anuvṛttaḥ ca iti vyarthā vastu bheda kalpanā kalpitasya api tasya vyavahāre anupayogāditarasya ca upayogāt  yathārtha tvāya hi vyāvahāri kīṇām buddhīnām vastu bhedaḥ kalpyate kalpite ca tasmin para upādhi tvāt tāsām na ayathārtha tva parihāraḥ syāt etad  asati vastu bhede ayathārtham api anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta avagraham vyāvahārikam vijñānam na udetum arhati bīja abhāvāt na khalu sthāṇu śakala ādiṣu puruṣa rajata ādi vibhrāntayaḥ nirbījāḥ sāmānya nibandhana tvāt  ucyate ayathārtha dhiyaḥ bījam avaśyam bāhyam eva na dṛṣṭaḥ timirakāma ādiḥ āntaraḥ  api hi upaplavaḥ na viṣaya doṣāt eva sādṛśya ādeḥ ayathārtha jñānam ādhyātmikebhyaḥ  api tu doṣebhyaḥ timira kāma śoka ādibhyaḥ tatra asati vastu bheda ādhyātmikaḥ doṣaḥ  avidyā lakṣaṇaḥ  vyāvahārika jñāna bījam iti na arthaḥ  vastu bhedena astu tarhi ekam dvi ātmakam evam hi paraspara ātma pratipattiḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ kalpate vastu viparītaḥ ca na artha sāmarthya atiśayaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ vastu nibandhanaḥ  vyavahāraḥ na vyāvahārika jñānānām ayathārthā vṛttiḥ syāt etad  ekasya dvi ātmaka tā virodhavatī ekam ca dvi ātmakam ca iti vipratiṣiddham api ca sāmānyam bheda antara anuyāyi tatas  vyāvṛtta svabhāvaḥ  bhedaḥ tayoḥ eka tvam hi virodhāt aśakyāvaham na etad sāram viruddham iti naḥ kva saṃpratyayaḥ yad pramāṇa viparyayeṇa vartate yad tu yathā pramāṇena avagamyate tasya tathā abhāve viruddha tva abhidhāne kam bata ayam āśritya hetum viruddha tva aviruddha tve vyavasthāpayet  pramāṇam ca ekasya sāmānya viśeṣa ātmaka tām avagamayati vyāvṛtti anuvṛttibhyām prakhyā rūpa bhedāt sāmāna adhikaraṇyā avagamāt ca (a eka adhikaraṇyā avagamāt ca edition) tad idam asāṃpratam yatas  na īdṛśām vipratiṣiddha artha jñānānām prāmāṇyam eva yujyate saṃśaya jñānavat anyathā saṃśaya viṣayaḥ  api dvi ātmā syāt  dvi ābhāsa tvāt tasya sāmānādhikaraṇyāt ca tad avabhāsayoḥ atha matam na saṃśayite rūpa samuccaya avagamaḥ yathā sāmānya viśeṣavati ‘ayam vā ayam vā aiti pratīteḥ mā bhūt samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ syāt  saḥ  api na vastunaḥ  vikalpa anupapatteḥ ekam api tarhi na dvi ātmakam ekasya dvi ātmaka tā virodhāt  tatra yathā saṃśaya jñānam vipratiṣedhāt apramāṇam tathā sāmānya viśeṣa pratipattiḥ api aika adhikaraṇyāt  syāt etad  na saṃśaya jñānam vipratiṣedhāt apramāṇam nirṇaya jñānena tu bādhanāt  yatra tarhi na nirṇayaḥ tatra vikalpa ātma tā syāt  api ca yathā bādhāyām ekasya aprāmāṇyam nirākaraṇāt  evam virodhe api dvayoḥ ekasya vā jñānasya viruddha rūpa upagrahe tad rūpa adhigatyoḥ anyonya nirākaraṇāt tatra eka nirākaraṇe itarasmāt niścayaḥ paraspara nirākṛtau tulya bala tve sandeha iti na saṃśaya jñānāt ekasya sāmānya viśeṣa pratipattiḥ viśiṣyate tasmāt iha anaikāntikam vastu iti evam jñānam su niścitam iti sva pakṣa upavarṇanam api ca eka tvam avirodhena bheda sāmānyayoḥ yadi na dvi ātma tā bhavet ekatara nirbhakta bhāgavat avaśyam anena padārthānām bheda abhedau vyavasthāpayatā yathā tāvat sāmānyam abhinnam viśeṣā bhidyanta iti bheda abhedayoḥ lakṣaṇam vācyam tatra rūpa virodhaḥ  anyonya abhāvaḥ  bheda lakṣaṇam viparyayaḥ  abheda lakṣaṇam rūpa virodhāt hi anyonya abhāva paryāyāt viśeṣā bhidyante bhidyamāneṣu api teṣu sāmānyam abhinnam viparyayāt  tatra sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ yadi sva rūpa virodhaḥ  anyonya abhāvaḥ na ekatvam bhedānām iva parasparam atha sāmānya viśeṣa buddhi eḥ aika ādhikaraṇyena utpatteḥ sva rūpa virodhaḥ  abhyupeyate na tarhi ekam dvi ātmakam sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sva rūpa virodha abhāvāt asati bhede dvi tva anupapatteḥ yathā na sāmānya aṃśa u dvi rūpaḥ  viśeṣa aṃśaḥ  vā rūpa virodha abhāvāt tatra ekasmin nirbhakte dvi tva abhāvāt  tathā sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ api sāmānādhikaraṇya buddheḥ yadi na rūpa virodhaḥ na paraspara ātma abhāvaḥ (ṃ=  bh paraspara abhāvaḥ edition) dvi tvam na yujyate atha rūpa virodhaḥ na ekatvam iti yadi matam na sva rūpa virodhāt nānātvam tad abhāvāt ca eka tvam yena sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sva rūpa virodha abhāvāt dvi tvam na syāt anyatarasya iva bhāgasya kim tu buddhe rūpa bheda abhedābhyām sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ ca paraspara ātma tvena pratipatteḥ asati api anyonya abhāva lakṣaṇe sva rūpa virodhe buddhe rūpa bhedāt dvi tvam aṃśe tu rūpa abhedāt eka tvam atas  vastunaḥ  dvi rūpa buddhi grāhya tvāt  dvi ātma tā iti tatra ucyate aikātmya buddheḥ bhāge ced evam vastuni tarhi asau na ced kutastyam eka tvam asti ced  dvi ātma tā katham yadi tarhi buddheḥ eka rūpa upagrāhi tvāt abhedom aśasya vastu vicāryam tatra api buddhiḥ kim eka rūpa upagrāhiṇī na vā iti tatra yadi na eka rūpa upagrāhiṇī vastuni buddhiḥ sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam hi vastu tad dvi rūpa buddhi upagrāhyam katham eka tvam vastunaḥ buddhi rūpā bhedasya abheda lakṣaṇasya abhāvāt  rūpa bhedasya ca bheda lakṣaṇasya bhāvāt  atha eka rūpa upagrāhiṇi eva vastuni buddhiḥ na dvi ātmaka tvam aṃśavat eva atha matam buddhi rūpa bhedaḥ paraspara ātmā abhāvaḥ ca (ṃ= s ābh paraspara ātma tā bhāvaḥ ca edition) bheda lakṣaṇam tatra gavādayaḥ  bhedā bhinna rūpa buddhi upagrāhyāḥ parasparān ātmānaḥ ca na tu sāmānya viśeṣau buddhi rūpa bhede api paraspara ātma tvena pratipatteḥ evam api sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bheda lakṣaṇena virahān na dvi ātma tā aṃśavat iti uktam yadi manyeta buddhi rūpā bhedaḥ (ṃ=  bh buddheḥ rūpa abhedaḥ edition) paraspara ātma pratipattiḥ ca dve abheda lakṣaṇe tatra aṃśasya rūpa abhedāt eka tvam ubhayoḥ tu paraspara ātma tva pratīteḥ viśeṣāṇām tu na buddhe rūpa avibhāgaḥ na paraspara ātma pratipattiḥ iti bhinnā iti evam api abheda lakṣaṇe sati paraspara ātma pratipattau ubhaya abhāve ca bheda lakṣaṇe avidyamāne na dvi ātma tā na ca ekasya abhedasya dve lakṣaṇe yujyete lakṣaṇa abhedaḥ  hi abhedam vyavasthāpayati tad bhedaḥ ca bhedam lakṣaṇa bhede api ced tattvam anya tvam ca lakṣaṇa abhede api yadi vyartha tā eva lakṣaṇasya syāt iti api ca sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ abhede buddhi antarasya vaiyarthyam eka aṃśa iva ca āpatet  nānā tvāt arthavat tā ced eka tvāt vyartha tā na kim buddhi antara pravṛttiḥ eva sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ eka vastu ātma tām apākaroti sā hi nānā ātma tve bhedeṣu iva arthavatī anadhigata adhigamāt ekatve tu yathā sāmānya viśeṣa vibhāgayoḥ sva buddhi samadhi gatayoḥ na vilakṣaṇam buddhi antaram arthyate tathā sāmānya buddheḥ na buddhi antaram vilakṣaṇam viśeṣa adhigamāya prārthyeta tathā viśeṣa buddheḥ na sāmānya adhigamāya atha na atyantam avyatirekaḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ vyatirekaḥ  api tu tatra vyatirekāt arthavat tā iti tad asat  evam api kuta etad  vyatirekāt arthavat tvam bhedavat  na punar avyatirekāt eka aṃśavat vaiyarthyam tulyayoḥ hi bheda abhedayoḥ kuta etad  bhedāt ekayā buddhyā na grahaṇam na punar abhedāt grahaṇam iti buddhi antara vaiyarthyam autsargikaḥ ca hetu abhāve phala abhāvaḥ svabhāva siddhaḥ tasya hetu bhāve phala bhāvaḥ  apavādaḥ tatra abhede hetu bhāvāt ekayā eva buddhyā ubhaya adhigamaḥ  yuktaḥ na ekatve anyatara adhigama hetuḥ na asti iti śakyam vaktum atha api kathañcid nā asti iti ucyeta tathā api asti tāvat  eka tvāt  tatra hetu bhāvāt  phala bhāvaḥ syāt  tasya kāraṇa tvāt  na tu abhāvaḥ  abhāvasya kāraṇam svabhāva siddhaḥ tu abhāvaḥ phalasya tasya hetu nibandhanaḥ phala bhāvaḥ  nivartakaḥ sa ca hetuḥ ubhayatra asti tāvat  asattvam tu anupayogam akāraṇa tvāt iti api ca sāmānyam na hi vastu ātmā na bhedaḥ citra eva saḥ tasyānanvayataḥ  bheda vādaḥ śabda antara āt ayam yasya ekam ubhaya ātmakam vastu na tasya sāmānya mātram vastuna ātmā na viśeṣa mātram tanmātra tve vastu bheda prasaṅgāt  tasmāt  saṃbhinna ubhaya rūpaḥ śabalaḥ  vastu ātmā na ca śabalasya anyatra anugamaḥ yasya tu anugamaḥ sa vastu rūpam na bhavati tathā ca śabda antaram avalambya bhedā eva satyā iti etad pratipādyate śabda antareṇa vā hetunā dvi ātmakam ekam iti anuganturavastu svabhāva tve kalpanā viṣaya tvāt syāt etad  mā bhūt vastu tad aṃśa tvam tu na vāryate anyathā nirbījā kalpanā api na bhavet  kaḥ punar ayam aṃśaḥ  nāma na tāvat vastu eva tanmātra rūpa tve vastunaḥ  bheda prasaṅga iti uktam na api vastunaḥ  anyat svayam vastu sāmānya viśeṣa tadvatām trayāṇām vastūnām prasaṅgāt  atha na vastu eva na anyat svayam vastu pariśeṣāt  kalpanā viṣayaḥ tattva anya tva abhyām anirvacanīyaḥ nanu na aṃśa um aśinaḥ artha antaram na api sa eva ubhayathānaṃśa tvāt  na api avastu ata eva na hi khapuṣpam kasyacid aṃśaḥ  bhavati tatra aṃśa anugame vastu eva anugatam bhavati tasya tad avyatirekāt  na etad sāram ananugamāt aṃśa antarasya kim na vastunaḥ  ananugamaḥ api tu ananugama (api tu ananugama edition) eva tasya samudāya ātmaka tvāt eka abhāve api abhāvāt  tathā hi itaretara apekṣau vā sāmānya viśeṣau vastu tad samāhāraḥ  vā ubhayathārtha antare viśeṣasya abhāvāt na vastu anvayaḥ pratyekam anapekṣayoḥ vastu tve na ubhaya ātmakam ekam vastu syāt iti suṣṭhu ucyate tasyānanvayataḥ  bheda vādaḥ śabda antara āt ayam iti yadi vā akhila bhāvānām abhedāt tad atattvataḥ abheda vāda āśrayaṇam syāt anya vidhayā girā aṃśa anuvṛttyā vā vastu anugame advaita vādaḥ tathā hi gauḥ svatas tāvat gauḥ sat dravya ādi rūpa anugamāt aśva vastunaḥ  anugamāt aśvaḥ tad evam gauḥ gauḥ ca aśvaḥ ca aśvaḥ  api tāvat aśvaḥ sat dravya ādi rūpa anugamena gaḥ vastunaḥ  anvayāt gauḥ tad evam aśvaḥ  api aśvaḥ  gauḥ ca tad evam sarva bhāvānām tad bhāvāni abhāvābhyām abheda iti advaitam jagat iti uktam anya prakārayā vācā satyam dvaitam api asti yatas tad bhāvāni abhāvābhyāmbhedaḥ na etad sāram gauḥ api ced aśvaḥ gauḥ ca aśvaḥ ca tad kutaḥ anya tvam gauḥ aśva iti api (gauḥ ca aśvaḥ ca iti api edition) bheda abhidhānam anibandhanam eva siddhe hi gavāśvabhede etad upapadyate gavāśvasya tu pratyekam gavāśva tve bheda abhāvāt anibandhanam eva tad  nanu viśeṣa aṃśānām vyāvṛtteḥ anyatva siddhiḥ tathā ca dvaitādvaita ātmakam jagat iti atha viśeṣa vyāvṛtteḥ anya tva siddhiḥ kim ubhaya rūpa tvāt vastunaḥ  vastu antare anugamaḥ  na asti aśvavastu gaḥ vastu na bhavati atha asti anugamaḥ aśvaḥ  api gauḥ bhavati tatra pūrvasmin kalpe vastunaḥ  ananvayāt anuyataḥ ca avastu tvāt bheda vāda iti uktam atha viśeṣa vyāvṛttau= api tad vastu anugatam bhavati aśvaḥ  gauḥ (bhavati aśvaḥ  api edition) kutaḥ anyatva siddhiḥ yadi matam anugatam ca ananugatam ca aśve gaḥ vastu bhavati ca aśvaḥ  gauḥ gauḥ tu gauḥ eva bhavati eva hi tatra gaḥ vastu tatas  anyatva siddhiḥ iti atha gaḥ vastu katham vaktavyam kim yad gauḥ bhavati eva atha yad na bhavati api tatra pūrvasyām kalpanāyām na vastunaḥ  anugama iti ananvitāni vastūni dvitīyasyām vastunaḥ  vastu antare anvayāt advaitam sarvathā yena viśeṣeṇa ayam aśvāt gaḥ vastu vyavasthāpayati anyat tad viśeṣa yujaḥ tu tasya ananvayāt bheda vādaḥ atha ananvaya doṣān na viśeṣam āśrayati abheda vāda iti na dvaita advaitakalpanā upapadyata iti dravya paryāya arthakānām naya etena vāritaḥ teṣām api dravya nayaḥ paryāyanaya eva vā ye ca dravyam nityam mṛd suvarṇa ādi tasya (tasya tu ṃs ā tasya ca edition) ghaṭa rucaka ādayaḥ paryāyā viśeṣa ākhyā apāyina upāyinaḥ ca avyatirekāḥ na ca te dravyam eva tasya sthitimat tvāt  na ca tatas  atyantam vyāvartante bhedena anupalabdheḥ dravyasya eva rucaka ādi rūpeṇa pratyayāt  evam dravya paryāya rūpam vastu atha (ṃ=  bh atha edition) tu dravyam eva syāt  vardhamānaka bhaṅgena rucaka kriyāyām na kiñcid utpannam naṣṭam vā iti prīti śokau tad arthinoḥ na syātām atha tu paryāya mātram hema arthinaḥ  madhyastha tā na syāt  paryāya mātre hi hemni hemnaḥ  vināśāt paryāya vināśe katham madhyastha tā utpāde vā tasmāt dravya paryāya rūpa tvāt vastuna utpatti sthiti bhaṅgānām ekatra saṃbhavāt dravya rūpa sthiteḥ mādhyasthyam paryāyayoḥ utpatti vināśābhyām prīti śokau= avakalpete iti manyante tad nītiḥ api anena eva nirākṛtā prakāreṇa tathā hi teṣām api vastunaḥ  vastu antara anvaye api bhāga abhāvāt dravya mātram syāt  atha na vastu anveti dravya paryāya rūpa tvāt vastunaḥ paryāya antare ca paryāya antarasya ananugamādananvitāni tarhi vyāvṛtta svabhāvāni vastūni yasya anugamaḥ kalpyate tanmātra rūpasya avastu tvāt paryāya mātram avasthitam hi dravyam ucyate na ca evam avasthitam kiñcid ekam vastu asti vastunaḥ tu apoddhṛtasya aṃśasya avasthāna kalpanā kalpanā eva vastunaḥ citra tvāt tasya ca atathā bhāvāt iti api ca utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām ekatra samavāyataḥ prīti madhya stha tā aśokāḥ syuḥ na syuḥ iti durghaṭam yasya khalu dravyāt paryāyā bhidyante tasya dravya mātra arthinaḥ  dravyasya sthiteḥ vināśa abhāvāt apūrvasya anutpādāt madhyastha tā rucaka arthinaḥ tasya apūrvasya utpatteḥ prītiḥ vardhamānaka arthinaḥ tasya vināśāt śokaḥ iti vyavasthā kalpate yasya tu na paryāyebhyaḥ  anyat dravyam (ṃ=  ā yasya tu paryāyebhyaḥ  ananyat dravyam edition) na dravyāt anye paryāyāḥ tasya utpatti sthiti bhaṅgānām ekatra samavāye dravya arthinaḥ  madhyastha tā bhavet  na bhavet ca prīti śokau syātām na syātām na hi tad dravyam avatiṣṭhata eva vinaśyati apūrvam ca utpadyate tatra vināśāt apūrva utpatteḥ ca prīti śokau syātām na madhyastha tā madhyastha tā ca sthiteḥ syāt  iti durghaṭam āpadyeta tathā vardhamānaka arthinaḥ tad nāśāt śokaḥ syāt  na ca syāt  sthiteḥ prītiḥ ca tasya apūrvasya utpādāt syāt na ca bhavet  pūrvasya eva sthiteḥ vināśāt ca śokaḥ syāt iti atha bhedaḥ  api asti iti na ayam doṣaḥ abhedaḥ  api asti iti kim na bhavati atha na atyantam abhedaḥ tena na saṃkaraḥ na atyantam abheda iti vyavasthā api na yujyate na ca asya kiñcid kvacid ekāntataḥ sarvatra anekāntam abhyupayataḥ yena ayam viśeṣa ucyate na atyantam abheda iti asaṃkara iti tathā ca na ekāntaḥ sarva bhāvānām yadi sarva vidhānataḥ apravṛtti nivṛtti idam prāptam sarvatra hī jagat  yadā hi sarva prakāreṣu anaikāntika tvam bhāvānām tathā sati na ayam lokaḥ kvacid abhimata sādhana tā prakāram avadhārya pravarteta yatas  na asau tathā eva na api nivarteta yatas  na asā avatathā eva tathā duḥkha hetoḥ na nivarteta na asau tathā eva na api na nivarteta yatas  na asā avatathā eva iti kaṣṭām bata daśām āpadyeta atha vā yad uktam prīti madhya stha tā aśokāḥ syuḥ na syuḥ iti durghaṭam iti tatra brūyuḥ sarva vastuṣu sarva prakārāṇām anaikāntika tvāt kā durghaṭa tā tathā hi prīti madhya stha tā aśokā na ekāntataḥ santi na ekāntataḥ  na santi iti atra ucyate na ekāntaḥ sarva bhāvānām iti yadi khalu prīti ādīnām sat asat tve na aikāntike ( anaikāntike edition) na prīti arthī prīti sādhaneṣu pravarteta prīteḥ vidyamāna tvāt  na api na pravarteta tasyāḥ  abhāvāt  tathā duḥkha nivṛtti arthī na duḥkha sādhana saṃparkam pariharet  tasya asattvāt na api na pariharet  tasya sattvāt  iti apravṛtti nivṛttikam bata viśvam āpannam iti evam tāvat na dve vastunī na ekam dvi ātmakam tatra dvayam avaśiṣyate bhedaḥ satyaḥ tad upādāna abheda kalpanā abhedaḥ  vā satyaḥ tad upādānā bheda kalpanā iti tatra āpekṣika tvāt bhedaḥ  hi bheda graha purassaraḥ na eka jñānam samīkṣya ekam na bhedam tattva hānataḥ na bhedam upādāya abheda kalpanā kutas  āpekṣikaḥ hi bhedaḥ  na anyam anapekṣya śakyate grahītum na ca agṛhītaḥ  bhedaḥ  abheda kalpanāyā upādānam bhavati para apekṣa tve ca asya grahaṇam anupapannam yatas  na agṛhīte bhede para ātmānau vyavatiṣṭhete na ca para ātma vyavasthām antareṇa bheda grahaḥ  asti iti prāc prapañcitam na tu evam (ṃ=  ā na ca evam edition) abheda grahaṇam abheda grahaṇa apekṣam na api bheda grahaṇa apekṣam abheda hāna prasaṅgāt  na hi bhede gṛhīte abhedasya avakāśaḥ  asti tatra abhedam gṛhītvā tam upādāya tasya yathāvat niścaya aśaktau vyavaccheda kalpanā upapadyate yathā eka buddhi nirgrāhyeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu avayava vibhāga kalpanā na tatra bheda upādāna abheda kalpanā bhedaḥ  hi paramāṇuṣu vyavatiṣṭhate te ca atīndriyāḥ nanu ca eka tvam api anusandhāna pratyaya avaseyam sa ca na bhedam antareṇa bheda asparśe (bheda asaṃsparśe edition) hi kim kena anusandhīyatām iti pratyuktam etad  na idānīm abhinna deśa kālaḥ  artha  ekaḥ syāt  asati ca ekasmin kim āśrayā bheda āśaṅkā syāt  yasya anusaṃdhānāt eka tvam ucyata iti api ca sarva pratyātma vedanīyam etad abheda upādānaḥ  bheda iti tathā hi ālocyate vastu mātram jñānena āpāta janmanā acetyamānaḥ  bhedaḥ  api cakāsti iti ati sāhasam vastu mātra viṣayam prathamam avikalpakam pratyakṣam tad pūrvāstu vikalpa buddhayaḥ viśeṣān avagāhanta iti sarva pratyātma vedanīyam syāt etad  viśiṣṭa rūpa upagrāhi ā iva pratyakṣam sa tu bhedaḥ śabdena asaṃsparśāt na tathā upalakṣyate yathā vikalpa buddhau tad ayuktam vipratiṣedhāt  na ca upalakṣyate pratyakṣa buddhau viśeṣaḥ prakāśate ca iti vipratiṣiddham atas  atisāhasam ucyate yaḥ tu saṃvittau= eva vipratipadyate sarvān ātma vyāvṛtta spaṣṭa pratibhāsam pratyakṣam iti vadan tasya uttaram ‘āhuḥ vidhātṛ pratyakṣamityādi uktam eva iti kim ca pratiṣṭhitam ca vijñānam artha mātra avalambanam bhedeṣu tu apratiṣṭha tvam asti indriya dhiyām api vastu dvaya anupapatteḥ ekasya ca dvi ātma tā yogāt avaśya kalpanīye anyatarasya mithyātve yuktam viśeṣa avabhāsasya mithyātvam rajata ādi vibhrāntiṣu darśanāt  na ca vastu mātra avabhāsasya na hi vastu mātra vyabhicāraḥ kvacid jñāne dṛṣṭaḥ  asti antatas tasya eva vastunaḥ pratibhāsanāt  dṛṣṭa tad bhāvasya eva tad kalpanā laghvī kḷpta tvāt yogyatāyāḥ itaratra tu kalpya tvāt  syāt etad  mānasya eva buddhayaḥ kḷpta yogya bhāvā mithyātvam prati na indriya janmānaḥ indriya buddhi samadhigamyāḥ ca bhedā iti etad ca vārtam indriya doṣa anuvidhāyi tvāt bhrāntīnām iti (@doṣa viśeṣa anuvidhāyi@ edition) api ca yasya matam vyāvṛtta sva lakṣaṇā bhāvāḥ tena te anyonya abhāva svabhāvā vyākartavyāḥ tad viśeṣaṇā vā na anyathā vyāvṛtta śabdaḥ  arthavān bhavati tasya itaretara abhāva nimitta tvāt  tatra anyonya abhāva rūpa tvam sarveṣām na prakalpate tatra upādhau pratīyantām tathā bhinnā na rūpataḥ ekasmin= anapekṣe sthite tad abhāva rūpaḥ  anyaḥ  vyavatiṣṭhate sarve tu na anyonya abhāva rūpāḥ kalpante paraspara āśraya sthiti tvāt atha viśeṣaṇam anyonya abhāvaḥ kāmam atada ātmānaḥ  api viśeṣaṇa anurāgāt tathā avagamyantām na tu svabhāva bhedaḥ syāt  nanu na anyonya abhāvaḥ  nāma kaścid  yaḥ  bhāvānām tattvam viśeṣaṇam vā syāt  artha siddhiḥ eva eṣā na ced anyonya abhāvaḥ  kaścid  siddhaḥ tarhi abheda iti api ca bheda tvāt eva viśvasya bhedaḥ  abheda upādāna iti śakyate anumātum dṛṣṭaḥ  hi maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādiṣu abhinna mukha upādānaḥ tad bhedaḥ na ca tatra bhāva antara utpattiḥ viruddha pariṇāma tvāt  syāt etad  abhedaḥ  api śakyaḥ  bheda upādānaḥ  anumātum vana abhedasya taru bheda upādāna tvāt  na bheda abhāva prasaṅgāt  evam hi na kaścid ekaḥ abhinnaḥ paramāṇuḥ api tad abhedaḥ  api hi bheda upādānaḥ syāt vana ādivat  tathā tad aṃśa abhedaḥ  api iti anavasthāyām ekasya abhāvāt tad samuccaya rūpaḥ  abhedaḥ  na syāt  atha kvacid avatiṣṭhate sa ekaḥ tad abhedaḥ  na bheda upādāna iti vyabhicāraḥ tad idam ucyate daparṇa ādau mukhasya iva bhedaḥ  abheda avalambanaḥ bheda avalambanaḥ abhedaḥ  na tathā tad abhāvataḥ api ca pratyekam anuviddha tvāt abhedena mṛṣā mataḥ bhedaḥ  yathā taraṅgāṇām bhedāt bhedaḥ kalāvataḥ abheda anuviddha tvāt pratyekam viśvasya bhedaḥ  mṛṣā yathā jala taraṅgeṣu candramasaḥ tatra hi pratyekam candramā iti abheda anvayaḥ tathā viśvasya bhede api pratyekam ‘idam‘tat‘arthaḥ‘vastu aitya bheda anvayaḥ taru bhedaḥ tu yadi api na mṛṣā vanam iti abheda anugamaḥ ca na pratyekam na hi pratyekam taruṣu vanam iti buddhiḥ atas  na tena vyabhicāraḥ etad artham ca pratyekam iti uktam api ca ekasya eva astu mahimā yad nāneva prakāśate lāghavān na tu bhinnānām yad caka asati abhinnavat idam tāvat ayam bheda vādī praṣṭavyaḥ katham ayam vyāvṛtta sva lakṣaṇeṣu abheda avabhāsa u anuvṛtta vyavahāraḥ ca yadi sādṛśyāt  tad atyantam ananviteṣu anupapannam atha vyāvṛtteḥ agrahāt  kaḥ  hi guñjā pravāla ādīnām rāga vyāvṛttim avagrahītum kṣamate iti tad asat  vyāvṛtta svabhāvasya tad agrahe grahaṇam eva hi na syāt  atha niścaya pratyakṣayoḥ ātma bhedāt aniścayāt  tad asat  ubhaya rūpa vyavahāra darśanāt  tathā hi kāla akṣyām gaḥ sāmāni anibandhanaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ  gavā antara vyāvṛttiḥ ca dṛśyate na ca gavā antara vyāvṛtteḥ aniścaye sa yujyate atha eka artha kriyā kāri tvāt atad kriyā vyāvṛtteḥ tulya tvāt  tad api asāṃpratam artha kriyāṇām api bhedāt atad kriyā vyāvṛtteḥ tulya tva ayogāt na eka sādhya anyasya artha kriyā yena atad kāri vyāvṛttiḥ tulyā syāt  vastu svabhāvaḥ ca vyāvṛttiḥ prativastu bhedāt na tulyā atha asvabhāvāḥ teṣām katham tulyā atha anādi vāsanā upādānaḥ  na vastu gata viśeṣa apekṣaḥ tad api ayuktam niyamāt  kāsucid eva hi vyaktiṣu kaścid eva avabhāsaḥ (ṃ=  bh kaścid eva abheda avabhāsaḥ edition) sa vāsanā mātra upādāna tve na yujyate tasmāt prakṛtyā eva kecid kasyacid abheda avamarśasya yogyāḥ kecid na iti svabhāva viparītā bhāvānām sāmarthya atiśayā kalpayitavyāḥ tathā sati evam gauravāt kalpanāyāḥ ekasya eva astu māhātmyam yad ekaḥ  api na aneva avabhāsate (nānā iva bhāsate edition) laghu tvāt kalpanāyāḥ na tu bhinnānām te sāmarthya atiśayāḥ yad amī abhinnā iva bhāsante (iva avabhāsante edition) bheda vyavahāraḥ ca (bheda vyavahārāḥ ca edition) yathā avabhāsam bheda vādinām iva abheda vyavahāra upapadyate (@vyavahārā upapadyante edition) tathā hi ātyantika bheda vādinām yathā avabhāsam abheda vyavahāraḥ na yathāvastu saṃsarga vādinām api sāmānyasya arthasya artha antara tvāt yatha avabhāsam eva bhedeṣu abheda vyavahāraḥ ye api anartha antara vādinaḥ teṣām api śabala tvāt vastunaḥ tasya ca ananvayāt yathā avabhāsam eva ubhaya vyavahāraḥ na vastu anupāti iti darśitam iti yathā anuvṛtta vyavahāra siddhim yathā avabhāsam kathayanti bāhyāḥ tathā eva bheda vyavahāra yogam vadanti vedānta viveka bhājaḥ iti śrī maṇḍana miśraviracitāyām brahma siddhau tarkakāṇḍaḥ samāptaḥ niyoga kāṇḍaḥ evam pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt karma vidhi virodhāt ca śruta artha parigrahe ye manyante vedāntānām upacarita artha tvam tad pratibodhanāya vihitaḥ prayatnaḥ saṃprati tu kārya eva arthe vedasya prāmāṇyam na bhūta rūpe evam hi uktam ‘codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharmaḥcodanā pramāṇa kaḥ  veda artha  iti yāvat  codanā ca pravartakam vacanam tasmāt kārye arthe vedaḥ pramāṇam vedāntānām api tu pratipatti kartavya tā pramāṇa bhājām tad mukhena tad anugata bhūta ātma tattva viṣaya bodhaka tvam atas te api kārya niṣṭhatām na ativartante tathā ca katham tarhi mantra artha vādāḥ sa upaniṣad kā iti āśaṅkya ‘codanā hi bhūtam bhavantamiti ādi uktam etad uktam bhavati kāryam artham avagamayantī codanā eva bhūta ādikam api artham avagamayati iti ye manyante tad pratibodhanāya prayatyate tisraḥ ca pratipattayaḥ  brahmaṇi prathamā tāvat śabdāt  anyā śabdāt pratipadya tad santānavatī dhyāna bhāvanā upāsana ādi śabda vācyā anyā tatas  labdha niṣpattiḥ vigalita nikhila vikalpā sākṣātkaraṇa rūpā tatra prathamām adhikṛtya ucyate śabdāt yad ātma vijñānam tad na tāvat vidhīyate bhavati adhīta vedasya tad hi karma avabodhavat brahmaṇaḥ  hi pramāṇa antara anadhi gamanīya rūpa tvāt śabda adhigamya svabhāva viṣayam jñānam vidheyam tatra yad śabdāt eva jñānam tad avidheyam vidhim antareṇa bhāvāt karma avabodhavat yathā eva ‘svarga kāmaḥ  yajetaiti śruta vākyasya vākya artha avabodhaḥ tad vākya prāmāṇyāt eva bhavati na vidhi antaram apekṣate tathā ātma svarūpa abhidhāyi vākya prāmāṇyāt ātma avabodhaḥ  vidhi anapekṣaḥ saṃjāyate sati pramāṇe tad sāmarthyena eva prameya bodha utpatteḥ na khalu sa upakaraṇe samagre pramāṇe sati icchā api puruṣasya apekṣyate jñānam prati aniṣṭānām api avabodhāt prāk eva vidhiḥ tām eva vidheḥ anapekṣatām karma avabodhe darśayati svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti bodhe asmin=vyapekṣyate vidhiḥ anyaḥ  anavasthānāt na ayam karma vyavasthiteḥ na karma vidhi vākya artha jñāna pravṛttau vidhiḥ apekṣyate anyaḥ na tad gata eva vā anyasmin= anavasthā doṣāt  tad artha jñāne api vidhi antarasya apekṣaṇīya tvāt tad gatasya ca karma viṣaya tvena tad bodham vidhātum asāmarthyāt  nanu yathā eṣām grahaṇe vidhi antaram apekṣyate ‘svādhyāyaḥ  adhyetavyaḥiti na ca anavasthā tadvat tad artha bodhe api syāt  asti ca vidhiḥ ‘vedaḥ kṛtsnaḥ  adhigantavyaḥiti viṣama upanyāsaḥ apravṛttaḥ  api hi svādhyāya adhyayana vidhi vākya adhyayane puruṣa antara adhītāt tatas tasya ca anyeṣām ca vākyānām adhyayane pravartate śākhā antarīya aṅga upasaṃhāra iva śravaṇa mātrāt  na khalu svādhītam eva vākyam pravartayati yathā ekaḥ tathā puruṣa antarāṇi api anādi tvāt vedavat tad adhyayanasya api anavabuddha arthaḥ tu avabodha vidhiḥ na avabodhe pravartayati tad artha bodhaḥ ced vidhi apekṣaḥ na tatra sa eva pravartayati anavabuddha artha tvāt itaretara āśrayam syāt  tad artha bodhāt pravṛttiḥ pravṛttasya ca tad artha bodha iti tasmāt vidhi antaram apekṣitavyam iti anavasthā na ca ‘vedaḥ kṛtsnaḥ  adhigantavyaḥ aitya pūrva artha vidhiḥ ‘dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanamiti nyāya prāptaḥ  arthaḥ pradarśyate atha api eṣa vidhiḥ svādhyāya adhyayana vidhinā artha ākṣiptam artha jñānam na ucyeta (@jñānam ucyeta editiā ūn alteḥ native reat ing in thattva samīkṣā) tathā api brahma svarūpa abhidhāyi veda vākya prabhave bodhe na pṛthagvidhiḥ apekṣitavyaḥ karma vidhi vākyavat  yathā eva ‘svarga kāmaḥ  yajetaiti sāmānya vidhinā siddhe na anyaḥ  apekṣyate anavasthānāt  sati api vidhau= anyasya apekṣaṇāt  na ca etad gata eva karma viṣaya tvāt  evam tattva pratipatti pareṣu api vākyeṣu na vidhiḥ apekṣitavyaḥ vākya sāmarthyāt eva tattva bodha utpādāt iti itas ca phalam vidheya avagamāt pravṛttiḥ ca uttarā vidheḥ anyonya saṃśrayāt na eṣa śābdaḥ  bodhaḥ sa naḥ paraḥ śabdāt avagamya vidheyam yā pravṛttiḥ sā vidheḥ prayojanam na tu śabda prabhavaḥ  vidheya avagama eva anyonya saṃśrayāt  avagate śabda arthe pravṛtteḥ pravṛttasya ca avagamāt  śabda artha bodhāt eva vā śabda artha bodha iti ātma āśrayaḥ anyonya saṃśrayaḥ tu tulya anupapatti tvāt uktaḥ yaḥ tu tattva avabodha parāt vākyāt tattva avabodhaḥ na asau śabda artha bodhāt parācīnaḥ kintu sa eva iti api ca jāte bodhe na pravartyaḥ  natarām khalva bodhake śabde na (śabdena edition) niścaye tasmāt anyasmāt anya vāñchanam udapādi ced  ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsīt ekam eva advitīyamiti upakramāt  ‘tattvam asi aiti antāt vākyāt ātma tattva avabodhaḥ padānām paraspara anvitā artha tvāt kim anyat vidhiḥ kariṣyati na pravṛtta eva pravartyaḥ atha padārtha samanvaya mātrāt na tattva bodha utpādaḥ suta rām apravartyaḥ śābdasya tattva avabodhasya asaṃbhavāt syāt etad  utpanne api tattva avabhāse śabdāt  niścaye pravartyaḥ ‘evam idamiti tad na yadi tasmāt śabdān niścayaḥ sa jāta eva atha anyatas  niścayaḥ anyavāñchanam pramāṇa antara apekṣā na tatra tattva niścaya nibandhanam śabdaḥ syāt  evam tāvat na tattva niścayāya vidhiḥ arthyate atha avivakṣita artha tva nivṛttyai prārthyate vidhiḥ arthaḥ  jñātavya iti ukte jñeyaḥ syāt na avivakṣitaḥ yad api matam sati api vākyāt artha upaplave tātparyam durlabham bhūta artha parasya vaiyarthyāt  sāṃśayika tvam vā atātparyasya api darśanāt japa mantreṣu vidhau tu satyartha jñānasya codita tvāt na arthaḥ  avivakṣitaḥ  bhavitum arhati tasmāt vivakṣita artha tvāya vidhiḥ prārthyaḥ tad vārtam artha para tā śabdānām loka vedayoḥ ‘a viśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaiti utsargavatī yatas  autsargikaḥ śabdānām artham prati śeṣa bhāvaḥ nimitta antarāt tu sva rūpa pradhāna tvam avivakṣita artha tvam apavādaḥ  loke tathā vede api lokau= agamya tvāt śabda sāmarthyasya tad uktam ‘a viśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaḥiti api ca dṛṣṭa artha tā ca svādhyāya vidheḥ atra na bhidyate bhavet itarathā kṛtsnaḥ sa vidhi arthaḥ  avivakṣitaḥ yathā eva karma vidhīnām ‘dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanamiti na avivakṣita arthānām adhyayanāt phala antara kalpanā tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt ātma tattva avabodhasya vedāntānām na ca bhūta artha pratipattau vaiyarthyam iti vakṣyate pratipatti vidhau ca tulyam avaśyam ca etad evam vijñeyam anyathā saha vidhāyakena kṛtsnasya avivakṣita artha tā syāt  yatas  vidhāyaka śabda nibandhanam anyeṣām vivakṣita artha tvam vidhāyakasya tu na tad nibandhanam asti evam ca tasya avivakṣita artha tve itare api tathā syuḥ atha vidhāyakaḥ prakṛtyā dṛṣṭa artha tvena ca artha paraḥ itare api tathā iti vyarthaḥ  asau vidhiḥ jñānasya puruṣa artha tva siddhaye vidhiḥ iṣyate sarvatra puruṣa artha tvam vidheḥ iti api apeśalam vidhi adhīnaḥ puruṣa artha sādhana tā avabodhaḥ tad śabdataḥ labdha janmanaḥ  api ātma tattva avabodhasya puruṣa artha sādhanatva avagamaḥ  vidheḥ iti etad api na śobhanam jñeya abhivyāptitaḥ  yasmāt na vijñānāt phala antaram iṣyate mokṣa iti ced sādhyaḥ tattva cyuteḥ na saḥ jñānasya hi dṛṣṭam eva phalam jñātrā jñeya abhivyāptiḥ jñātāram prati tasya prakāśanam (prakāśa tā edition) na tu adṛṣṭam kāla antara bhāvi yad arthaḥ  vidhiḥ syāt  syāt etad  ātma jñānasya phala antaram api iṣyate mokṣaḥ tad na asādhya tvāt  na hetu janyaḥ  asau mokṣaḥ tattva cyuteḥ kāryatve vināśāt tasya punar saṃsārāt  ātyantikī ca saṃsāra nivṛttiḥ mokṣa iti ucyate nanu kāryaḥ  api na āśaḥ na naśyati satyam bhāva rūpam tu mokṣam niratiśaya ānanda lakṣaṇam niratiśaya aiśvarya lakṣaṇam ca abhipretya etad ucyate bhāvasya kāryasya vināśena āvinā abhāvāt  āgāmi śarīra indriya buddhi saṃyoga abhāvasya prāgabhāvasya kāryatvam anupapannam eva bandha hetu nivṛttiḥ tu yadi api kāryā kāryatve api ca na asyāḥ  anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā api na asau tattva jñānāt pṛthak iti na tena sādhyā avidyā hi bandha hetuḥ tattva jñāna udaya eva ca tad nivṛttiḥ athavā ‘param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa avatiṣṭhateiti svarūpa sthitiḥ muktiḥ uktā sādhya tve ca na svarūpa sthitiḥ syāt  atas  mokṣa tvāt cyaveta yad tu ‘na sa (na ca edition) punar āvartateiti śruteḥ prāmāṇyāt kāryasya api mokṣasya nitya tvam iti dṛṣṭa viparītam api tadā aśrīyeta ananya gati tve śruteḥ yadā tu vidita ātma tattvasya advayam viśuddha prakāśam ātmānam paśyataḥ samutkhātāyām anavayavena avidyāyām hetu abhāvāt punar bandhasya asaṃbhāvya tvāt prāptam eva artham vartamāna apadeśāt anuvadati śrutiḥ artha vāda tvena tadā kutas tad prāmāṇyāt ananta phala tvam tathā hi vartamāna apadeśāt eva na apunarāvṛttiḥ sādhya tvena avagamyate na ca kāma upabandhaḥ  asti yatas  sādhya tā gamyeta tasmāt artha vādaḥ arthavādāt api ca yā phala kalpanā sā api jñāne jñeya tattva avabhāsa dṛṣṭa phala nirākāṅkṣe anupapannā puruṣa artha tā ca asya vakṣyata iti anye punar āhuḥ vidheḥ vinā kārya śūnyam bhūta artham anuvādakam vacaḥ syāt anuvādaḥ ca pramāṇa antara gocare tad pramāṇa antara apekṣam prāmāṇyam ativartate māna antarasya aviṣaye vidhi arthe tu pratiṣṭhitam anapekṣam pramāṇa tvam aśnute karma vākyavat  para pravṛtti abhāve api prāmāṇyāya eva tad vidhiḥ vidhim antareṇa na kārya upadeśa pratītiḥ yathā avasthitam vastu tadvidhasya anuvāda mātra tvam gamyate anuvādaḥ ca pramāṇa antara viṣaya iti tad apekṣaḥ  bhūta arthaḥ  na artha ucyata iti sa apekṣa tvāt aprāmāṇyam vidhi arthasya tu pramāṇa antara aviṣaya tvāt tad niṣṭham anapekṣam pramāṇam karma vidhi vākyavat  pramāṇa antara aviṣayaḥ ca vidhi arthaḥ na hi ‘kuru aiti śabda jñānāt anyatas  pratītiḥ evam ca sati tattva pratipatti pare vākye yadi api vākya artha bodhāt parācīnā pravṛttiḥ vidhi phalam na asti prāmāṇyāya eva tu vidhi niṣṭha tvam eṣitavyam iti atra ucyate pramāṇa antara yātā artha bhāvaḥ kim anuvāda tā uta bhūta artha tā tatra siddhārtham api yad vacaḥ na māna antara labdha artha tayā tasya avabodhakam na tad sa apekṣam eṣā ced abhipreta anuvāda tā kaḥ punar anuvādaḥ adhigama antara saṃbhinna artha tvam māna antareṇa adhigata iti pratipādanam āhosvit bhūtārtha tā mātram tatra pūrvasmin kalpe bhavatu adhigama antara saṃbhinna artham sa apekṣam yad tu bhūta artham api na māna antara adhigata iti bodhayati na tad anuvādakam na sa apekṣam pūrva adhigama saṃsparśena pratipatteḥ abhāvāt  atha aparaḥ kalpaḥ sa apekṣatāyāḥ kaḥ  hetuḥ śuddhā siddhārtha tā yadi pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ tad vyapekṣaṇa kāraṇam anṛdhī prabhave na asti bhūta arthe api sa vaidike bhūta artha mātram ced anuvāda tā na sa apekṣa tva hetuḥ asti na bhūta artha tā eva sa apekṣa tva hetuḥ bhūta arthayoḥ api pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ anapekṣa tvāt tasmāt bhūta arthe abhūta arthe vā adhigama antara saṃsparśaḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣā hetuḥ smṛtau darśanāt  sā hi adhigama antara saṃbhinna artha iti tad sādhanam apekṣate evam ca puruṣa buddhi prabhavam bhūta artham abhūta artham vā vacaḥ  bhavati sa apekṣam tatas  hi tad saṃbhinna eva arthe pratyayaḥ na tu anapekṣita pūrva adhigamaḥ svātantryeṇa arthe yathā uktam ‘api ca pauruṣeyāt vacanāt  ‘eva mayam puruṣaḥ  veda aiti bhavati pratyayaḥ na ‘evam arthaḥitiapuruṣa buddhi prabhava tvāt veda vacasi bhūta arthe api na sa apekṣa tva hetuḥ puruṣa saṃbandha kṛta tvāt pūrva adhigama saṃbhedasya syāt etad  apauruṣeye api bhūta arthe tad viṣaye pramāṇa antarasya saṃbhavāt tad apekṣā tathā hi saṃbhavati pramāṇa antare tad viṣaye tad visaṃvādaḥ  api śaṅkyeta tasmāt tad abhāvāya tad saṃvādaḥ  apekṣaṇīyaḥ asaṃbhavati tu kārye arthe na kutaścid visaṃvāda āśaṅkā iti na apekṣyam asti atra ucyate na ca saṃbhava mātreṇa tad apekṣau= akalpate viśeṣaḥ  na hi gamyeta sa apekṣa tve tadā tayoḥ dvayoḥ eka viṣaya saṃbhave kuta etad  śabdaḥ tad apekṣaḥ na punar tad pramāṇa antaram śabda apekṣam syāt iti yadi śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara adhigata viṣayaḥ  loke dṛṣṭa iti pramāṇa antarasya aviṣaye tarhi natarām prāmāṇyam tasya bhavati pramāṇa antara viṣaye hi pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt api tāvat syāt  anyatra tad abhāvāt  durlabham tad  atha pauruṣeya tva kāritā loka vacasām pramāṇa antara adhigata artha tā na śabda sāmarthya kāri tā śabdasya pramāṇa antara asaṃbhinna eva arthe sāmarthyam na tarhi pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt śabda eva sa apekṣaḥ tad api śabda saṃbhavāt śabda apekṣam syāt  kim atas tasya sa apekṣa tvena apramāṇam syāt  na śabdasya tatra apekṣā yujyate sati hi tasya prāmāṇye tad saṃvāda visaṃvādau= apekṣyeyātām atha śabdasya aprāmāṇyāt na tad  śabda apekṣayā pramāṇam pramāṇam eva anapekṣa tvāt  śabdasya aprāmāṇyam kutas  pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt tasya ca prāmāṇyam anapekṣa tvāt anapekṣa tvam ca śabdasya aprāmāṇyāt itaretara āśrayam pramāṇe hi śabde tad viṣaye saṃbhavati tad api sa apekṣam syāt tad saṃbhava iva śabdaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt atha śabda saṃbhave api na tad sāpekṣam tad saṃbhave api na śabdasya sa apekṣatā viśeṣa abhāvāt api ca pratyakṣa anumayoḥ evam vṛtteḥ anyonya gocare paraspara vyapekṣa tvam aviśeṣam prasajyate syāt akṣam api sa apekṣam yad akṣa antara gocare saṃbhava mātreṇa sa apekṣa tve pratyakṣa anumayoḥ ekasmin viṣaye saṃbhavāt anyonya apekṣa tvāt aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ tathā sattā guṇa tva dravyeṣu aneka indriya grāhyeṣu indriya antarāṇām indriya antara sāpekṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ atha śabdasya eva pramāṇa antara saṃbhave sa apekṣa tvam viśeṣa hetuḥ vācyaḥ pramāṇa antara adhi gata artha tva darśanāt iti ced  uktam atra yadi śabda mātra dharmaḥ  ayam asaṃbhavāt eva tad viṣaye pratyakṣa ādeḥ buddha ādi vākyavat aprāmāṇyam prāpnoti saṃbhave tu indriya viṣaye pratyayita puruṣa vacaḥvat yujyate prāmāṇyam yathā uktam ‘tat ced pratyayitāt puruṣāt indriya viṣayam vā avitatham eva taditi atha pauruṣeya dharmaḥ  ayam na saṃbhavat pramāṇa antara viṣayasya api apauruṣeyasya śabdasya sa apekṣa tvam api ca pratyakṣa adhigata viṣayam kiñcid anumānam iti na sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya tathā pratyakṣa sāpekṣatā yathā ca āgama pūrvakam ṣaḍja ādi viveka viṣayam pratyakṣam iti na sarvam pratyakṣam tathā evam puruṣa vacasām pramāṇa antara adhigata viṣaya tva darśane api na apauruṣeyasya tathā abhāvaḥ  bhūta arthasya api anyathā sutarām pramāṇa antara asaṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam syāt iti uktam api ca asaṃbhavāt auṣadha ādi niyogasya anapekṣatā laukikasya prasajyeta nara pratyaya pūrvakaḥ viniyogaḥ tatra tena vyapekṣā vaidike punar  abuddhi pūrvakaḥ saḥ  api iti anapekṣa tvam ucyate yadi kārye niyoga arthe pramāṇa antarasya asaṃbhavāt veda vacasām tad niṣṭhānām anapekṣa tvam ‘jvara viyoga kāma idam auṣadham pibet‘svarga kāmaḥ sikatā bhakṣayetiti loka vacāṃsi api kārya niṣṭhāni anapekṣāṇi prāmāṇyam aśnu vīran atha yaḥ tatra sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sa puruṣa vivakṣā pūrvakaḥ tena tatra sa apekṣatā vede tu sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ  api na puruṣa vivakṣā pūrvakaḥ iti anapekṣa tvam yaḥ  vā viṣaya niyojya niyogānām saṃbandhaḥ sa puruṣa buddhi viracitaḥ  loka vākye vede tu kevalam niyogaḥ  apuruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ saḥ  api iti anapekṣa tvam ucyate nṛ buddhi pūrva tā eva ittham hanta apekṣā nibandhanam māna antara asaṃbhave api tatra sa apekṣatā yatas  asaṃbhavat pramāṇa antara kārya niṣṭhe api ced vākye puruṣa saṃbandhāt sa apekṣa tvam puruṣa buddhi pūrva tā eva tarhi pramāṇa antara vyapekṣā kāraṇam anvaya vyatirekābhyām tad bhāve loke sa apekṣa tvāt  tad abhāve vede nirapekṣa tvāt  na viṣaye pramāṇa antara saṃbhavaḥ tad abhāve api loka niyoge sa apekṣa tva darśanāt atha matam vede niyoga niṣṭha tvam viniyoga pradhāna tā loke vede na vyapekṣā tad loke ca vyapekṣaṇam niyoga paryavasitam vaidikam vacaḥ sa ca pramāṇa antarasya agocara iti anapekṣa tvam sādhya sādhana bhāva niṣṭham tu laukikam vacaḥ sa pramāṇa antara viṣaya iti sa apekṣatā na śabda mātra sāmarthya pravibhāgaḥ  ayam īdṛśaḥ loka avagata sāmarthyaḥ śabdaḥ  vede api bodhakaḥ na tāvat ayam śabda mātrasya anapekṣita puruṣa saṃbandha asaṃbandhasya śakti pravibhāgaḥ yad ekatra niyogaḥ śabda arthaḥ anyatra viniyogaḥ yathā gaḥ śabdasya sāsna ādimān aśva śabdasya kesara ādimān yatas  loka adhigata sāmarthyaḥ  vede api pratipādakaḥ loke ced viniyogaḥ śabda arthaḥ tatra eva asya sāmarthyam adhigatam na niyoge tatra vede api viniyoga eva pramāṇa arthaḥ syāt  atha māna antarāt jñātvā prayuṅkte puruṣaḥ  vacaḥ arthe tad tena tad niṣṭham itarat tu anyathā sthitam atha matam na eṣa śabda mātrasya sāmarthya vibhāgaḥ śabdasya hi nijam sāmarthyam kārya niṣṭhatā eva tathā hi kāryaḥ  niyoga arthaḥ kāryāya ca anyasya anvayaḥ pratīyate na tu kāryasya anya arthaḥ  anvayaḥ tasmāt kāryatvāt niyogasya tad pradhāna tā puruṣaḥ tu pramāṇa antarāt avagamya artham tatra prayuṅkte vacanam na ca niyogaḥ pramāṇa antara gocaraḥ tasmāt na tatra prayoktum arhati viniyogasya tu tathā abhāvāt tatra yujyate prayogaḥ tasmāt viniyoga pradhānam puruṣa vacaḥ vaidikam tu sāmarthyena kāryatvāt niyogasya tad pradhānam iti atra ucyate māna antara vyapekṣa tvāt saṃbhavī anya pramāṇakaḥ hanta asya gocaraḥ  na asmāt apekṣā asya pramā antare yadi puruṣaḥ  adhigate viṣaye vacaḥ prayuṅkte iti viniyoga viṣaya tā tasya kalpyate pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt tarhi saṃbhavat pramāṇa antaraḥ  asya viṣayaḥ na tu saṃbhavat pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt puruṣa vacaḥ  api sa apekṣam sa apekṣa tva nimitta tvāt tadvidhasya viṣayasya tasmāt māna antarāt gatvā parasya pratipattaye vacaḥ prayuṅkte puruṣaḥ  na akasmāt tena tad giri pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ  vyapekṣātaḥ  na saṃbhavāt  sva upalabdhi khyāpanāya puruṣasya gīḥ tatas tasyām pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ ‘mayā upalabdhaḥ  ayam arthaḥ aiti arthaḥ tena tatra upalabdhe saṃbhava asaṃbhavau= eva apekṣyeyātām yatra upalabdheḥ niścayaḥ ‘saṃbhavati asya upalabdhiḥ na ca anupalabhya ayam bravītiiti tatra prāmāṇyam yathā āpta puruṣasya pramāṇa viṣaye yatra tu upalabdheḥ asaṃbhava eva yathā dṛṣṭa arthe buddha ādi vākye yatra ca anupalabhya api vacana pravṛtti saṃbhāvanā tatra aprāmāṇyāt  na tu pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt puruṣa vacane api tad apekṣā apauruṣeya tā tena pauruṣeya tvam eva ca anapekṣa vyapekṣa tva nimitte varṇite budhaiḥ bhūta artham api sa apekṣam na atas  apuruṣa buddhi jam ata eva pauruṣeya tva apauruṣeya tve sa apekṣa tva anapekṣa tva kāraṇe nyāya vidbhiḥ daśite pauruṣeya tva nirākaraṇa prayatnena ‘autpattikaḥ tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥiti autpattike śabda artha sambandhe asvātantryāt śabdasya na puruṣa buddhi pūrvakatvam iti na pramāṇa antara saṃbhinnā śabdāt artha avagatiḥ iti nirapekṣa tvam nanu pramāṇa antara asaṃbhave api kṛta eva yatnaḥ ‘sat saṃprayogeiti satyam codanā eva pramāṇam na anyat  iti avadhāraṇa siddhaye na tu pramāṇam eva iti atha pramāṇa antara saṃbhave api yadi codanā prāmāṇyam na vyāhanyate kaḥ  arthaḥ pramāṇa antara nirākaraṇena dharma tattva jñānam pramāṇa antara saṃbhave hi sarvajña abhimata buddha ādi upadiṣṭaḥ  api dharmaḥ pratīyeta tatra na dharma tattvam avadhāritam syāt  tad avadhāraṇa arthaḥ ca ayam yatnaḥ codanā prāmāṇyam api tad artham mṛgyate na adṛṣṭāya athavā tad virodhāt codanāyāḥ  bādhaḥ syāt  saṃśayaḥ  vā tulya bala tve tena tasya asaṃbhavaḥ pratipādyate na tu tad saṃbhavāt sa apekṣatā iti nanu tad abhāvaḥ  apekṣaṇīyaḥ syāt  kāmam na tu śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣam artham pratipādayati yatas  yad arthasya pratipādakam na tu tad apekṣyate yad apekṣyate na tad artham pratipādayati na hi virodhi pramāṇa abhāvaḥ pratipatti hetuḥ virodha saṃbhava mātreṇa ca aprāmāṇye pratyakṣa ādīnām api tad syāt  api ca virodhi saṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam kārya niṣṭhatve api aparihāryam kartavyatā dvāreṇa bhūta artha pratipatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt  tatra tu pramāṇa antara virodhi saṃbhāvanāt bhūta arthasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt tena kārya niṣṭhatā varṇyate pramāṇa antara viṣaya tve kila anuvāda tvāt pramāṇa antara apekṣam artham pratipādayati pramāṇa antareṇa ayam adhigataḥ iti na svātantryeṇa kārya niṣṭhatve tu svātantryeṇa tasya pramāṇa antara agocara tvāt uktena prakāreṇa na sa apekṣa tvam iti ‘bhūta artham api sa apekṣam na atas  apuruṣa buddhi jam aiti suṣṭhu uktam atha saṃsarga bhājaḥ  naḥ padārthāḥ kriyayā vinā kim āyātam vidheḥ sā api tu astyādiḥ sulabhā kva na yadi matam ākhyāta padārtham antareṇa na nāma padārthānām saṃsargaḥ kriyā hi padārtha saṃśleṣa hetuḥ tad abhāve sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  atas  siddhaḥ  arthaḥ  brahmādiḥ na śabda gocaraḥ padasya avidita saṃgati tvena anavabodhaka tvāt  na vākya arthaḥ tasya saṃsarga ātmaka tvāt  kriyā rahitānām ca padārthānām asaṃsargāt  evam api kriyā abhyupeyatām tad dvāreṇa ca padārtha saṃsarga siddhiḥ āśāsyatām na vidheḥ kaścid arthaḥ sā api ca kriyā sarvatra sulabhā eva aśrūyamāṇā api astyādiḥ ‘astiḥ bhavantī paraḥ prathama puruṣaḥ  aprayujyamānaḥ  api gamyateiti tatra brahma svarūpa pratipatti param vākyam asti artha niṣṭham tad nibandhanaḥ tatra padārtha saṃśleṣaḥ sattāyāḥ ca prakṛtyā eva sat pradhāna tvāt  tad dvāreṇa viśiṣṭa vastu siddhiḥ iti atra āhuḥ na pramāṇau= agamya tāyāḥ  anyā kācana sattā tathā hi yad  pramāṇena avagamyate tatra ‘astiiti vyavahāraḥ  laukikānām viparyaye ‘nāstiiti na khalu anyaḥ sat asat vibhāga hetuḥ lakṣyate artha kriyā bhāva abhāvau ced  na tayoḥ api pramāṇa bhāva abhāva adhīna tvāt  tathā hi kārye api sat vyavahāraḥ  yadi kārya antara nibandhanaḥ anavasthā tasmāt ante api pramāṇāt eva sat vyavahāraḥ tad viparyayāt ca asat vyavahāraḥ evam ced ādau= eva pramāṇa abhāva abhāva nibandhanau sat asat vyavahārau stām tathā ca asti artha niṣṭham vākyam pramāṇa antara apekṣam eva artham bodhayati pramāṇa viṣaya tāyāḥ  asti artha tvāt atra ucyate na ca mānau= agamya tvam asti iti viṣayaḥ  mataḥ mānāt eva yatas  buddhiḥ abhūt asti bhaviṣyati dhūma ādinā mite hi syāt vahni ādau= iyam anyathā bhidyeta uttara kāle vā bhavantī na khalu tridhā na pramāṇau= agamya tvam asti arthaḥ na ‘astiiti buddheḥ tad viṣayaḥ yatas  pramāṇāt eva tridhā buddhiḥ bhavati ‘dhūmāt asti atra agniḥ‘nadīpūra viśeṣāt abhūt vṛṣṭiḥ‘megha udaya viśeṣāt  bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥiti tatra yadi buddhiḥ pramāṇa viṣaya tām gocarayati pramite hi syāt  na pramāṇāt eva na hi prāk  pramāṇa utpatteḥ san pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ pramāṇa saṃbandha nibandhanā ca iyam buddhiḥ atha vaiyātyāt uttara kāla tām eva asyā brūyāt  traividhyam anupapannam pramāṇa saṃbandhasya abhedāt bhinna kāleṣu api artheṣu sva saṃbandhi tayā mānam atha vastu adhigacchati tathā api na eva bhidyeta na ittham ca anya vyapekṣatā atha matam ātma saṃbandhi tayā eva pramāṇena arthaḥ  avagamyate atas  na ‘asti aiti buddheḥ uttara kāla tā pramāṇa saṃbandha viṣayāyā api sva ātma saṃbandhi tayā eva arthasya pratīteḥ evam api asti iti eva sarvatra syāt  na traividhyam sarvasya pramitau pramāṇa saṃbandhasya vartamāna tvāt  na ca ittham pramāṇa antara vyapekṣa tvam asti artha niṣṭhe vacasi tad pramāṇa saṃbandhasya eva asti artha tvāt anyamānau= agamya tvam atha liṅgāt tridhā iṣyate syāt liṅgam api sa apekṣam tad siddheḥ tata eva ced  nairapekṣyam yadi na tad vede daṇḍaiḥ nivāryate atha matam pramāṇa antara gamya tā eva liṅgena adhigamyate tena na uttara kālatā tad ca pramāṇam tri kālam iti traividhyam kim punar tad pratyakṣam tathā hi bhūtāyām dṛṣṭau kasyacid bhūtam pratyakṣam bhaviṣyantyām bhaviṣyat  vartamāne agnau vartamānam iti etad ca vārtam nitya anumeye tasya abhāvāt  api ca liṅgam api evam pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt apramāṇam syāt  atha liṅgāt eva pramāṇa antara sadbhāvasya siddheḥ nirapekṣa tvam tathā hi pramāṇa antara sadbhāva eva idānīm liṅgam pramāṇam na ca tatra anyat apekṣyate pramāṇa sadbhāva dvārā prameya siddhiḥ iti na ayam vidhiḥ vede daṇḍa vāritaḥ vaidikam api vacaḥ  asti artha niṣṭham viśiṣṭa artha pramāṇa sadbhāva eva pramāṇam tatra nirapekṣam tad pramāṇa dvārā ca viśiṣṭa artha siddhiḥ iti samānam tad saṃbhavaḥ  alaukika arthe (laiṅgike arthe edition) buddha vākya arthavat na tu atra iti sākṣātkaraṇa abhyupāyāt asamañjasam syāt matam yuktam liṅgasya prāmāṇyam evam arthe tasya pramāṇa antarasya saṃbhavāt  saṃbhavati hi vṛṣṭi ādiṣu pramāṇa antaram tatas tad dvāra artha gatiḥ na tu sarva viśeṣa atīte brahmaṇi āmnāya eka nibandhane abhyupagamyate tatra yathā eva buddha ādi vākyānām ‘eva mayam puruṣaḥ  vedaiti jñāna niṣṭhānām atīndriya arthe jñānasya asaṃbhavāt na arthe prāmāṇyam atīndriya artha upadeśinām tathā atra api syāt  saṃbhavi pramāṇa viṣaya āpta vacana vattu liṅgasya
