pramāṇa niṣṭha tve api yujyate prāmāṇyam tad asat  brahmaṇi api sākṣātkaraṇasya abhyupagamāt avidyā saṃhāre avidyāvatām tu tad āmnāya eka nibandhanam ucyate api ca meya tvam eva sattā ced māne trividha tā kutas  tad saṃbandhāt atas  na arthe traividhyam avakalpate yadi ca liṅgena pramāṇam eva mīyate mīyamāna tā eva ca sattā tatra pramīyamāṇa tvāt pramāṇam sarvam sat eva sat ca vartamānam iti ucyate tatra vartamāna tvāt pramāṇasya sarvatra arthe ‘astiiti eva syāt  na pramāṇa traividhyāt arthe traividhyam mīyamānasya sattvāt sataḥ ca vartamāna tvāt iti api ca idamayam praṣṭavyaḥ kim vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ sattā tad viparyayaḥ asattā āhosvit  pramāṇa yoga mātram anāśrita kāla viśeṣam tatra vartamāna pramāyogaḥ sattā sat tā viparyayaḥ mate yadi tatas  prāptam asat tvam smṛti gocare na smaryamāṇasya vartamāna pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ nanu smaryamāṇe vināśa saṃbhavāt na eva ‘astiiti vyavahāraḥ satyam ‘nāstiiti api na asti yadi vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ sattā tad viparyayaḥ asattā ‘nāstiiti eva syāt  na ca ‘astiiti tasmāt anye sat asat tve pramāṇa yoga mātram ced sattā sattā viparyayaḥ prāptā pramita naṣṭena ghaṭena madhu dhāraṇā pramite ca na jijñāsā punar  syāt sada sattvayoḥ anāśrita kāla viśeṣe pramāṇa yoga mātre sattve pramita naṣṭam api vastu sat iti tena artha kriyā prasaṅge anaṣṭena iva sattva aviśeṣāt naṣṭānaṣṭayoḥ viśeṣāt na evam iti ced  sa eva tarhi viśeṣaḥ sat asat vyavahāra vyavasthāyā hetuḥ kārya vyavasthāyāḥ  iva na pramāṇa yogaḥ tad anusāriṇī eva eṣā dṛśyate loke na khalu pramita naṣṭam ‘sat aiti upacarati lokaḥ kim ca pramite arthe sat asat tve jijñāseranna punar laukikāḥ siddha tvāt pramāṇa yoga mātrasya tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca sattvasya atha pramāṇa yogya tvam sattā (ṃ= s ābh sattvam edition) naṣṭāt ca tad cyutam smaryamāṇe pracalitam kvacid iti api asundaram atha matam na vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ sattā nānā āśrita kālam tad yoga mātram api tu pramāṇam prati yogya tā sā ca naṣṭāt cyutā iti na tasya sattva prasaṅgaḥ smaryamāṇe tu kutaścid cyutā kutaścid na iti na sarvasya asattvam iti etad api na sundaram abhyupagata hānāt  tathā hi ittham artha svabhāva eva sattā varṇitā bhavati pramāṇa yogyaḥ  artha svabhāvaḥ sattā artha svabhāva nibandhana eva sat asat vyavahāra vibhāgaḥ na pramāṇa tad abhāva upādhiḥ tasya tu eṣa kathana upāyaḥ na pramāṇa saṃsparśaḥ yathā ‘nīla ākāra jñāna yogyaḥ  arthaḥ  nīlaḥ aitiākhyāte api na nīla śabdaḥ  nīla jñāna upādhiḥ tathā ca saḥ  asti śabdena abhidhīyata iti artha svabhāva niṣṭham asti artha pradhānam vākyam iti kutas  sa apekṣa tvam pramāṇasya asaṃsparśāt  syāt etad  bhinnā eva artha svabhāvāḥ pramāṇam prati yogyāḥ sat śabda vācyāḥ santu na ekā sattā mā bhūt  na etad sādhyam sarvathā artha svabhāva abhidhāyyasti śabdaḥ  na pramāṇa yoga nimitta iti pramāṇa saṃsparśe hi sa apekṣatā syāt  aneka tā tu na kañcid doṣam āvahati api ca yadi tasya aneka tvam katham abhinna śabda pravṛttiḥ tathā hi bhinneṣu abhinnam viśeṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam vā āśrityā ekaḥ śabdaḥ  varteta bhinna nimittaḥ  vā sādhāraṇa śabdaḥ syāt akṣa ādivat  tatra na tāvat ananta artha svabhāveṣu sādhāraṇa tvam upapadyate saṃbandha grahaṇa sāmarthyāt  parimita jāti viṣayā hi akṣa ādi śabdāḥ parimita upalakṣaṇa lakṣitā vā syuḥ syāt etad  dravya tva ādi sāmānya traya upalakṣitānām arthānām sat śabdaḥ sādhāraṇa iti tad na yaḥ  hi sattām avajānīte sa dravya tva ādīni api avajānīta eva na kila tejaḥ  dṛṣṭavataḥ  apsu tad avam arśaḥ  bhavati api ca sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyā api santa eva na teṣu aupacārikaḥ sat śabdaḥ pratyayasya availakṣaṇyāt  na ca sāmānyāt vinā upacāraḥ sati vā sāmānye tad eva sat śabda arthaḥ tad eva ca sattā tulya tvāt pratyayasya atha matam sarva pravādeṣu sarva padārthāḥ parimitaiḥ kaiścid dharmaiḥ upasaṃgṛhītāḥ tad upalakṣaṇānām anantānām api arthānām ‘satiti sādhāraṇaḥ śabdaḥ tad ayuktam saṃgrahaḥ  hi na ekam antareṇa tatra yadi sat śabda artha tayā (sat śabda tāyām edition) saṃgrahaḥ ‘etāvat prabhedaḥ sat śabda arthaḥ aiti na artha antara nivṛttiḥ syāt  tatra na sarva artha saṃgrahaḥ syāt  yathā ‘navavidhaḥ  gaḥ śabda arthaḥ aiti na anyeṣām abhāva eva tatra na pravādebhyaḥ kācid artha tattva avagatiḥ syāt  nanu na pravādānām arthavat tā sādhyā na brūmaḥ pravādānām arthavat tā sādhyeti kim tu pratipadyante pravādinaḥ kañcid artha svabhāvam ekam yasya ayam ‘pañca ṣaṭ aityādi prabheda saṃgrahaḥ yatas  na ekam antareṇa upasaṃgrāhakam avāntara saṃkhyānām niveśaḥ atha etāvān pramāṇa yogyaḥ  artha kriyā sāmarthyaḥ  vā iti pramāṇa yogya tve artha kriyā sāmarthye vā saṃgrahaḥ tābhyām eva sat śabda artha upalakṣyatām vyarthaḥ parimita dharma upanyāsaḥ tatra sāmānya śabda tā eva syāt  na sādhāraṇa śabda tā bhinna nimitta tve cākṣa ādi śabdebhya iva nimitta bhedāt saṃśayaḥ syāt  na viśeṣa pratītiḥ na hi ‘san ghaṭaḥiti nimitta bhedeṣu pratipattāraḥ saṃśerate yathā eva ‘śuklaḥ paṭaḥ aiti nirākāṅkṣaḥ tathā ‘san ghaṭaḥiti api yaḥ tu dravyam guṇaḥ karma rūpam vijñānam iti vā saṃśayaḥ na sa laukikānām laukikāḥ tu abhinnam eva nimittam pratipadyante arthāt ca saṃdehaḥ na śabdāt  kutas  viśeṣa pratītim antareṇa api pratipattuḥ naiḥ ākāṅkṣyāt  yatra hi artha sāmarthyena saṃśayaḥ yathā ‘vṛkṣaḥ chidyatāmiti paraśu kuṭhāra ādiṣu tatra anyatara viśeṣa an avagame api nairākāṅkṣam yasya kasyacid upādānāt anyathā anavasthānāt yatra tu śabdāt  tatra viśeṣa avagama hetoḥ vinā sa ākāṅkṣa tvam eva tad evam na nānā nimittaḥ sādhāraṇa śabdaḥ viśeṣaṇam api ekam pramāṇam syāt  tad ca prāk api tatas  sat śabda anuviddha buddhi utpādāt anupapannam iti uktam ‘mānāt eva yatas  buddhiḥiti prapañcena api ca kāryāt api vṛttam eva pramāṇam avasīyate tatra kutas tad viśiṣṭa tā na khalu arthaḥ  asat nihita viśeṣa guṇa u viśiṣṭaḥ  bhavati na ca niścite viśeṣaṇa abhāve viśiṣṭa abhidhāna anuviddhaḥ saṃśayaḥ  bhavati daṇḍa abhāva niścaya iva ‘daṇḍī na vāiti bhavati ca śūnya nagara ādiṣu cira nikhāta nidhiṣu pramāṇa abhāva niścaye api ‘santi na aiti saṃśayaḥ tasmāt anyaḥ pramāṇa yogāt sadarthaḥ yatra eṣa saṃśayaḥ na api upalakṣaṇam pramāṇam pramita dhvasteṣu sat śabdā prayogāt smaryamāṇe ca sat śabda anuviddhāt saṃdehāt vṛtta pramāṇa saṃbandhasya pramāṇa upalakṣita tvāt sattvam eva syāt  na asattvam na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ  api artha kriyayā sat śabda artham viśinaṣṭi upalakṣayati vā tasya api prāc kārya darśanāt na sat śabda yogaḥ syāt  atha pramāṇa jananam eva artha kriyām brūyāt  pramāṇāt eva asti buddhiḥ na syāt  atha vaikalpikīyam pramāṇa uttara kālatā iti matam liṅgāt na syāt  atha nirjñāta kārya saṃbandham eva liṅgena anugamyate evam tarhi prameya abhāvaḥ tathā hi kāryavat tā hi asti arthaḥ sā ca adhigatā eva kāryavat tayā eva kāryavat tā a= agamyata iti acatur asram kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca yaugapadya abhāvāt viśiṣṭa tā anupapattiḥ atha upalakṣaṇam atītasya api sattva prasaṅgaḥ smaryamāṇe ca saṃśayaḥ  na syāt iti uktam tasmāt yathā eva nīla ādi śabda arthaḥ  artha svabhāvaḥ na kārya lakṣyaḥ na pramāṇa lakṣyaḥ anavasthānāt  svarūpa vyavasthaḥ tu yathāpramāṇam avasīyate tathā sat artha svabhāvaḥ  api iti yuktam kārya pramāṇa sadasadbhāva nibandhane hi sat asat vyavahāra vibhāge tasya apravṛttiḥ eva kārya pramāṇa sadasat vyavahāra vibhāgasya api tad nibandha tva prasaṅgāt  anavasthānāt  tasmāt artha svabhāva ekā sattā iti (@svabhāva ekaḥ sattā iti edition) brahma vidaḥ  manyante atha matam na artha svabhāvaḥ  yogya tā pramāṇa hetu sadbhāvaḥ tu na ca āsatām pramāṇa hetavaḥ santi iti tad ayuktam bhūmau nikhātam nirliṅgam avedya anupapannakam naṣṭa draṣṭṛkam atyeti yad sarvam iti yogya tām bhūmau nikhātam avidyamāna indriya saṃbandham adṛśyamāna avinābhūtama saṃvedyamānānyatha anavakalpamānam vastu pralīna draṣṭṛkam yad tasya na pratyakṣa anumāna artha āpatti āgama hetavaḥ santi sādṛśya viṣayam hi upamānam tasya hetuḥ dūrā apeta eva sarva pramāṇa yogyatām atikrāmati na ca tad asat  nanu sattvam api asya katham evam api saṃśayaḥ tatra pramāṇa hetu bhāva lakṣaṇa yogya tā rūpe sattve pramāṇa hetu abhāvasya niścayāt saṃśayaḥ  na syāt  atha svabhāva viśeṣaḥ kaścid pramāṇam prati yogyaḥ sattvam prakṛta hānāt asundaram iti uktam atha vā pramāṇa viśiṣṭaḥ sat śabda artha iti etad anena nirākriyate na niścite viśeṣaṇa abhāve viśiṣṭa abhidhāyi śabda anuviddhaḥ saṃśayaḥ  yukta iti api ca abhāvasya api prameya tvāt na pramāṇa yogya tā sattā lakṣaṇam tathā hi asat prameyam ca tathā yathā eva sthāpayati ayam amitam hi tathā kasmāt tathā na punar anyathā avaśyam khalu anena sat asat vyavahāra vibhāgam icchatā asat kathañcit vyavasthāpyam anyathā vyavahāra saṃkarāt  tatra yadi pramāṇasya aviṣayaḥ yadi sarva śakti virahaḥ  vā asat buddheḥ viṣayaḥ sarvathā tathā prameyam aparicchinnam hi tathā pramāṇena kim iti tadvidham na punar anyathā syāt  na ced tasya tathā abhāve atathā abhāve vā pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ kiṃnimitta eka pakṣa anurāgaḥ api ca amitvā kaṇṭaka abhāvam caraṇam nyasyate katham na anya grahāt tasya bhāve purastāt ca prasaṅgataḥ jijñāsā na pravarteta yadi saṃvitti abhāvataḥ ‘dṛṣṭi pūtam padam nyasetiti kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi abhāve apramite katham tad nyāsaḥ tathā hi kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi artha antara bhū tala ādi paricchedāt sa syāt  kīṭa ādi aparicchedāt abhāva paricchedāt vā tatra na tāvat artha antara paricchedāt kaṇṭaka ādi bhāve api prasaṅgāt  tatra api vastu antara paricchedasya sattvāt  prāk api ca bhū bhāga paricchedāt prasajyeta yasya kasyacid vastu antarasya paricchitteḥ vidyamāna tvāt  atha kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādiparicchedāt na tad bhāva abhāva jijñāsā syāt  jijñāsā pūrvam api ( jijñāsā pūrvakāt api edition) prayatnāt tad apariccheda mātram eva prāpyate yasya abhāvaḥ  na prameyaḥ tad ca prāk api tatas  asti abhāve tu prameye abhāva niścayāya jijñāsā yujyate na ca apariccheda eva jijñāsyaḥ svatas  siddha tvāt  paricchedena hi sa nivartyate aprameya tvāt ca saḥ  api khalu abhāva iti aprameyaḥ atha matam satsu upalambha hetuṣu pramāṇa viṣayasya aparicchedāt pravṛttiḥ tad asat  pramāṇa viṣaya tvasya na upayogaḥ  atra dṛśyate asat bodhe ananya hetu bhānena hi upayujyate aparicchedāt ced pravṛttiḥ na pramāṇa viṣaya tvasya upayogaḥ itaratra api aparicchedasya tulya tvāt tatas ca pravṛtteḥ yasya svabhāvaḥ prameyaḥ tad paricchedāt pravṛttiḥ tasya ananya nimitta tvena upayogavat pramāṇa viṣaya tvam na ayam aparicchedaḥ sati eva arthe hetu vaikalya nimittaḥ samagra tvāt tad hetūnām tasmāt artha abhāvāt iti atha yatra pravṛttiḥ syāt tatra kevala saṃvidaḥ jijñāseta na sūkṣma artham kaivalyam saṃvidaḥ  yadi kevalaḥ  viṣayaḥ  na iṣṭaḥ  rūpa unmiśre api tad yatas  viśiṣṭasya ca na asti anyat anyā abhāvāt viśeṣaṇam yadi matam yatra bhū bhāga ādau caraṇa nyāsa ādi lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ tasya kevalasya sā jñānāt iti tatra api saṃpradhāryam kim idam jñānasya kaivalyam abhisaṃhitam eka viṣaya pratiniyamaḥ  viṣaya antara asaṃsargaḥ āhosvit viṣayasya yadi vijñānasya pramite api bhū bhāga ādau sthūle sūkṣma kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi bhāva abhāva parīkṣā na syāt  pravarteta eva kevala bhū talāva graha jñānāt atha viṣayasya tatra api saṃpradhāryam sva rūpeṇa vā viṣayasya kaivalyam viśeṣaṇa yogena vā tatra na tāvat svarūpeṇa miśre api tasya bhāvāt  viśeṣaṇa yogena kaivalye prāptā kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi abhāva viśiṣṭa paricchedāt pada nyāsa ādi lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ yatas  na anya abhāvāt viśeṣaṇa m anyādṛśam kiñcid dṛśyate yad viśeṣaṇam vastu kevalam syāt iti na asti iti dhī vyavahṛtī viṣayam kam upāśrite māna abhāvam yadi kṣuṇṇam meyā bhāvasya tatra kim api ca anena ‘nāsti aiti buddhi śabdayoḥ viṣayaḥ  vācyaḥ sa na vastu svarūpeṇa miśre api prasaṅgāt  na kevalam abhāvāt anyasya viśeṣaṇasya abhāvāt iti uktam nanu ‘nāsti aiti ayam arthaḥ ‘nedam pramīyateiti na punar abhāvaḥ  avagamyate viruddham idam na asti avagamyate ca iti yadi evam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ  viṣaya uktaḥ syāt  ‘nāstiiti dhī śabdayoḥ tatra kaḥ  aparādhaḥ syāt prameya abhāvasya yena tam ati laṅghya pramāṇa abhāvaḥ  viṣaya ucyate na hi tayoḥ nirupākhya tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ atha matam agrahe asat graha bhrāntiḥ abhāva vyavahṛt bhramaḥ abhāve ca vyavahṛteḥ adṛṣṭau dhvānta dṛṣṭivat  na eva stām ‘nāstiiti buddhi vyavahārau katham imau sarva janānām pratītau= apahnūyete ucyate bhramaḥ  ayam sat buddhi abhāve tad viparyaya pariccheda iti tathā sat vyavahāra abhāve tad viparyaya vyavahāra bhramaḥ yathā loka darśana abhāve ‘tamaḥ paśyāmi aiti vibhramaḥ na hi tamaḥ  nāma kiñcid dṛśyam asti na etad sāram ittham bhavet suṣupta ādau trailokya abhāva dṛś bhramaḥ aparicchindataḥ kiñcid vibhramaḥ ca na yujyate āropaviṣaya āropye na ajānan rajata bhramī na abhāva bhinnā vyavahṛt ta dabhāvaḥ ca dhīpade tamaḥ dṛṣṭiḥ tu bhūt chāyām āloka abhāvam eva vā ālambate na tu adṛṣṭa āviṣṭaḥ  darśana vibhramaḥ yadi khalva darśane viparyaya darśana bhramaḥ  bhavati suṣupta ādi avasthāsu viśva abhāva darśana bhramaḥ syāt āloka adarśana bhramavat na ca kiñcid aparicchindataḥ vibhramaḥ tathā hi āropasya viṣayam puras varti vastu āropaṇīyam ca rajatam jñānena anāpnuvan na rajata bhramavān bhavati anyathāpratipattiḥ smṛtiḥ sāmānya pratipattiḥ vā na ca buddhi abhāvaḥ  jñānasya viṣayaḥ  na vyavahāra abhāvaḥ nābhauva buddhiḥ na abhāva vyavahāraḥ viśeṣaṇasya abhāvasya jñāna aviṣaya tvāt tatra ubhayoḥ viṣaya āropaṇīyayoḥ agrahaṇe na mithyājñānam iti abhyupagamya pramāṇa yogya tām sattām doṣa abhāva ucyate astu vā māna yogya tvam sattvam tad ca pramīyatām tasmin mite vastu sattvam bhavati āgama gocare na ca sa apekṣatā na asmin= antara artha vibhinna tām pracakṣate ye api sattām anyām na pratijānate bhavatu vā pramāṇa yogya tā sattā sā eva ca prameyāḥ tu tad prameyam vastu sattvam āgama arthaḥ na ca pramāṇa antara apekṣa tā doṣaḥ pramāṇa antara saṃbhedasya abhāvāt  ‘pramāṇa yogyaḥ aiti etāvat mātra adhigateḥ tathā hi ye api pramāṇa yogya tām sattām āhuḥ na tad vyatirekiṇīm te api na atra antara artha saṃsparśam icchanti tad saṃsparśe hi anyat pramāṇam anveṣyam syāt  katham na anveṣyam yadā vacaḥ pramāṇa yogya tāyām paryavasitam na viśiṣṭa artha sattvam bodhayati tatra yasya pramāṇasya yogyaḥ  viśiṣṭaḥ  arthaḥ tad avaśya apekṣaṇīyam kimartham tad apekṣyate viśiṣṭa vastu sattva adhigamāya kam punar viśiṣṭasya vastunaḥ sattvam pramāṇa yogya tvam adhigatam eva tarhi tad asti artha niṣṭhāt vacanāt  pramāṇa yogya tāyā asti artha tvāt pramāṇa antara saṃbheda abhyupagame api na aprāmāṇya prasaṅga doṣa iti darśayati pramāṇa antara bhinna artham api mānam na naḥ vacaḥ nirapekṣam iha arthe tu pramitam vastu idam mayā artha mātre ca sa apekṣam anya apekṣā artha bodhanāt abādhitam api tu arthe pramāṇa aṃśe apabādhanāt  tatra apramāṇa tām eti buddhān āpta vacaḥ  yathā na khalu pramāṇa antara saṃbhinna artham api vacaḥ  na pramāṇam pramāṇam eva hi āpta vākyam katham punar  pramāṇam sa apekṣam iti ced  ucyate nirapekṣam eva tad  ‘pramitaḥ  ayam mayā arthaḥ aiti asmin= arthe kevale hi arthe ‘evam ayam arthaḥ aitya pratīteḥ ‘eva mayam puruṣaḥ  veda aiti ca pratīteḥ puruṣa jñāna apekṣam tatra upalabdhau tāvat anapekṣa tvāt prāmāṇyam aśnute tad siddhi dvāraḥ ca paścāt artha iti katham tarhi puruṣa vacaḥ kiñcid abādhita artham api sa apekṣa tvena apramāṇam kathyate ucyate yadi api arthe bādhaḥ  na asti yad apekṣam tu asya arthe prāmāṇyam yad siddhi mukhena tam sādhayati tatra pramāṇa aṃśe bādhyate tasya asiddheḥ tad dvāreṇa na artha siddhiḥ iti arthe apramāṇam yathā atīndriya arthe buddha vacaḥ puruṣasya darśana asaṃbhavāt yathā uktam ‘puruṣa aśaktitaḥ tatra sa apavāda tva saṃbhavaḥiti yathā ca vipralambhaka vākyam ayathā dṛṣṭa artha vādi tvasya pramāṇa avagata tvāt āpta vākyam punar na arthe na māna aṃśe apabādhitam nirapekṣam pramāṇa aṃśe vyavahāraḥ  anyathā katham āpta vacaḥ punar na arthe na api pramāṇa aṃśe saṃbhavat pramāṇa gocaram bādhyate pramāṇa aṃśe ca anapekṣam tad mukhena ca artha siddhim vidadhanna apramāṇam bhavitum arhati anyathā śabda nibandhanaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  na syāt  mayā iti vaktra bhāvena saṃbheda rahitam tatas  pralīna jñāna vijñeya vibhāgam sva ātma vedanam pravedayantu vedāntā māna antaram alaukikam tad siddhi siddha tā arthasya puṃvacaḥvat bhaviṣyati evam ca pramāṇa antara saṃbhinna artha tve api vedānta vacasām na prāmāṇya vyāhatiḥ āpta vākyavat  tathā hi tāni api jñāna jñeya vibhāga vikalam sva prakāśa rūpam alaukikam kāmam avagamayantu pramāṇa antaram tad dvārā ca artha siddhiḥ āpta vacanavat iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ syāt  vede vaktuḥ abhāvāt  ‘mayā aiti saṃsparśaḥ  na syāt  abhyupagama vādam parisamāpya prakṛtam upasaṃharati evam na meya tā sattā paraḥ punar  pratyavatiṣṭhate nanu anyā api na yujyate na hi pūrva avamarśena vinā sāmānya kalpanā gām ekām īkṣitavataḥ  jāyate anyatra yādṛśaḥ avamarśaḥ  dṛṣṭa sataḥ tathā na hi sat antare eka śabda pravṛttiḥ tu daṇḍya ādivat upeya tām dṛṣṭa rūpa avamarśaḥ sāmānya kalpanāyām pramāṇam yathā bāhuleyam dṛṣṭavataḥ śābaleye ‘sa eva ayamiti na ca kiñcid sat gṛhītavataḥ  anyatra sa bhavati eka śabda pravṛttiḥ tu vinā api sāmānyena artha antara yoga nimittā daṇḍi pācaka ādi śabdavat atra ucyate kaḥ  nu pūrva avamarśaḥ  ayam pūrvarūpa anvayaḥ  dhiyaḥ sat antare api saḥ  asti eva kayācid khalu mātrayā sarva ātmanā tu anugamaḥ  na dṛṣṭaḥ khaṇḍa muṇḍayoḥ na tādṛśaḥ ced naḥ bheda mātrāt vedyaḥ sva pahnavaḥ na bheda mātrāt mṛd jāti hīnam maṇikamallakam rūpa anvayaḥ pratyayasya maṇikeṣu hi yādṛśaḥ na dṛṣṭa mallakasya asti maṇike khalu tādṛśaḥ kaḥ punar ayam pūrva avamarśaḥ pūrvarūpa avabhāsaḥ  buddheḥ atha ‘saḥ  ayamiti pūva arparānu sandhānam tatra yadi pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ saḥ  asti eva sat antare mātrayā tathā hi nirupākhya vailakṣaṇyena satām tulya rūpa tā prakāśate anyathā nirupākhya vatsantaḥ  api atyanta vilakṣaṇāḥ prakāśeran atha sarva rūpa anugamaḥ saḥ  abhiprete api sāmānya gocare na asti na hi khaṇḍa muṇḍayoḥ sarva ātmanā anvayaḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt sāmānya abhāva āpatteḥ atha na tādṛśaḥ  yādṛśaḥ khaṇḍa ādiṣu tad asat  na viśeṣa mātreṇa saṃvedyān vayi rūpa pratyākhyānam yujyate gaḥ tva ādeḥ api tad saṃbhavāt na hi devadattasya dvitīya darśane yādṛśaḥ  rūpa anugamaḥ tādṛśaḥ khaṇḍam dṛṣṭavataḥ  muṇḍa darśane sāmānya gocare api ca na sarvatra tulyaḥ nānā maṇika vilakṣaṇaḥ  hi maṇika śara ābayaḥ  rūpa anvayaḥ na ca tāvatā mṛd jāti hīna tā tayoḥ kiñcid tulya tayā avabhāsamāna tvāt  atha dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ atra ucyate pūrva avamarśaḥ sa iti prakhyā iti api na śobhate maṇikam vīkṣitavataḥ saḥ  api na udeti mallake pūrva apara anusandhāna ātmikā ‘saḥ  ayam aitya bhedam avagamayantī bhinneṣu api sāmānya kalpanā hetuḥ buddhiḥ pūrva avamarśa iti ucyata iti etad api na śobhate yatas  na anusandhānāt eva abheda siddhiḥ abhinna rūpa avabhāsāt api anyathā na abhinna deśa kāla ekaḥ  arthaḥ syāt  na hi tatra deśa kāla bheda abhāve ‘saḥiti anusandhānam api ca dṛṣṭa maṇikasya mallake na bhavati drāk iva ‘saḥ aiti anusandhānam khaṇḍa muṇḍavat  na ca evam mṛd jāti hīna tā vimṛśataḥ tu ‘tad jātīyam idam aiti buddhiḥ sat antare api samānā tulye tarhi sāmānya yoge kasmāt kvacid  ‘saḥ aitivamarśaḥ na anyatra ucyate sāmānya rūpa bhūyastve tasmāt tattvam prakāśate vilakṣaṇa tvam alpa tve cakāsti tad anudbhavāt yasmāt satī api sāmānya yoge maṇi śara ābayoḥ na ‘saḥ aiti prakhyā maṇikā antare ca bhavati bhūyiṣṭha sāmānya yukte tasmāt sāmānya rūpāṇām bhūyiṣṭhatvena udbhavāt  ‘saḥiti tattva prakhyā alpa tve tu na tathā teṣām anudbhavāt  na ca daṇḍya ādivat eka śabda pravṛttiḥ iti āha pramāṇam kārya vijñeyam asaṃyojya asti dhīryataḥ prathamam jāyate tasmāt na daṇḍya ādi samāna tā na agṛhīta viśeṣaṇā viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ na ca viśiṣṭa buddheḥ prāk  (sat buddheḥ prāk  edition) pramāṇa grahaṇam tad kālam vā tathā hi pramāṇāt eva sā bhavati pramāṇam ca pramiti kārya unneya tvāt paścāt sat pratipatteḥ gṛhyate tasmāt agrahāt pramāṇasya tad saṃyojana vikalā sā na pramāṇa yoga nimittā yadi tarhi na pramāṇa yogaḥ  asti arthaḥ katham tad kāla anuvidhāyinī kāla pravṛttiḥ asti arthe ‘kūpaḥ  asti‘kūpaḥ  abhūt‘kūpaḥ  bhaviṣyatiiti tad upādhi prakalpita bheda tvāt  devadatta sattāyā iva pāṭaliputra saṃyoga upādhi kalpita bhedāyāḥ  iti na ca ‘kriyām antareṇa na saṃsargaḥ padārthānāmiti śabda artha naya vidāma vigānam iti āha saṃbandha mātra a= asitam api ca anye vipaścitaḥ āhuḥ vacaḥ  akriya mayam rājñaḥ  nā phalinaḥ  drumāḥ ‘rājñaḥ  ayam puruṣaḥ aphalitā ete vanaspatayaḥ aiti kriyā rahiteṣu api saṃsargaḥ pratīyate na ca iha api ‘asti kriyāiti yujyate yatas  na nirjñāta rāja saṃbandhasya puruṣasya phalavatām ca vanaspatīnām satta iha pratipādyā gamyate na hi ete vākye sattāyām paryavasyataḥ kim tu puruṣasya rāja saṃbandhe drumāṇā ca phala saṃbandhe ‘yaḥ  ayam puruṣaḥ sa rājñaḥ‘ya ete vanaspatayaḥ te phalitāḥna ‘yaḥ  rāja puruṣaḥ saḥ  asti‘ye ca phalitāḥ te santiiti yad api kecid  ‘avadhāryatāmiti pratipatti kriyā vidhinā kriyāvat tām manyate tad api śabdāt eva pratipatteḥ siddha tvāt prāṅ nirastam eva iti atha api na kriyā rahitam vākyam asti kriyāyām ca sa apekṣatā tathā api na doṣa iti āha jani kriyā avasānāt ca viśiṣṭam śakya bodhanam kāraṇam jāyata idam īdṛkṣāt kāraṇāt iti ‘īdṛkṣāt kāraṇāt jagat jāyateiti jani kriyā niṣṭhāt api vākyāt tadvidha kāraṇa sattā śakyate pratipattum yathā ‘īdṛśāt taroḥ idam phalam ajaniiti tadvidha taru sadbhāvaḥ tathā ca śrutayaḥ kāścid evam eva brahma pratipādayanti ‘sarvāṇi ha vā imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante‘yathā agneḥ kṣudrā viṣphuliṅgā vyuccaranti evam eva asmāt ātmanaḥ sarve devāḥityādi tathā yathā ūrṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ca yathā pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavanti yathā sataḥ puruṣāt keśa lomāni tathā akṣarāt saṃbhavati iha viśvamtad etad satyam ayathā su dīptāt pāvakāt viṣphuliṅgāḥ sahasraśas  saṃbhavante sarūpāḥ tathā akṣarāt vividhāḥ somya bhāvāḥ prajāyante tatra ca eva apiyantitathā adivyaḥ  hi amūrtaḥ puruṣaḥ sa bāhya abhantaraḥ  hi ajaḥ aprāṇaḥ  hyamanāḥ śubhraḥ  akṣarāt paratas  paraḥ etasmāt jāyate prāṇaḥ  manaḥ sarva indriyāṇi ca kham vāyuḥ jyotirāpaḥ pṛthivī viśvasya dhāriṇiiti idānīm padārtha saṃsargāya eva vidhiḥ āśrayitavya iti pratyavatiṣṭhate nanu pramā antara adhīna saṃsargāḥ puruṣoktiṣu padārthā vidhi adhīna ātma saṃśleṣā itaratra tu padānām racanā tatra vivakṣā paripūrtaye pramāṇa antara gamye arthe vivakṣā ca vyavasthitā vidhi artha siddhaye vede tad abhāve tu asaṃgateḥ viśiṣṭa artha gatiḥ bhrāntiḥ agrahe graha vibhramaḥ vivakṣita artha niṣpattaye hi loke padānām samabhivyāhāraḥ na ekapadsādhyaḥ  vivakṣita arthaḥ pramāṇa antara upalabdhaḥ ca vivakṣā viṣayaḥ tena tatra pramāṇa antara āyattaḥ saṃsargaḥ tathā ca tad virodhe asaṃsarga eva padārthānām ‘jaradgavaḥ pāduka kambalābhyāmiti vede tu pramāṇa antara abhāvāt vidhi nibandhanaḥ  asau tad abhāve tu asaṃbhava ādyeyam viśiṣṭa artha gatiḥ ucyate sā bhrāntiḥ samabhivyāhārāt  saḥ  ayam viveka agrahe saṃsarga graha vibhramaḥ atra idam eva vicāryam katham loke pramāṇa antara adhīnaḥ saṃsargaḥ iti yadi pramāṇa antareṇa tad avagamāt tad asat  apūrvasya api tasya pratīteḥ anyathā vacana vaiyarthyāt  anadhigatam hi śrotuḥ artham bodhayitum vacaḥ prayujyate atha saṃsarga yogya tā mātrasya pramāṇa antareṇa avagamāt samānam etad vede tathā hi aruṇayā krīṇāti iti saṃsargaḥ na aruṇayā eka hāyanyā iti tathā bhāva arthaḥ  niyoga viṣayaḥ na dravya guṇa śabda artha iti pramāṇa antara avasita yogya tā sāmarthyena eva vyasthāpyate atha na vivakṣa eka padau= agamyā tad artha mātra vivakṣāyāḥ  niṣprayojana tvāt  tasmāt vivakṣā viśeṣa siddhiḥ na asaṃsṛṣṭeṣu padārtheṣu bhavati iti tathā vivakṣayā prayuktāḥ saṃsṛjyante sā ca pramāṇa antara siddha  iti evam api vivakṣā nibandhanaḥ syāt  tad prayuktānām saṃsargāt  na pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ yatas  na tad tasya pratipādakam na prayojakam vā yad tu pramāṇa antara siddhe vivakṣā iti bhavatu na tu tasya saṃsarga upayogaḥ tathā hi (na tasya saṃsarga upayogaḥ tathā ca edition) vipralambhaka vākye api saṃsarga pratītiḥ yad tu virodhe na saṃsargaḥ kāmam na tu tatas  saṃsargaḥ virodhe api tu na asaṃsargaḥ pratīteḥ pratītaḥ  api tu bādhyate pramāṇa antareṇa evam ca anṛtam kiñcid vacaḥ kiñcid anarthakam daśa dāḍima ādi kiñcid satyam anyathā anṛta anarthaka vibhāgaḥ  na syāt  atha pramāṇa antareṇa upalabhya artham vivakṣitvā parasmai pratipādayati puruṣaḥ tena tad vacasaḥ pramāṇa antara upalabdhiḥ eva arthaḥ sā eva prayojikā padārtha saṃsargasya tasyāḥ prayojikāyāḥ  abhāvāt na vede padārtha saṃsarga siddhiḥ mā bhūt sā viśiṣṭa artha eva prayojakaḥ atha lokau= agamya tvāt śabda sāmarthyasya laukika prayojaka abhāvāt na saṃsargaḥ vidhimat tve api na syāt  atha loke saṃsarga mātra paratve arthāpattiḥ na tad viśeṣe tanmātreṇa pratīti prayogayoḥ upapatteḥ vinā api pramāṇa antara upalabdhyā viśiṣṭa artha gati siddhiḥ atha pramāṇa antarāt loke saṃsarga satyatā avagamaḥ apūrva u api hi śrotuḥ saṃsargaḥ  vaktuḥ pramāṇa anumāna mukhena satyatām labhate tad asaṃbhave asatya tvāt buddha ādi vākyeṣu tena pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ  loke saṃsarga ucyate bhavatu vede tu pramāṇa antara saṃbheda abhāvāt svātantryeṇa artha pratīteḥ śabda nibandhana eva tadā astām etad  bhavatu yathā loke idam tu paryanuyujyate katham nu vidhi adhīna tvam yadi syāt anyathā vṛthā vidhiḥ nirviṣayaḥ tulyam idam anya pada udite viśiṣṭa artha avagatya anya padārthaḥ  api prayujyate arthavat tve pramābhau= ādaḥ tu asau ced anarthakaḥ vidhiḥ na evam kasya hetoḥ atha syāt aparam padam pramāṇa antara siddhe arthe prayogi na vidhāyakam tad arthaḥ  ananya gamyaḥ  hi mīyamānaḥ samākṣipet  viṣayam na yathā siddha padārthaḥ tu anuvāda bhāj  avyutpanna pravṛttiḥ syāt saṃbandha jñāna nihnave padam svadharmam vyutkrāmet anya siddhārtha tā anyathā na tāvat vidhiḥ sākṣāt saṃsarga sāmānyam tad viśeṣam vā bodhayati atha ākṣipati anyathā niyoga mātram nirviṣayam anarthakam syāt  padārtha antareṣu api tulyam etad  te api kevalāḥ padārtha antara saṃsargam anāpnuvantaḥ  apūrva artha pratipatteḥ abhāvāt anarthakāḥ na ca loke padaiḥ sva arthāḥ sva rūpa mātra niṣṭhatayā eva pratyyante kim tu viśiṣṭa artha pratyaya prayuktāḥ tathā vyavahāra upapatteḥ tathā ca pratipadārtham saṃsarga ākṣepaḥ syāt etad  loke buddhi pūrva prayuktānām mā bhūt ānarthakyam iti saṃsarga artha tā vede tu na arthavat tve pramāṇam asti atas  padārtha antaram anarthakam eva astu na etad sāram na anyathā anarthakyam iti apramāṇaḥ  arthaḥ śakyaḥ pratipattum yasya kasyacid pratipatti prasaṅgāt  tasmāt vyavahārāt saṃsarga prayukta sva artha avabodha sāmarthyam eva padānām gamyate tatas  vede api saṃsarga ākṣepaḥ yadica anya padārthānām ānarthakyam vidhi arthasya tad na kasmāt  ātha matam pada antarāṇi pramāṇa antara siddhe arthe prayujyante tāni yathā avagata artha anuvāda paryavasitāni tathā hi anūdyamānaḥ  arthaḥ  yathā avagamam anuvāda at na apūrva artha ākṣepāya alam vidhāyakaḥ tu śabdaḥ  ananya gamya artha viṣayaḥ tad arthaḥ pramīyamāṇaḥ śaknoti apūrvam artham ākṣeptum anyathā anava kalpamānaḥ tasmāt vede vidhi nibandhanaḥ  apūrva saṃsarga iti tad ayuktam pramāṇa antara aviṣayaḥ ced vidhāyaka arthaḥ tatra saṃbandha jñānam aśakyam iti nihnūyeta tathā ca saṃbandha jñāna anapekṣa tvāt avyutpannaḥ  api pravarteta saṃbandha jñāna apekṣa tā ca pada dharmaḥ  vyutkramyeta tad nirapekṣa tā vākya dharma āśrīyeta atha saṃbandha apekṣatā na asya nihnūyeta balāt pramāṇa antara siddhārtha tā āpadyeta tathā ca na viśeṣaḥ śabdāt eva mite yaḥ  api manyate saṃgati graham na anyonya saṃśraya avadyam na svayam pramite hi saḥ pareṇa śabda avagate tad pravṛttyā ca sūcite padārtha antaravat tatra sukaraḥ saṃgati grahaḥ yaḥ  api manyate na pramāṇa antara siddhe viddhi arthe saṃbandha jñānam api tu śabda siddha  eva na ca anyonya saṃśraya doṣaḥ śabdāt siddhe saṃbandha jñānam saṃbandha jñāna pūrvikā ca śabdāt siddhiḥ iti yatas  na svayam śabdāt pramite tad ucyate kim tu vṛddha prayuktāt vṛddha antareṇa avagateḥ tad avagamāt ca tasya vṛddhasya yā pravṛttiḥ tayā anumite ‘nūnam anena vṛddhena pratipannaḥ kaścid pravṛtti hetuḥ arthaḥ  asmāt śabdāt  yena ayam etad śravaṇāt pravṛttaḥiti yathā ‘gāma anayaiti sāsnādi mada ānayana darśanāt tad pratyayam anumāya tatra saṃbandha grahaṇam iti tasya evam anumeya tve katham śabda eka gocaraḥ tasya api śabda pūrva tvāt anumāna eka gocaraḥ kasmāt na śabda bodhaḥ  api hi anumāna purassaraḥ na idaṃprathama tā labhyā bīja aṅkuravat etayoḥ śabdāt boddhuḥ ca anumānam sarvasya eva puras  sthitam padārtha antaravat tena tasya śabda unuvādakaḥ anumānāt budhyamānaḥ śabdāt buddham na budhyate pratipad tṛ antere bodhaḥ  na anya bodha anuvāda kṛt pravṛtti hetu mātram ca śabda arthaḥ syāt alaukikaḥ na sa kalpayitum śakyaḥ tad siddheḥ laukikāt api yadi pravṛtti unnīyamāna pratyaya viśeṣaṇa tvena vyavasthitaḥ  anumeyaḥ  vidhāyaka arthaḥ saṃbandha jñāna viṣayaḥ na tarhi śabda eka pramāṇakaḥ atha anumānam śabda pūrvakam iti tathā ucyate śābdaḥ  api pratyayaḥ anumāna pūrvaka iti anumāna eka gocaraḥ syāt  na khalu bīja aṅkurayoḥ iva ānayoḥ ekasya prāthamyam vyavasthāpayitum śakyam śabda avagatasya anumānāt  anumitasya vidita saṃgateḥ śabdāt avagamāt  api ca sarva pratipattṝṇām anumāna pūrvā śabdāt pratipattiḥ iti teṣām śabdaḥ  anuvādaka eva tathā hi śabdāt buddhyamānaḥ  anumitam vidita saṃgatim budhyate sarva pratipattā na tu anumimānaḥ śabda avagatam anumimīte nanu śabda avagata eva anumīyate satyam anena tu pratipattrā na ca anyadīyā pratipattiḥ anya pratipattim anuvādīkaroti pravṛtti hetu mātre ca saṃbandha vyutpatteḥ tanmātram śabda arthaḥ syāt  na ca ālaukikaḥ kalpayitum api śakyaḥ laukikāt api pravṛtti siddheḥ syāt etad  vaidikīṣu pravṛttiṣu tad asaṃbhavāt alaukika kalpanā na etad  loka avagata sāmarthyaḥ  hi śabdaḥ  vede api pratipādakaḥ tatra laukikīṣu pravṛttiṣu laukike vidita saṃbandhe vede api tad pratipattiḥ eva syāt  asaṃbhave vā mithyātvam atha bahuvidha tvāt pravṛtti hetūnām vyabhicārāt aśabda artha tve pravṛtti hetu sāmānyam śabda arthaḥ tatra vede laukikānām viśeṣaṇānām asaṃbhavāt alaukikam viśeṣa antaram pratīyate evam api yaḥ śabda arthaḥ  vede sāmānyam sa loka siddha iti na anuvāda tā vyāvartate padārtha antaravat yaḥ  api viśeṣaḥ saḥ  anya asaṃbhavena pariśeṣa anumāna gocara iti na pramāṇa antara aviṣaya tvam na ca pariśeṣa anumānam api śreyaḥ sādhana tāyāḥ saṃbhavāt  atha matam loka vyavahāra iva veda vyavahāraḥ  api anādiḥ tatra vaidikīṣu pravṛttiṣu laukika pravṛtti hetu abhāvāt alaukike tu pravṛtti hetau vaidikānām vidhāyakānām saṃbandha jñānam na ca anumeya tvam tad pratyayasya pravṛttyā anumānāt  tad siddhiḥ tu tad pratyaya sāmarthyena eva sa ca pratyayaḥ śabda uttha iti ananya pramāṇa tā na ca laukikasya eva śreyaḥ sādhana tvasya saṃbhava iti yuktam laukikī hi pramāṇa antarau= agamyā śreyaḥ sādhana tā tatra prayoga darśanāt liṅā ādeḥ tad anusāreṇa ca śabda artha avadhāraṇāt pramāṇa antara gamya tā api śabda artha anupraveśinī atra ucyate bhavatu nāma veda vyavahārāt eva śabda artha anugamaḥ tathā api na pramāṇa antara gocara tā vyāvartate tathā hi alaukike pravṛtti hetau śabdasya sāmarthya jñāna kāle pramitaḥ  vā syāt  na vā pramitaḥ ced  śabda saṃbandhasya tadā eva jñāyamāna tvāt avaśyam pramāṇa antareṇa iti vācyam atha na pramitaḥ katham tatra saṃbandha jñānam na hi apramitayoḥ saṃbandhinoḥ tad āśrayaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pramātum śakyaḥ yaḥ  api manyate śaktiḥ hi śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ sā ca na arthe tasya vyavasthita tvāt  pratyayaḥ tu tasya kāryaḥ sa ca pravṛttyā anumitaḥ tatra eva sāmarthya lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pramīyata iti sa idam praṣṭavyaḥ kim pratyaya mātre sāmarthyam gṛhyate atha viśiṣṭe pravṛtti hetu pratyaye yadi pratyaya mātre yad kiñcittatas  pratīyeta atha viśiṣṭe laukika vyatirikta pravṛtti hetu pratyaye pravṛtti pariśeṣābhyām tasya anumita tvāt prāptam pramāṇa antara gocara tvam dvayī hi viśeṣaṇasya gatiḥ smārta ākṛṣṭam viśiṣṭa pramitau= aṅga tvam eti yathā agnimān dhūmāt iti viśiṣṭa grāhi pramāṇa prameyam vā yathā śuklaḥ  gauḥ iti ubhayathā ca pramāṇa antara viṣayaḥ śabdasya anadhigata saṃbandha tvāt smārta ākṛṣṭa tve pramāṇa antaram anveṣyam dvitīye api kalpe viśiṣṭa pratyaya anumāna anumita tvāt  atha anumānasya pratyaya eva prāmāṇyam pratīti mātram tu tatra viśeṣaṇasya tāvatā ca tad viśiṣṭa prati iti aṅgam viśeṣaṇa pramitiḥ tu anumitāt pratyayāt  yathā puruṣa vacanāt viśiṣṭa artha pramāṇe anumite artha siddhiḥ tata eva pramāṇāt  tatra hi arthaḥ pratīti mātreṇa eva vaktṛ jñānasya viśeṣaṇam tad etad apeśalam smṛti pramāṇa saṃśaya viparyāsa vikalpa antargamāt pratīteḥ tatra alaukika viśeṣaṇa pratītiḥ na smṛtiḥ prāc anadhigateḥ na saṃśayaḥ koṭi dvaya saṃsparśa abhāvāt na vikalpaḥ pravṛtti hetu pratyayasya api tathā prasaṅgāt  tathā na viparyāsaḥ katham hi tatra yathārtha tve tathābhūta grāhiṇī tad pratītiḥ artha śūnyā syāt  pariśeṣāt pramāṇam para jñānena ca paraḥ pratipadyata iti subhāṣitam atha matam na para jñānena paraḥ pratipadyate kim tu sva jñānena eva para jñāna sāmarthyāt  atha tasya sva jñānam katamat pramāṇam iti vācyam na tāvat śābdam śabda vijñānāt arthe vijñānam iti lakṣaṇāt  na ca tad śabda jñānāt  kutas tarhi śabda uttha jñānāt anumitāt  atha tasya prāmāṇye pravṛtti hetu sadbhāva siddhiḥ prāmāṇyam ca tasya doṣa rahita śabda udbhavāt  tena śabdasya tatra prāmāṇyam ucyate tad adhīnaḥ tatra artha niścaya iti tad api asāṃpratam śabdāt artha jñānam śābdam iti lakṣaṇāt  puruṣa vacanam api na arthe na pramāṇam kim tu jñāna viśeṣaṇe dvayī ca viśeṣaṇasya gatiḥ uktā tatra smṛti asaṃbhavāt pramīyamāṇa  eva sa viśiṣṭa artha pramiti aṅgam anyathā arthe pramāṇa antaram anveṣyam syāt  na ca vaktṛ jñānena eva artha siddhiḥ para jñānena na paraḥ pratipadyata iti uktam yad tu uktam vaktṛ jñāna adhīna artha siddhiḥ iti tad tad mithyā tve tad asaṃbhave vā pramāṇa pratīti bādhane artha pratīteḥ api bādhanāt tad abādhe ca ābādhāt  na tu vacasaḥ  arthaḥ  na viṣayaḥ anyathā pramāṇa antara paratantram puruṣa vacaḥ  arthe sa apekṣam iti etad eva na syāt  na hi yaḥ  yasya aviṣayaḥ sa tatra sa apekṣaḥ  anapekṣaḥ  vā tathā ca ‘prāmāṇya sthāpanam tu syāt vaktṛ dhīhetu saṃbhavātiti uktam sthāpanam abādhaḥ na tu prāmāṇyam eva tad ca vaktṛ dhī hetu saṃbhavāt vākyasya na tu vaktṛdhiya eva śabdasya ca arthena saṃbandhaḥ na tu jñānena evam hi uktam ‘autpattikaḥ tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥiti artha grahaṇam atra ‘arthā saṃspaśī śabdaḥ jñānena eva śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ iti paśyatām nirākaraṇāya tasmāt anyonya yogya tā śabda arthayoḥ eva saṃbandhaḥ na ca apramite arthe sa śakyaḥ  grahītum pramite pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvam uktam na ca pratīti mātre arthavatyāḥ pratīteḥ smṛti pramāṇayoḥ anyataratra antargamāt ānarthakye kena saṃbandha yadi ca śābda pratīti vyatirekiṇyā api pratītyai  sa viṣayīkriyate apramāṇa ātmikayā api bhavati ayam aśābdasya api jñānasya gocara iti pramāṇa antara āśaṅkā kena vāryate na ca pramāṇa antara avagamyatā śabda artham anupraviśati yatas  na anvaya mātreṇa vyatireka mātreṇa vā śabda arthaḥ sati hi anyasmin prayojake arthe yasya abhāve na prayogaḥ saḥ  api tasya śabdasya prayojaka iti gamyate yathā satsu hetu antareṣu yasya abhāve na kāryam saḥ  api hetuḥ gamyate iha ca śreyaḥ hetu vivakṣāyām liṅga ādeḥ darśanāt  tad abhāve sati api pramāṇa antara gamya tve adarśanāt śreyaḥ hetu tvam tāvat śabda arthaḥ pramāṇa antara gamya tve yadi api darśanam tad abhāve ca yadi api adarśanam na tu śreyaḥ hetu tve sati pramāṇa antara gamya tāyāḥ  abhāvāt  tatra saṃdigdhaḥ  vyatirekaḥ ubhaya abhāve aprayogāt  kiṃnibandhanaḥ  aprayoga iti tatra śreyaḥ sādhana tāyāḥ prayojaka tvasya avadhārita tvāt tad abhāve tad nibandhana iti gamyate tanmātreṇa anvaya vyatireka upapattau na anyasya śabda artha tve pramāṇam anyathā śiṃśapā śabda arthe sattva āt ayaḥ  api anupraviśeyuḥ teṣu satsu prayogāt tad abhāve ca aprayogāt  atha śiṃśapātu asya śabda artha tvāt tad abhāva nibandhana eva sattā ādya bhāve aprayogaḥ tad sadbhāvāt ca prayoga upapadyata iti na teṣu sāmarthya kalpanā samānam etad atra api atha śreyaḥ hetutvasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt tasya ca vede asaṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam tad asat  na hi ya ekatra yasya pramāṇasya gocaraḥ saḥ  anyatra api mithyā samīpe hi bahis indriya viṣayaḥ dūre tu āgama anumāna gamyaḥ tathā yāga ādiṣu viprakṛṣṭa kāla phaleṣu vedau= agamyam śreyaḥ sādhana tvam bhaviṣyati na ca pramāṇa antara anupalabdhyā pramāṇa antara gamyaḥ  bādhyate viṣaya vyavasthayā api pramāṇa pravṛtteḥ atha pramāṇa antara viṣaya tve tad virodhāt aprāmāṇyam anantara phala anupalabdheḥ tad aviṣaye tu śabda arthe na tad virodha iti syāt  yadi virodhaḥ syāt  na ca asau ‘a ānantaryam hi acoditamiti uktam atha mā bhūdānantarya codanā mā ca bhūt pramāṇa antara avagamyatā śabda arthaḥ sarvathā pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ ced padārtha āśrīyate sa yathā siddhi āśrayaṇīyaḥ anyathā na tad siddhaḥ syāt  anantara śreyaḥ hetutā ca tad siddhā tad na na tāvat anantara phala sādhana tā niyogataḥ karmaṇām kṛṣi auṣadha pāna ādiṣu anyathā api darśanāt  avāntara kāryasya yāga ādau= api pramāṇa sāmarthyena siddheḥ api ca viśiṣṭa siddhau viśeṣaṇam api śreyaḥ hetutva mātram siddham tāvat ca śabda arthaḥ na ca tāvati pramāṇa virodhaḥ tad evam laukike api pravṛtti hetau doṣa abhāvāt vyarthā alaukika kalpanā sukha ādivat ca asya anumeya tvāt tathā hi mukha prasāda ādi unneya saṃvedanāḥ sukha ādayaḥ tena eva sahonnīyante na evam sattve pṛthak pramāṇam arthyate yadā api idam darśanam vaktṛ jñānam eva puruṣa vacana arthaḥ tatra jñānam na artham antareṇa saṃbhavati iti artha āpattyā anumānena vā artha siddhiḥ tadā api pravṛtti pramitaḥ tadhetu pratyayaḥ  na tam antareṇa iti āpta vacana arthavat anumeya tā na vyāvartate atha anumāna hrtoḥ pratyayasya śabda sādhana tvāt śabda pramāṇaka tvam tad asat  na āpta vacana artha jñānasya akṣa sādhana tvāt tad arthaḥ śrotuḥ pratyakṣa pramāṇakaḥ  bhavati tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate ‘tasya evam anumeya tve katham śabda eka gocaraḥtathā ‘na sa kalpayitum śakyaḥ tad siddheḥ laukika dapiiti atha pramāṇa rūpeṇa sa sva śabda prakāśitaḥ ākṣeptā nirapekṣaḥ ca kathyate anya pramām prati atha ucyate na brūmaḥ  vidhiḥ anyathā vṛthā syāt iti tad adhīnaḥ saṃsargaḥ kim tu pramāṇān tmanā eva sa sva śabdena pratipādyate tathā ca pramāṇa tvāt prameyasya ākṣeptā pūrvasya pramāṇa antara anapekṣaḥ ca na hi asau śabdavat saṃbandha apekṣa tvāt pūrva siddhim apekṣata iti tathā api asiddhe prāc uktau doṣau siddhe anuvāditā prāmāṇyam asya yatra astu śruteḥ tatra vṛthā tu ayam evam api avyutpanna pravṛtti pada dharma vyatikramau pramāṇa ātmā api sa yadi na pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ atha siddhaḥ  yathā avagata anuvāda at na apūrva artha ākṣepaḥ api ca yatra asya prāmāṇyam iṣyate śabdasya eva tatra astu kim anena nanu uktam śabda saṃgati jñāna apekṣa tvāt anuvādakaḥ  na apūrva artha avagamāya prabhavati na etad sāram śabdaḥ ced anuvādakaḥ tad prakāśyam pramāṇam api anūdyamānam yathā adhigatam katham apūrva artham bodhayet  na prameya saṃsparśa rahitā pramāṇauvagatiḥ atas  yathā adhigata prameyam eva tad pratīyate kva ca pramāṇam eṣaḥ  arthe na yāga ādau sva śabdake laukike apūrva saṃsargaḥ śrotuḥ asti avidhau= api phala sādhana śaktau ca īchabdaḥ tatra na dūṣyati padārtha antara tulya tvāt vidhi ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ na saṃsargaḥ padārthānām sva śabdaiḥ tu prakāśitāḥ saṃbandha yogya rūpeṇa tasmāt saṃsarga bhāginaḥ viśiṣṭa artha prayuktā hi samabhivyāhṛtiḥ jane atas  na viddhi abhāvena saṃsargaḥ  na prakalpate na ca niyogasya prameyam nirūpyate na tāvat yāga ādayaḥ prameyāḥ teṣām yajati ādi śabda viṣaya tvāt na api teṣām pramāṇa antarasya agocaraḥ saṃsargaḥ tathā hi avidhiṣu api laukikeṣu vākyeṣu śrotuḥ anadhi gataḥ  apūrvaḥ saṃsargaḥ pratīyate ‘brāhmaṇa putraḥ te jātaḥ aityādiṣu atha phala sādhana sāmarthyam prameyam ucyate na kila kāminaḥ  niyogaḥ  akāma upāye dhātu arthe avakalpate anupāya tve hi tasya na sa kāminyā kṛtaḥ syāt iti tad api asaṃpratam na hi śabdasya tatra kaścid aparādhaḥ yena tam atikramya anyat pramāṇam mṛgyate pramāṇa antara apekṣa tā pratyuktā anantara phala adarśanena tu virodhaḥ  niyoga gamye api tasmin= aviśiṣṭaḥ ānantaryasya apramāṇa artha tvena tad abhāvaḥ śabde api tulyaḥ atha vā śabdaḥ tatra na duṣyati phala sādhana sāmarthye niyogaḥ tu duṣyati eva na hi tatas  puruṣartha sādhana avabodhaḥ saṃbhavati tad ca idam vidhi viveka bhāvanā vivekābhyām avagantavyam tasmāt  saṃbandha jñāna apekṣa tvena padārtha antaraiḥ samāna tvāt vidhāyaka arthasya na śakyam viśeṣeṇa vaktum tad nibandhanaḥ padārtha saṃsarga iti sarva eva tu padārthāḥ saṃbandha yogyaiḥ kāraka ādi bhāvaiḥ sva padebhyaḥ pratītāḥ sannikarṣeṇa saṃsṛjyante yatas  lokāt śabda vyāpāra avagamaḥ loke ca padaiḥ sva arthānām pratipādanam sannikarṣeṇa viśiṣṭa artha para tayā na sva artha mātra pratipatti para tayā tathā ca sarva padārtha ākāṅkṣā nibandhana eva saṃsargaḥ sarve hi te padaiḥ aparyavasita rūpāḥ sva rūpa mātre prakāśyante evam padārtha antaraiḥ tulya tvāt vidheḥ na viśeṣeṇa tad nibandhanaḥ saṃsargaḥ sarva padārtha nibandhane ca saṃsarge na vidhi abhāvena saṃsargaḥ  na upapadyate tad evam na saṃsarga artham api vidhiḥ upāsanīyaḥ katham na upāsanīyaḥ yadā niyoga para tayā eva padānām sva artheṣu saṃsarga jñānam pravartaka vacana antara pravṛtti darśanena hi tad hetu pratyayam anumāya tatra tasya sāmarthyam gamyate na etad  apravartake api vākye svarūpa niṣṭhe saṃbandha grahaṇāt  sannidhāpita agni vyatirikta pākya upakaraṇam agni arthinam prati yadā ucyate ‘caitra gṛhe kṛśānuḥiti tadā tatas tena ānayanam dṛṣṭvā gamyate ‘ihānena agni sattā pratītā sā ca asmāt vākyātna ca śakyam vaktum ‘tata ānaya‘gaccha vā tatraiti vākyāt pratyayaḥ agni sattā mātra pratyayena vākyāt pravṛtti siddheḥ na vākyasya niyojane api sāmarthyam śakyate kalpayitum artha antara anvaye ca prayoga pratyaya upapattau na viśeṣa anvaye pramāṇam anyathā veda arthaḥ  niṣpramāṇaka eva syāt iti uktam atha kartavyatā jñānāt vinā anarthakyam ucyate na pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām anyat vākya prayojanam pratipatti vidhau tulyam yadi sā eva prayojanam samānam et tad artham ca samarpayati ced ayam prajñā kriyā upāsana adhikāra siddhi vyapekṣitam hanta tarhi svarupe tad na vacaḥ paryavasati tulyam etad samāptam ca vākyam vākya antara anugam niyoga anupraveśaḥ  asti tavat yadi vṛthā anyathā tattva avabodha vidhi aṃśaḥ tāvat evam samuddhṛtaḥ atha manyate vastu svarūpa mātra jñānam kartavyatā jñāna rahitam pravṛtti nivṛtti śūnyam anarthakam pravṛtti nivṛtti prayuktā hi vākya pravṛttiḥ athaḥ arthavat tvāya vidhiḥ anyathā narthakyam tatra ucyate pratipatti vidhau= api tulyam ānarthakyam tathā hi ‘evaṃvidhaḥ pratipattavyaḥ aiti api na tad svarūpa jñāna atiriktā kācana pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā atha svarūpa jñānam eva prayojanam tad svarūpa mātra niṣṭhe api tulyam atha pratipatti vidhiḥ ‘prajñām kurvīta‘sa kratum kurvīta‘a ātmā iti eva upāsita aiti adhikāra vidhi vyapekṣita prajñā upāsanā viṣaya samarpaṇena arthavān na avagata viṣaya svarūpā prajñā śakyā iti sva rūpa niṣṭham api vacaḥ tathā arthavat  tasya samarpaṇe sutarām sāmarthyam nanu evam asya sva rūpa niṣṭhā hīyate niyoga anupraveśinaḥ sva gata niyoga niṣṭham api tarhi tad na niyoga antara anupraveśāt atha matam sva artha paryavasitam eva vākyam vākya antareṇa eka vākya tām upaiti saḥ  ayam prākaraṇikaḥ saṃbandha ucyate anyathā vākya lakṣaṇa eva syāt  etad api samānam niyoga anupraveśe api na sva rūpa niṣṭhatā hīyate nanu asti niyoga anupraveśaḥ anyathā ānarthakyāt  kāmam tattva pratipatti vidhiḥ tu tāvat ānarthakyāt nirākṛtaḥ vidheḥ vinā api tasmāt śabdāt tatva avabodha siddheḥ nanu utpatti vidhiḥ karma rūpa bodhe vyavasthitaḥ yathā tattva jñāna vidhiḥ tathā bodhe avatiṣṭhatām adhikārāt pravṛttiḥ ca matā karma adhikāravat  ajñāna jñāpana matas  atha apravṛtta pravartanam vidhim ācakṣate dhīrā iti etad api tādṛśam karma svarūpa avagamaḥ tatra na iṣṭam vidheḥ phalam kim tu kārya vyapekṣasya phala vākyena saṃgatiḥ iha adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ  yasya tad na vidhīyate tattvam tattva avabodhasya na adhikāra praveśitā na hi vrīhi ādi viṣayam pratyakṣam adhikāra bhāj  yad api codyate yathā utpatti vidheḥ karma rūpa pratipatti mātram arthaḥ ‘āgneyaḥ  aṣṭa kapālaḥiti na tatas  pravṛttiḥ adhikāra vidhi nibandhana tvāt tasyāḥ tathā tattva avabodha vidheḥ tattva avabodha mātram arthaḥ pravṛttiḥ adhikāra vidheḥ ‘prajñām kurvīta aityādeḥ yatas ca pravṛtti pratipatti prayojana bhedaḥ  vidheḥ atas  asya lakṣaṇa dvayam āhuḥ ajñāta jñāpanam apravṛtta pravartanam iti etad api asāram yatas  na utpatti gatasya vidhāyakasya svarūpa avagama mātram iṣyate phalam api tu adhikāra vākya saṃbandhaḥ tathā hi vidheḥ puruṣa artha mātra sādhana tve avabuddhe tad viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ  labhyate na ca tattva pratipatti vidheḥ api tad eva phalam yatas  yasya adhikāra saṃbandha upāsana ādi viṣayasya ātma tattvasya tad akriyā ātmat tvāt na vidhi viṣayaḥ yad tu tad viṣayaḥ tattva jñānam tasya na adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ vrīhi ādi pratyakṣavat  na hi vrīhi ādi svarūpa grāhi pramāṇam prayoga eka deśa tām bhajate pramitānām adhikāra saṃbandhāt niṣpannānām iva anaḥ vāsaḥ prabhṛtīnām vāna takṣaṇa ādiḥ hi tad kriyā na adhikāram anupraviśati iti idānīm tṛtīya pratipatti gocaraḥ  vidhiḥ parāsyate tattva avabodha viṣaya tvena saṃbandhāt  dvitīya pratipatti viṣayaḥ  hi na tattva avabodha viṣayaḥ kim tu tad abhyāsa viṣayaḥ sā upāyam anyat tarhi idam śābdāt jñānam vidhīyate pralīna grahaṇa grāhya vibhāga udgrāham advayam na hi bhinna artha saṃsarga rūpa vākya artha dhī padam ātma tattvam niṣprapañcam iti etad api pelavam advaya ātma prakāśaḥ  asau= anavaccheda vibhramaḥ sva ātma sthitiḥ su praśāntā phalam tad na vidheḥ padam tad sādhana avabodhe hi vidhātṛ vyāpṛtiḥ matā apekṣita upāya tā eva vidhiḥ iṣṭaḥ  manīṣibhiḥ tatas  hi adhyavasāya ādiḥ na akasmāt na abhidhānataḥ na brūmaḥ śabda utthaḥ tattva bodhaḥ  vidhīyata iti kim tu pratyasta mita buddhi bodhya bheda avagrahaḥ atas ca advayaḥ  dvitīya tadvidha bodha abhāvāt vā pramātṛ prameya dvaya virahāt vā tatas  anyaḥ tasya ca ālaukikasya pramāṇa antarāt utpatti upāyasya anavagamāt saha upāyaiḥ śama dama manana dhyāna brahmacarya ādibhiḥ vidhānam yatas  na śābda jñāna viṣaya ātma tattvam vākya lakṣaṇaḥ  hi śabdaḥ pramāṇam tasya ca viṣayaḥ  nānā padārtha saṃsarga ātmā tad anugamena pratīteḥ tad jñānasya ca vividha artha mātra saṃbheda avabhāsasya ātma tattvam niṣprapañcam dvaita leśena api anavamṛṣṭam katham gocaraḥ syāt iti etad api asāram yatas  yaḥ  asau= advayaḥ  dvaita leśa saṃsparśa vikala ātma tattva bodhaḥ saḥ  avaccheda vibhrānti virahāt tasya svarūpa avasthānam avaccheda kaluṣa tayā hi tad anātma rūpeṇa prakāśate na tu tatas  anyaḥ tattva bodhaḥ ‘satyam jñānam anantamiti śruteḥ ātma tattvam ca praśānta śoka ādi viśvāśivam apahata pāpma ādi śruteḥ prakāśamānān atiśaya ānandam ‘vijñānam ānandam brahma‘eṣaḥ  asya parama  ānandaḥ etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvantiiti śrutibhyaḥ tathā ca tad svarūpa sthitiḥ viśva aśiva upaśamāt niratiśaya āhlāda avāpteḥ ca suṣṭhu praśānta aparaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ phalam uktam ca ‘a ātma lābhāt na param vidyateiti na ca puruṣa arthe api ajñāta upāye na pravartata iti yuktam yatas  pravṛtteḥ pūrvarūpam icchā tathā ca tad vāreṇa pravṛtti upadeśa kvacid  ‘atha atas  dharma jijñāsātathā ‘yaḥ  hi yad icchati sa tad karotiiti uktam api ca ajñāta upāye ced na pravartate avaśyam upāya jñāpanayā tatra pravartyaḥ phalam uddiśya tāvatā ca tatra api pravṛtti siddheḥ na vidhāyakasya tatra vyāpāra āśrayitavyaḥ tad uktam ‘tasya lipsā artha lakṣaṇāiti tasmāt phala sādhana eva vidhi vyāpāraḥ nanu phalavatī api artha lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ kva tarhi vidhi vyāpāraḥ itthaṃbhāve na etad sāram yatas  yathā eva sādhana sāmānye arthāt  pravṛttiḥ tathā itthaṃbhāva sāmānye api yatas  na ananugrahakam sādhanam samartham atha tad viśeṣe pravartyaḥ sādhana viśeṣe api tathā astu api ca apekṣita upāya tā eva vidhiḥ tasyāḥ  apravṛtta pravartanā lakṣaṇa tvāt  pravṛtti hetoḥ ca dharmasya pravartanā śabda abhidheya tvāt iṣṭa tāyāḥ tad sādhana tāyāḥ ca anyasya pravṛtti hetoḥ abhāvāt iṣṭa tāyāḥ ca pramāṇa antara avaseya tvāt svayam pravṛtteḥ jānāti eva asau ‘mayā etad kartavyamiti na iṣṭatāyāma pravṛtta pravartanātvam iṣṭa sādhana tāyām tu pramāṇa antara avagama abhāvāt śabda eka gamyāyām na śabdam antareṇa apravṛtta puruṣa pravṛtti hetu tvam atas  sā śabda pramāṇikā satī vidhiḥ iti gīyate anutiṣṭhataḥ  ca sādhanam anuṣṭheyam pravṛtti hetuḥ na svabhāva siddham tena anutiṣṭhataḥ sādhana tā vidhiḥ atas  anuṣṭhānam sādhana viṣayam eva vidhāyakāt śabdāt gamyate nanu adhyavasāyaḥ ākūtam ādyā pravṛttiḥ kāla traya viyuktam pravṛtti mātram ajñāta kriyā kartṛ saṃbandha iti vidhi vidaḥ  vidhim vyācakṣate na etad sāram yatas  adhyavasāya ādīnām eva hetuḥ atra mṛgyate sa ca na anyaḥ  apekṣita upāya tāyāḥ na ca te nirasta hetavaḥ syāt etad  abhidhānam eṣām hetuḥ tad ca vārtam abhidhānāt hi pratītiḥ eṣām syāt  na utpattiḥ na hi pratīti mātreṇa ghaṭa ādayaḥ pravṛtti hetava ityādi varṇitam vidhi viveke athavā na abhidhānataḥ na ca śabdādadhi avasāya ādiḥ jñāpaka tvāt avyutpanna pravṛtti prasaṅgāt ityādi tatra eva uktam athavā ‘yaḥ  manyate ‘mayā idam kartavyamiti yatas  adhyavasāyaḥ ‘niyuktaḥ  asmiaiti yatas  buddhiḥ sa niyogaḥ  vidhi śabda paryāya iti tam pratyucyate tatas  eva apekṣita upāya tvāt ‘kartavyam aitidhyavasāyaḥ tathā hi kartuḥ iṣṭa abhyupāye ‘kartavyam aiti loke buddhiḥ tad abhāve tu ‘akartavyamiti anvaya vyatirekābhyām te ca tad viṣaye gamyete tathā ‘niyuktaḥ  asmia iti ‘pravartitaḥ  asmiaiti sva ātma pravṛtti hetu pratītiḥ na ca saḥ  anya iṣṭa abhyupāya tāyāḥ na khalu dṛṣṭa sāmarthye akasmāt vinā hetunā hetuḥ iti yuktimat  na hi tam parityajya laukikam alaukika kalpane pramāṇam asti kutas ca na abhidhānataḥ na khalva laukikasya abhidhānam saṃbhavati saṃbandha agrahāt iti uktam atha vā tatas  hi adhyavasāya prārambha anuṣṭhāna parisamāpanāḥ apekṣita upāya tvāt tad sadbhāva eva niyukta pravṛtteḥ yasya kasyacid niyogāt apravṛtteḥ syāt etad  ‘kartavyamiti pratyayāt pravartate anyathā kartavyam na kṛtam syāt  tad ca na na akasmāt kartavya pratyaya utpādaḥ sa hi sva artha avāpti nimittaḥ syāt etad  śabdāt eva kartavyatā buddhiḥ tatra ucyate na abhidhānataḥ na śabdāt kartavya tā buddhiḥ niyogaḥ  hi śabda arthaḥ sa hi niyoktṛ dharmaḥ svatantraḥ  vā syāt  kartavyatā tu viṣaya dharmaḥ atha viṣaya dharmam niyogam brūyāt  prāptam apekṣita upāya tvam atha niyogāt kartavya tā syāt  evam api na tasyām śabdaḥ pramāṇam sākṣāt tasya niyoga abhidhāyi tvāt  na api arthāt  akartavye api anāpta niyoga darśanāt atha niyogasya kārya tā gamyate tad niṣpatti adhīna iti viṣaye kartavyatā avagamaḥ tad asat  viṣaye kārya tā pratīteḥ loke tathā hi ‘gauḥ duhyatām tvayāiti niyoge anyena dugdhāyām na punar doham ārabhate viṣayasya kārya tā pratīteḥ tasya niṣpādita tvāt  na ca anyena eva niyogaḥ  niṣpāditaḥ tasya aniyukta tvāt tatra niyoga siddhaye punar doha ārambhaḥ syāt  vistareṇa ca ayam arthaḥ  vidhi viveke vicārita iti alam ati prasaṅgena syāt etad  asya jñānasya mokṣa sādhana tvāt vidhānam vidyā asādhyaḥ  hi mokṣaḥ śrūyate ‘vidyayā tad ā ārohanti‘vidyayā amṛtam aśnute ayaḥ tam ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti sa sarvān= ca kāmāntathā ‘sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ  bhavati saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhantiityādi na ca sādhya tve api antavat tvam śabda gamya tvāt anāvṛtteḥ ‘na ca punar āvartateiti na hi eṣa tarka gamyaḥ yena tarkeṇa asya tattvam vyavasthāpyeta śabda gamyasya tu śabdāt eva tattva vyavasthā ananta vidyā asādhya tvāt vā ananta tvam kṣaṇika tve api ca vijñānasya saṃtati rūpeṇa ananta tvam tatra āhuḥ na ca mokṣaḥ phalam tasya sādhyaḥ  mokṣaḥ  na ca aparaḥ avidyā astamayaḥ  mokṣaḥ sā saṃsāra udāhṛtā vidyā eva ca advayā śāntā tad astamaya ucyate kaḥ punar eṣa mokṣaḥ yadi anāgata deha indriya buddhi anutpādaḥ ‘a śarīram vāvasantam na priya apriye spṛśataḥiti darśanāt  sa prāgabhāvaḥ  na sādhyaḥ atha brahma prāptiḥ sā caitra grāmayoḥ iva vā syāt jīva brahmaṇoḥ mārga śrutibhyaḥ aśatam ca ekā ca hṛdayasya nāḍyaḥ tāsām mūrdhānam abhi nissṛtā ekā tayā ūrdhvamāyan= amṛta tvam eti ‘sa yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati etad vai khalu loka dvāramtathā ‘te arciṣam abhisaṃbhavati arciṣaḥ  ahaḥ aityādi yathā vā madhuni nānā kusuma rasānām samudre ca nadīnām prāptiḥ avibhāga lakṣaṇā tathā syāt  ‘yathā loke madhukṛtaḥ  madhu kurvantiiti‘yathā somya imā nadyaḥiti darśanāt  kāryasya vā kāraṇa bhāva āpattiḥ ‘tathā vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti aiti śruteḥ tad rūpa pariṇāma lakṣaṇā vā yoga vyāghravat  ‘sa yaḥ  ha vai tad paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatiiti darśanāt  ‘brahma saṃpadyataiti ca sphaṭikasya iva rāga apakarṣaṇena sva rūpa prāpti lakṣaṇā ‘param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyateiti śravaṇāt  tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ sarva gata tvāt ‘tad antarasya sarvasya‘nityam vibhum sarva gatamiti ananya tvāt ca tad vijñānena sarva vijñāna upadeśāt ‘tattva m asiiti sākṣāt pratipādanāt  pratyagātma vṛttinā ca sarvatra ātma śabdena nirdeśāt  ‘atha yaḥ  anyāmiti bheda darśana apavādāt ata eva ca na dvitīyaḥ niravayava tvāt ca ‘niṣkalam niṣkriyam aiti paraspara avayava saṃbheda lakṣaṇasya avibhāgasya anupapatteḥ na api tṛtīyaḥ kāryasya sarvadā kāraṇa tvāt  atha kārya rūpa nāśaḥ uccheda ātma tā prasaṅgaḥ  mokṣasya tatra ‘vidyayā amṛtam aśnuteiti virodhaḥ vidyayā eva uccheda prasaṅgāt  ātma ucchedasya ca aniṣṭa tvāt aphala tvam pratiṣiddhaḥ ca ‘akṣaram aiti atra mukhyaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ‘vāca ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam aiti vikāra anṛta tva pratipādanāt śrutyā na caturthaḥ ananya tvāt eva caitanyasya ca brahma rūpasya aviśeṣāt  atha vijñāna ātmanām śoka moha ādi abhāvaḥ  viśiṣyata iti ced tatra api śoka ādayaḥ ced ātmānaḥ  vijñāna ātmanām anucchedyāḥ atha guṇā artha antaram āgama apāyinaḥ kṣaṇikāḥ kṣaṇika tvāt eva ca ucchidyanta iti na tad sādhanam apekṣyam na ca āgāminām anutpattaye apekṣyata iti uktam atha aiśvarya viśeṣaḥ  brahmaṇi tad prāptiḥ tad rūpa pariṇāmaḥ  mokṣaḥ ‘sa svarāj  bhavatiiti śruteḥ tad asat  aneka īśvara anupapatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ  nyūnam samam vā vijñāna ātmanām aiśvaryam syāt  nyūna tvena brahma rūpāpattiḥ na svārājyam tathā hi brahma śabda vācyaḥ parameśvaraḥ teṣām adhipatiḥ syāt  tathā ca anya rāja tā tatra ca antava tvam śrūyate ‘atha ye anyathā atas  viduḥ anya rājānaḥ te kṣayya lokā bhavantiiti upapadyate ca parameśvara icchayā nyūna aiśvaryāṇām aiśvarya pracyuti darśanāt loke ‘samatvasya tu anapapattiḥ eva yugapad  ekaḥ ced sarva adhipatiḥ sarvasya praśāsitā paraḥ kim kurvan= īśaḥ syāt  virodhāt ca na khalu eṣām ekam ati tve hetuḥ asti tatra ekasmin vastuni viruddha abhiprāyayoḥ eka abhiprāya anuvidhāyi tve tasya itarasya anīśvara tvam ubhaya anuprāya anuvidhānam na virodhāt  ubhayoḥ ananuvidhāne anīśvara tvam ubhayoḥ kārya asiddhaḥ ceda ekamatye hetuḥ pariṣadvat  anyathā tasya āsiddheḥ iti ced  pratyekam anīśvara tvam atha paryāyeṇa aiśvaryam avirodhāya ucyate antavat tā jagat sargasya ca asaṃbhavān na brahma tulyam aiśvaryam yatas  para eva jagat sarge śrūyate tad upāsanena sarga uttara kālaḥ  apavarga iti tasmāt sphaṭikasya iva rāga ādi apakarṣaṇena svarūpa āvirbhāvaḥ  brahma prāptiḥ brahma rūpa tvāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ tathā ca ‘param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate aiti uktam anya rūpa niṣpattau sva śabda anupapatteḥ niṣpadyamānasya abhedāt saṃbandhāt vopapattiḥ iti ced  na viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyāt sarvasya tasya niṣpadyamānasya sva tvāt  tatra yathā mala apagame śuklam eva sat vastram ‘śuklam jātam aiti ucyate tathā moha āvaraṇa vigame svarūpa āvirbhāve ‘svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyateiti ucyate tathā ‘brahmā eva san brahma apyetiiti tad evam sva rūpa sthiti lakṣaṇa tvāt mohasya na kārya tā prāk api svarūpasya bhāvāt  āgantukasya asva rūpa tvāt na ca anya tvam yatas  avidyā apagama eva uktena prakāreṇa muktiḥ avidyā saṃsāraḥ vidyā eva ca avidyā nivṛttiḥ yadi agrahaṇam avidyā yatas  bhāva eva abhāva vyāvṛttiḥ atha viparyāsaḥ tathā api virodhita tattva jñāna udaya eva tad nivṛttiḥ na hi śuktikā jñāna utpādāt anyā rajata jñāna nivṛttiḥ tad sādhyā prayatna antara sādhyā vā tayoḥ yaugapadyāt prayatna antara anapekṣaṇāt ca tathā ca vidyā brahma prāptyoḥ tulya kālatā śrūyate ‘brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatiiti tathā ‘a ānandam brahmaṇaḥ  vidvān na bibheti‘tad ā ātmānam eva avedaham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat‘tatra kaḥ  mohaḥ kaḥ śoka eka tvam anupaśyataḥveda bhavati vidvān na bibheti kaḥ  mohaḥ paśyata iti paurvāparya aśravaṇāt yad tu kvacid paurvāparyam tad  ‘vyādāya svapiti aiti yathā nanu eka tve tulya kāla tā api anupapannā na ekasya api vastunaḥ  bhāva abhāva rūpeṇa vyapadeśāt  tathā ‘yadā ghaṭaḥ  naśyati tadā kapālāni jāyanteiti katham tarhi mārga avibhāga sarga apyayā aiśvarya śrutayaḥ tatra āhuḥ na mārgaśrutayaḥ nirupādhi viśuddha brahma vidyā viṣayāḥ yatra hi sarva upādhi viśuddham asthūla ādikam brahma upāsyam tatra ‘brahmā eva san brahma apyeti‘na tasmāt prāṇā utkrāmanti atra eva samavanīyanteiti prāṇān utkramaṇena vijñāna ātmana eva āgatiḥ ucyate na hi tad agamane tad upādheḥ tasya brahmaṇaḥ  bhedena vijñāna ātma tvam yatra tu ‘manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ  bhā rūpaḥiti sa upādhi upāsyam tad viṣayāḥ tāḥ yatra etad śrūyate ‘araḥ ca ha vai ṇyaḥ ca arṇavau brahma loke tṛtīyasya amitas  divi tadaiḥ aṃmadīyam saraḥ tad aśvatthaḥ soma savanaḥ tad aparājitā pūrbrahmaṇaḥ prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam veśmaiti tathā ca abrahma vidām api tad gati śravaṇam ‘ye cāmī araṇye śraddhām satyam tapa iti upāsateiti para brahma prāptiḥ tu na abrahma vidām yujyate ‘vidyayā tad ā ārohanti yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ na tatra dakṣiṇā yānti na avidvāṃsaḥ tapasvinaḥiti tathā ‘tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum etiiti vacanāt  apunarāvṛtti śrutiḥ tarhi katham atra kecid manyate krama mukti āśrayaṇāt tad prāpya tatra utpanna nirupādhi tattva jñānāḥ param padam aśnuvate yathā uktam ‘vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthāḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt yatayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ te brahma lokeṣu para anta kāle para amṛtāḥ parimucyanti sarvebrahma lokeṣu iti kārya brahma loka nirdeśaḥ bahuvacanāt tatra avayava dvāreṇa bahutva upapatteḥ para anta kālaḥ  mahāpralayaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ sva adhikāra paryavasānam tasmin para amṛtāḥ para brahma rūpeṇa amṛtāḥ santaḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt bhedena parameśvare sva kṛtānām karmaṇām phalānām ca saṃnyāsāt yogāt ca sarvam idam kartṛ ādi brahma iti upāsanāt tathā ca smṛtiḥ ‘brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare parasya ante kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti param padamanye tu manyate yathā candra loke yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā sthita eva tasmin bhukta bhogā āvartante na evam sthita eva brahma loke tatas  āvṛttiḥ kim tu tad pralaya paryavasānā tatra sthitiḥ tad pralaye hi na tatas  āvṛttaḥ  bhavati tatas ca anāvṛttiḥ śrūyate tathā ca ‘imam mānavam āvartam na āvartanteiti ‘imam( im edition) iha aiti viśeṣaṇam ‘amṛta tvam eti aiti amṛta tvam āpekṣikam yathā ‘amṛtā devāḥiti tathā ca paurāṇika smaraṇam ‘ābhūtasaṃplavam sthānam amṛta tvam hi bhāṣyateiti yad tu manyate sarva gata tve api brahmaṇaḥ  vikṛta avikṛta bhedaḥ tatas ca deśa bhedaḥ tathā ca avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ  deśa bhedaḥ śrūyate ‘atha yad atas  paraḥ  divaḥ  jyotiḥ dīpyateiti atas  avikṛtasya niyata deśasya brahmaṇaḥ prāptaye yujyate mārga viśeṣaḥ tad saṃpradhāryam na tāvat anutpannā dvaya viśuddha vidyasya ayam mārgaḥ brahma vidaḥ śravaṇāt  na api vidyāvataḥ vidyā udaye nikhila bheda ucchedāt iti madhunadī nidarśana avibhāga śrutiḥ api viveka jñāna abhāva parā na tu tadvidha eva avibhāgaḥ sarga śrutayaḥ api na sarga parāḥ kim tarhi eka ātma tattva pratipatti pradhānāḥ tatas tad anuguṇa tayā eva tāsām artha vyavasthānam na tu tad virodhena tathā hi kasmin nu bhagavaḥ  vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsīt ekam eva advitīyamiti eka tvena upakramāt  ‘a etad ātmyam idam sarvam tad satyam sa ātmā tad tvam asi aiti upasaṃhārāt eka tvena eva aikātmya tattva pratipatti param ekam idam vākyam gamyate tatra yadi aparaḥ tejaḥ prabhṛti tattva sargaḥ satyatayā vidhīyeta vākya bhedaḥ syāt  atas  yathā upāṃśu yāja vākye ajāmi tva upakrama upasaṃhāre ‘viṣṇuḥ upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ aitya ādīni vacāṃsi vākya bheda doṣāt pṛthagvidhi tvam alabhamānāni tādarthyāt tad ānukūlyena stuti artha tayā vyavatiṣṭhante tathā sarga śrutayaḥ api ekatva upāya tayā na ca viparītam śakyam vaktum ekatva śrutiḥ eva bheda pratipatti artha iti sarvatra eka tvena upakramāt  upasaṃhārāt ca yena upakramyate yena ca upasaṃhriyate sa vākya arthaḥ bheda pratipatteḥ ca aphala tvāt  eka tva pratipatteḥ tu dṛṣṭam śrutam ca phalam śoka ādi nivṛttaḥ viśuddha aikātmya darśanena tad avagamāt ‘tatra kaḥ  mohaḥ kaḥ śoka eka tvam anupaśyataḥiti śravaṇāt  phalavat aṅga tā ca aphalasya upāya tvam ca na ca idam jagat asat mūlam kim tarhi advitīya ekasat mūlam kāraṇa avyatirekāt ca kāryasya sat ekam eva idam ghaṭa ādivat  mṛd rūpeṇa hi ghaṭa ādayaḥ  na eka tvam atikrāmanti nanu evam mukhya  eva kārya kāraṇa bhāva uktaḥ syāt  na etad  ekatva avatāra upāya mātra tvāt na khalu atra kārya kāraṇa bhāva eva pratipādyaḥ yena asau yathāśabdam mukhya  eva gṛhyeta ekatva upāyattvāt iti uktam eka tvam ca anena upāyena avatāryate puruṣaḥ sa ca mukhyaḥ pradhāna virodhī ‘ekam eva advitīyam aiti punar  punar  śruteḥ sarva bheda nirāsa para tvāt na śakyam vaktum kāraṇa ātmanā ekatvam kārya ātmanā nānātvam ‘tat satyam sa ātmāiti ca kāraṇasya eva satya tva avadhāraṇāt anyatra ca‘indraḥ  māyābhiḥiti bhedasya māyā gamya tva śruteḥ sākṣāt ca bheda abhāvasya śravaṇāt  ‘na iha nānā asti kiñcanaiti bheda abhedayoḥ ca virodhāt prāc anupapatteḥ varṇita tvāt tad avirodhena varṇyate tad upādāna mātra tayā bheda vikalpasya bimba pratibimbavat varṇa pada vākya ādivat ca yathā hi na bimbāt pratibimbānām utpattiḥ nānā rūpāṇām bimba upādāna mātra tayā pratibimba bheda vikalpasya na hi bimbāt  parasparataḥ  vā vyāvṛttāni kānicid vastūni pratibimbāni bimba upādānam tu tad nānā nirbhāsa mātram tathā na varṇebhyaḥ pada vākya prakaraṇa ādīni kānicid vastūni santi tad upādāna mātra tvāt tad kalpanāyāḥ ‘varṇebhyaḥ padāni niṣpadyante padebhyaḥ  vākyamiti ucyate api ca svapne api sṛṣṭiḥ śrūyate ‘na tatra rathā na ratha yogā na panthānaḥ  bhavanti atha rathān ratha yogān pathaḥ sṛjate aiti tadvat eṣā syāt  anya paratvāt svayam eva ‘vāca ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyamiti vikāra asatya tayā na pāramārthikī iti uktam aiśvarya śrutiṣu api sva guṇa vidyā vipākaḥ  ayam śrūyate ‘sa ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati‘sarvān= ca kāmān āpnoti‘sa svarāj  bhavatiiti na tu mokṣaḥ sa hi nirupādhi brahma vidyā nimitta eva yad api kvacid apunarāvṛtti śravaṇam tasya api dvayī gatiḥ vyākhyātā iti ekam darśanam anye tu manyante āvirbhūta brahma rūpaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ sarva ātma tvāt sarva īśitṛ tvāt ca sarva upabhogānām ca bhoktṛ tvāt tad ānanda mātrā rūpa tvāt deva ādi ānandānām ‘sa sarvān= ca lokān āpnoti sarvān= ca kāmān‘sa svarāj  bhavati aiti tasya tad saṃkīrtanam brahma rūpa āvirbhāva lakṣaṇa mokṣa praśaṃsā artham nanu sarva ātma tvena sarva kāma avāptau sarva śoka moha ādi āptiḥ api syāt  na teṣām abrahma rūpa tvāt avidyā adhyastatvāt  jñāna aiśvarya ānanda bhogāḥ tu brahmaṇaḥ  rūpam ‘vijñānam ānandam brahma‘na anyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā‘etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti‘sarvasya īśānaḥ‘etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi aiti ādi śrutibhyaḥ tathā ca yad kiñcid īśvara tvam yad ca vijñānam yaḥ ca ānandaḥ  brahma ādiṣu sthāvara anteṣu bhūteṣu brahmaṇi tāni tāni āvirbhūta brahma svarūpaḥ samaśnuta iti yuktam loka ādayaḥ tu avidyā adhyaḥ tāḥ  na brahma rūpam te katham āvirbhūta brahma svarūpam āskandeyuḥ nanu prapañca śūnyasya advaitasya brahma rūpasya jñeya abhāvāt īśita vyābhāvāt ca vijñānam aiśvaryam ca anupapannam tatra ‘sarvajñaḥ‘sarva īśvaraḥiti api śrutī samādheye eva na etad sāram yatas  na īśitavyakṛtam īśvara tvam jñeya kṛtam vā jñātṛ tvam kim tu siddhena jñāna rūpeṇa siddhayā ca īśana śaktyā jñeyam avāpnoti īśitavyam ca viniyuṅkte praśāsti ca prakāśa dāhavat  siddhena hi prakāśa rūpeṇa prakāśyam prakāśayati vivasvān na tu prakāśya adhīnam tasya prakāśa rūpam dāhya adhīnā vā agneḥ dāha śaktiḥ tathā ca tad caitanyena eva kṛtsnasya prapañcasya avabhāsanāt  ‘tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti‘na anyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā aitya ādi śruteḥ sarvajña tvam sarveśvara tvam api tad aiśvaryeṇa yathāyatham īśvaraiḥ īśitavyānām īśanāt  evam ca ‘eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ‘eṣa lokapālaḥ aiti brahma indrayama ādīnām ca aiśvaryam uktam sarva kāma avāptiḥ ca tadīya tvāt deva ādi ānandasya kāmeṣu ānanda prāptyā kāmā āptā bhavanti na sva rūpeṇa evam ‘sa tatra paryeti jakṣan krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ strībhiḥ vāiti varṇanīyam tad viṣaya ānanda bhogāt  na tu strī ādi yogaḥ yathā ‘a ātma ratiḥ ātma krīḍa ātma mithunaḥiti na hi mukhyam ātma krīḍa tvam ātma mithuna tvam vā saṃbhavati yatas ca anavacchinnāni tadīyāni eva sarva bhūteṣu jñāna ādīni kalpita avacchedāni atas  yatra yatra na atyantam avacchedaḥ samutkarṣāt teṣām tāni tāni pratyāsatteḥ bhūtāni ātma tvena bhagavān uktvā ‘munīnām api aham vyāsaḥ aityādi upasaṃjahāra ‘yat yad vibhūtimat sattvamiti tathā ‘a dṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ aśrutam śrotṛ aityādi sarva bhūta darśana ādīnām tad caitanya nibandhana tvāt  anye tu āhuḥ yāvān kaścid parasminnāma rūpa āśrayaḥ  vyapadeśaḥ sarvaḥ  asau= ādhyānāya yathā ‘yaḥ  asau= āditye puruṣaḥ‘hiraṇya śmaśruḥityādi na hi sva mahima pratiṣṭhasya parasya deśa viśeṣa avarodhaḥ sarva viśeṣa atigasya ca rūpa viśeṣa yogaḥ paraḥ ca eṣaḥ sarva pāpma udaya śruteḥ ‘uditaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥiti ādhyānam tu tathā vidhīyate tathā sarvajña tvāt api draṣṭavyam iti tad evam brahma ātmanaḥ tad rūpa āvirbhāvaḥ tad prāptiḥ sa mokṣaḥ sā ca vidyā eva tasmāt na sādhyaḥ  mokṣaḥ na ca vidyayā anya iti puṣkalam atha matam mā bhūt mokṣaḥ sādhyaḥ bandha hetu kṣayaḥ tu sādhyate tad sādhanam ātma darśanam syāt  śrūyate ca tasya phalam bandha hetūnām karmaṇām kṣayaḥ ‘kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvaretathā ‘tad yathā iṣīkātūlam agnau protam pradūyeta evam hāsya sarve pāpmānaḥ pradūyante‘pāpma śabdena puṇyam api saṃgṛhītam sāvadya phala tvāt anyatra ca ‘na etam setum ahorātre tarataḥ  na jarā na mṛtyuḥ na śokaḥ  na sukṛtam na duṣkṛtamiti upakramya ‘sarve pāpmānaḥ  atas  nivartante aiti upasaṃhārāt  na ca tad kṣayam antareṇa kṣema prāptiḥ atas  avaśya kartavyaḥ na ca adatta phalasya karmaṇaḥ  na kṣayaḥ prāyaścittānām doṣa saṃyogena codyamānānām tad kṣaya phala tvāt tasmāt prāyaścittaiḥ iva vidyayā bandha hetu kṣayaḥ sādhyate sā eva ca muktiḥ bandhana viśleṣa artha tvāt muceḥ evam ca na antava tudoṣaḥ pradhvaṃsasya kāryasya api avināśāt tatra ucyate prāyaścitta diśā bandha hetu ucchedaḥ  api naḥ tatas  sarva avidyā pravilaye na cchedyam avaśiṣyate bandha hetuḥ avidyā ātmā vidyāyām sā astam āgatā bandha hetu dhvaṃsaḥ  api na ātma darśana sādhyaḥ tad hi vidadhadeva nikhila avidyā vyavahāra pravilayam udīyate karma phala bhoga vibhāgaḥ ca avidyā upādānaḥ tatra anavayavena unmūlitāyām avidyāyām na cchettavyam asti avidyā adhyastāni hi karmāṇi tad samucchede vidyayā samucchinnāni eva bhavanti tad vipākasya avakāśa eva na asti advaitam ātma tattvam paśyataḥ bheda darśana āśraya tvāt tasya yatas ca avidyā ucchedena eva karma ucchedaḥ atas tulyavat saṃśaya viparyāsābhyām prasaṃkhyātāni karmāṇi ‘bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvarenanu evam karma kṣayāmi upagame tattva darśana samanantaram eva muktiḥ syāt  na dehapāta pratīkṣā ‘tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣe atha saṃpatsyeiti deha pāta pratīkṣā śrutiḥ bādhyeta yasya tu vidyā tad kṣaya sādhanam śāstrāt gamyate tasya tad anusāreṇa keṣāñcid kṣayaḥ  vidyayā keṣāñcid upabhogena tatra ‘kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi aiti aviśeṣāt sarva kṣaya prasaṅge ‘tasya tāvat eva ciramiti deha pāta a= adhi śravaṇāt mukteḥ ārabdha kāryāṇām pravṛtta bhogānām na tatas  kṣayaḥ bhogena eva kṣaya iti gamyate na hi sarva kṣaye dehapāta pratīkṣā upapadyate tad uktam ‘ana ārabdha kārye eva tu pūrve tad avadheḥ‘bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā saṃpadyateiti vidyayā tu avidyā uccheda karma vipāka vyavahāra ucchittau= aviśeṣāt sarva uccheda iti sapadi eva mucyeta na eva doṣaḥ na hi iyam śrutiḥ cira kālatā viśiṣṭam dehapāta vadhim mukteḥ āha kim tu kṣipra tām yathā kaścid kṣepīyaḥ tam pratipādayan bravīti kvacid kārye ‘etāvat me ciram yad snātaḥ  bhuñjānasya caevam iyam api anyathā ‘tāvat eva aiti na vācyam syāt  ‘ciramiti eva brūyāt  ‘tāvat eva aiti tu vacanāt kṣaiprya para tā gamyate atas  kṣiprā eva muktiḥ na pratīkṣaṇīyam asti dehapāta pratīkṣā tu tatra na antarīyaka tvāt bhavati eva atha vā cira tvam anūdya dehapāta avadhi tvam atra ucyate anyathā cira tve avadhi viśeṣe cocyamāne vākyam bhidyeta tatra ayam arthaḥ yadi kasyacid ciram tāvat eva yāvat na vimokṣye iti nanu pūrvasmin pakṣe tattva jñāna anantara tvāt dehapātasya sthita prajña lakṣaṇa abhidhānam na yujyate ‘sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣāityādi dvitīyaḥ  api sarva kṣaye cira tva anupapatteḥ tatra avadhi viśeṣa vidhāna ayogāt anupapannaḥ ucyate sthita prajñaḥ tāvat na vigalita nikhila avidyaḥ siddhaḥ kim tu sādhaka eva avasthā viśeṣam prāptaḥ syāt  na ca brūmaḥ brahma vedanā anantara eva deha viyogaḥ kim tu ārabdha kārya karma kṣayam bhogena pratīkṣata iti tatra kasyacid tad kālaḥ  apavargaḥ kasyacid kiyān= citkṣepaḥ yathā rajjvām sarpa samāropa samuttha bhaya janmānaḥ  vepathu prabhṛtayaḥ tattva darśanāt apāvṛte bhaye kasyacid tadā eva nivartante kasyacid kiyan tañcitkālam anuvartante tad saṃskārāt  tathā sarva karma kṣaye api bhujyamāna vipāka saṃskāra anuvṛtti nibandhanā śarīra sthitiḥ kulāla vyāpāra vigama iva cakra bhrāntiḥ nanu evam brahma vidaḥ  api ced bhokra ādi vibhāga darśanam anuvartate deha pātāt uttara kālam api anuvarteta tatra viduṣaḥ  api na avaśyaṃbhāvi kaivalyam syāt  tathā ca ‘tāvat eva ciramiti śrutyā virodhaḥ atha ucchedāt avidyāyā na anuvṛttiḥ kṣaṇam api na syāt iti sa eva virodhaḥ sā eṣā ubhayataḥpāśā rajjuḥ ucyate yathā bhaya vigame labdha āśvāsasya api saṃskāra mātrāt kampā ādi anuvṛttiḥ na ca bhaya vigame api anuvṛttiḥ iti etāvatā cira kālā bhavati na ca mūla kāraṇa tulya phalaḥ saṃskāraḥ na ca sthāyī anyathā kampa ādīnām nivṛttiḥ eva na syāt  na ca bhaya vigama hetoḥ tattva darśanāt tad nivṛttaye hetu antaram apekṣate tatas  eva hi sa krameṇa nivartate svayam eva vā kulāla cakra bhrānti saṃskāravat tathā nivṛttāyām avidyāyām karmasu ca aviśeṣeṇa ārabdha kāryeṣu anārabdha kāryeṣu ca nivṛtteṣu ārabdha vipāka saṃskārāt śarīriṇam bhoktāram iva ca ayam ātmānam pratyetya ābhāsa mātreṇa vidvān api na tu avidvān iva ārūḍha abhiniveśaḥ sa ca ayam īdṛśaḥ sthita prajñaḥ  varṇitaḥ vīta kāma  ātma rūpa saṃtuṣṭaḥ  duḥkheṣu cchāyā mātra rūpeṣu tattva darśanāt abhiniveśāt kṛtrimebhya iva vyāghra ādibhyaḥ  anudvigna manāḥ sukheṣu ca kṛtrima ramaṇīyeṣu iva vigata spṛhaḥ yathā khalva viduṣaḥ  mṛd dāru racite strī ādau viṣaye chāyā mātra darśanam abhiniveśa vikalam tathā viduṣaḥ kṣīṇa karma avidyasya tad saṃskāra mātrāt darśanam chāyā mātreṇa eva viṣayeṣu tathā ca ‘tad yathā ahinirlvayanī valmīke mṛtā pratyastā śayīta evam eva idam śarīram aiti viduṣaḥ śarīre anāsthām darśayati yatas  na mūla kāraṇa tulya phalaḥ saṃskāraḥ kampa ādivat eva na ca cira kāla anuvṛttiḥ alpa kāla sthāyi tvāt saṃskārasya tadvat eva ca na tad nivṛttaye hetu antaram apekṣyate tattva darśanāt eva krameṇa tasya api nivṛtteḥ svayam eva vā sā ca iyam avasthā jīvanmuktiḥ iti gīyate ārabdha kārya karma saṃskāra kṣayaḥ ca dehapātāt eva gamyate tad anuvṛttau dehapāta eva na syāt iti na dehapāta uttara kāle tad vipākasya chāyā mātreṇa api darśanam śakyate yena hi karmaṇā yad śarīram ārabdham tatra eva tad vipāka śeṣa ābhāsaḥ anārabdha kāryāṇām tu alabdha vṛttīnām eva nivṛtta tvāt na asti tad saṃskāraḥ labdha vṛtti kāraṇa saṃskārāt hi kārya leśa anuvṛttiḥ na khalu bhaye apratilabdha vṛttau= anupajanita kampa ādau tad saṃskārāt  kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ tasmāt anārabdha kāryāṇām anālabdha vṛtti tvāt ārabdha kārya saṃskāra kṣayasya ca deha pātāt avagamāt viduṣaḥ patite asmin śarīre kaivalyam avaśyaṃbhāvi atra ca labdha vṛtti kāraṇa saṃskārāt vā kārya śeṣaḥ kārya saṃskārāt eva vā tathā ubhaya saṃskārāt eva vā kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ bhaya saṃskārāt vā bhayam tatas  kampa ādayaḥ kampa ādi saṃskārāt vā kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ sarvathā bhavati kāraṇa vigame api kārya śeṣa anuvṛttiḥ saṃskārāt  atas  labdha vṛtti karma saṃskārāt tad vipākāt vā viduṣaḥ  api śarīra sthitiḥ tad uktam tantra antare api ‘tiṣṭhati saṃskāra vaśāt cakra bhramavat dhṛta śarīraḥiti ye tu manyante pravṛtta bhogānām karmaṇām pravṛtta vegasya iṣoḥ iva cakrasya iva vā na śakyaḥ pratibandhaḥ atas  bhogena kṣaya pratīkṣā iti tad asat  śakyaḥ  hi iṣuḥ pratibandhum kuḍya ādibhiḥ nāśayitum ca ccheda ādibhiḥ svapna ādi sūcita upasthita vipāka vartamāna deha bhogya karma kṣaya arthāni ca śāntikāni karmāṇi tasmāt saṃskārāt eva sthitiḥ nanu saṃskāra kāryaśeṣau= avidyā eva tatra katham sarva avidyā pravilayaḥ katham vā na cchedyam avaśiṣyate ucyate viśuddha aikātmya darśana pratipakṣa grastau vilīnau= eva tāvat uditau akiñcitkara tvāt abandha tvāt  tad nivṛttaye hetu antarasya anapekṣaṇāt  viśuddham khalva ātmānam sākṣāt anubhavataḥ  vipāka ābhāsaḥ tam aspṛśan= akiñcit karaḥ  bandha ātmā pralīna eva yathā citra ādau citra ādi tattvam anubhavataḥ strī ādi ābhāsaḥ  rāga ādīnām animitta tvāt tathā avadātam ātmānam jānataḥ  viparītam vā khaḍga ādiṣu śyāma ādi ābhāsa utpannaḥ  api tattva darśanāt avakāśam alabhamānaḥ pravilīna eva tathā ca na tad nibandhanena malina tvena śocati ātmānam na tejasvitayā abhinandati avabhāsamānayoḥ api tayoḥ ātmani tattva darśana pratihata avabhāsa tvāt evam ca yad ucyate karmaṇaḥ  vā śarīra sthitiḥ syāt saṃskārāt vā kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ kaḥ ca karmaṇaḥ kṣayaḥ kārya anuvṛttau tad nivṛttyā hi tad kṣayaḥ  gamyate tasmāt  ‘bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā saṃpadyateiti eva yuktam tad api apāstam karma vipākaḥ  hi ātma saṃsparśī śoka abhinandana vān aviduṣaḥ viduṣaḥ tu tad asaṃsparśāt ābhāsa mātram maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādi nibandhana viśeṣavat na vipākaḥ anabhinandyamāna tvāt at viṣyamāṇa tvāt ca tathā ca ‘tat tad prāpya śubha aśubham na abhinandati na dveṣṭiiti darśitam tathā ‘yasyām jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyataḥ  muneḥpaśyata eva śarīra ādi prapañcaḥ  niśā tad asaṃsparśāt adṛśyamāna sama tvāt nanu tattva jñāna pratihataḥ ced utpannaḥ api prapañca avabhāsaḥ  na ātma saṃsparśī na kiñcitkaraḥ na bandhaḥ śabdāt eva tasya utpatteḥ kimartham upāsana ādi ucyate parokṣa rūpam śābda jñānam pratyakṣa rūpaḥ prapañca avabhāsaḥ tena tayoḥ avirodhena prapañca avabhāsaḥ  na ātma asaṃsparśī na akiñcitkaraḥ na na bandhaḥ yathā pramāṇa antarāt avasīyamāna mādhurye api dravye pratyakṣa sarūpa indriya dvāraḥ tikta avabhāsaḥ  adravya saṃsparśī na ābhāsa mātra tayā avatiṣṭhate tathā ca tad dravyam parama artha tiktam iva anavasita mādhuryam iva duḥkhāya bhavati upāsana ādinā sākṣātkṛtātma tattvasya tu virodhāt san= api prapañca avabhāsaḥ  na ātma saṃsparśī devadatta iva siṃha avabhāsaḥ ‘siṃhaḥ  devadattaḥiti samārope avabhāsamānaḥ  api tad asaṃsparśī akiñcitkaraḥ na bhaya hetuḥ nityaḥ ca ātma tattva prakāśaḥ tatra na punar vipayarya avakāśaḥ  asti śābdam tu pramāṇa adhīnam kṣaṇikam jñānam tatra punar api viparyaya avakāśaḥ dṛṣṭam hi pramāṇa ananu sandhāne punar  sarpa bhrāntyā rajjoḥ bhayam atha atra api satatam śābdam jñānam anusaṃdadhīta kim anyat upāsanam asmāt  tasmāt bandha hetu= chedaḥ  api vidyā eva na tayā sādhyaḥ evam uttarāgha āśleṣe api vācyam ‘yathā puṣkara palāśa āpaḥ  na śliṣyanta evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śliṣyate aiti kartṛ karma pravibhāgasya vidyayā pravilayāt  evam na vidyāyā aneka phala kalpanā bhaviṣyati vartamāna apadeśānām ca phala vidhi tvena na vipariṇatiḥ iti yad uktam na śābda jñāna viṣayaḥ  brahma iti tatra ucyate na brahma śabda dhī gamyam yadi aśakyaḥ  dhiyaḥ  vidhiḥ dhī viśeṣa prarūpāya na asiddhaḥ  viṣayaḥ kṣamaḥ vidhiḥ na arūpita padaḥ  dhī mātram na vidhīyate na khalu jñāna mātram vidhīyate jñāna viśeṣa vastu na ca aprasiddhe anirūpite tatra niyogaḥ na hi aprasiddhe viṣaye niyoktum śakyate jñānasya ca viśeṣaḥ  artha dvāraḥ na ca aprasiddhaḥ  arthaḥ tad viśeṣa nirūpaṇāya prabhuḥ na ca ātma rūpasya śabdāt anyatas  siddhiḥ śabdāt api ced na siddhiḥ tad dvāra jñāna viśeṣa asiddhau viṣaya anupapatteḥ niyoga anupapattiḥ api ca jñāna viśeṣa vidhi vādina ātma tattve prāmāṇyam eva hīyata iti darśayati vidhiḥ sva siddhi niṣṭhaḥ  vā kriyā siddhi paraḥ  athavā advaita brahma tattvasya pratipattiḥ ahetukā viniyogāt adhigatiḥ yāsyā jñāna kriyā artha tā atatparā na pramāṇam sārthavāda uttha buddhivat  vidhiḥ kriyā gocara tvāt na dravye vyāpṛti kṣamaḥ sattā anvayāt tu tad siddhiḥ pratyuta iti sa duṣyati viśiṣṭāni akriyā bodhaḥ pramāṇam na viśeṣaṇe pratipattiḥ viśiṣṭā api viṣayasya niyogataḥ sattām na sādhayati eva samāropeṇa saṃbhavāt  yadi tāvat niyogasya eva kārya tā pratīyeta tadā sa sva niṣpattau paryavasitaḥ saha śabdena atha viniyogāt viṣaye kartavyatā avagamaḥ tathā api viṣaya siddhau ubhayathā na vastu tattvam saṃspṛśati tatra advaita ātma tattva pratipattiḥ apramāṇikā syāt  syāt etad  ‘ya ātma apahata pāpmā vijaraḥiti padānām sāmānādhikaraṇyena sambandhāt anyathā vā vastu tattva pratipattiḥ iti tad ca na anya paratvāt sā hi na ‘evam idam aiti paryavasitā kim tu ‘evam idam pratipattavyam aiti kartavya tā niṣṭhā na vastu tattve pramāṇam vṛttānteṣu iva artha vāda uttha jñānam anya paratvāt na ca ātma tattvam eva vidheḥ viṣayaḥ tasya anuṣṭheya viṣaya tvāt kriyāyāḥ ca tathā abhāvāt siddha vatsva śabda upādāne ananuṣṭheye dravye vyāpāra ayogāt  pratyuta avidheya kāla traya anyatama saṃspṛṣṭa satta anugamena dravya svarūpa siddhiḥ ‘īdṛśam vastu abhūt asti bhaviṣyati vāiti tasmāt svarūpa siddhau duṣyati na hi vidheyasya kāla traye api sattā avagamaḥ na hi ‘yajeta aiti ukte yāgasya bhūtakālā vartamāna kālā bhaviṣyat kālā vā sattā pratīyate nanu bhaviṣyat kāla avagamyate bhaviṣyat kāla viṣaya tvāt vidheḥ na etad  na hi ‘vihitam niyogataḥ  anuṣṭhāsyate vihita akaraṇa doṣa abhāva prasaṃgāt  nanu viśiṣṭa kriyā abhidhānam viśeṣaṇe api pramāṇam iṣyate yathā ‘somena yajetatathā ‘aṅgadī kuṇḍalī vyūḍha uraskaḥ  devadattasya putraḥ  adhīte aiti adhyayana kriyāvat sarvaḥ  viśeṣaṇa kalāpaḥ pratīyate satyam viśiṣṭa kriyā pramāṇam viśeṣaṇe api pramāṇam anyatra pratipatteḥ pratipattiḥ hi viṣaya viṣeśa viśiṣṭā pramīyamāṇā na viṣaya viśeṣasya sadbhāvam gamayati anyathā bhūte tathā ābhāsa samāropeṇa api saṃbhavāt  ‘asau vāva lokaḥ  gautama agniḥ aiti yathā dyu prabhṛtiṣu anagni dṛṣṭeḥ atra āha nanu naḥ viparīta arthā dhīḥ pratīti virodhataḥ anāśvāsāt ca rajata pratyayaḥ rajate smṛtiḥ na khalu anyat anyathā pratīyata iti yuktam pratīti virodhāt  katham anyasmin pratibhā samāne anyaḥ  viṣayaḥ anāśvāsāt ca viṣaya rūpa vyabhicāriṇi jñāne na tatas  viṣaya niścayaḥ syāt  api ca viṣaya rūpam ananukurvat aviṣayam anālambanam jñānam agrāhyam eva syāt  jñāna hetu mātrasya anālambana tvāt cakṣuḥ ādivat  tathā ca āvedaka tvāt na anya apekṣāt api tatas  artha siddhiḥ kim tarhi idam śukti saṃnikṛṣṭe cakṣuṣi ‘rajatamiti smṛtiḥ sāmānya grahaṇāt bhrāntiḥ tarhi katham pratyakṣa smaryamāṇayoḥ viveka agrahaṇāt  saḥ  ayam bheda agrahaṇe abheda grahaṇa abhimānaḥ  viveka rahitānām yathā dūrāt antarālā grahaṇe vṛkṣa ādiṣu saṃśleṣa grahaṇa abhimānaḥ tasmāt  ‘smarāmi aiti viveka śūnyā rajata smṛtiḥ eṣā atra ucyate na etad na hi pravarteta śuktikā śakale tadā rajate sā pravṛttiḥ ced na tasya asaṃnidhānataḥ asaṃnidhāna ābodhāt ced pravṛtti niyamaḥ kutas  pravartate yad tatra eva tad tad saṃnidhi kāritam anyatra bheda grahaṇāt viveka agrahaṇāt tathā pravṛtti bhedaḥ sādṛśyāt vivekā grahaṇam yadi adṛṣṭeṣu pravarteta loṣṭa ādiṣu avivekataḥ na tatra yadi tad buddhiḥ śuktikā śakale api na atha asti viparīta arthā khyātiḥ nihnūyate katham adṛṣṭa tvāt apravṛttiḥ śuktikā śakale samā dṛṣṭam tad yena rūpeṇa tad pravṛtteḥ akāraṇam dṛṣṭa smṛtauvivekāt ced idam atra parīkṣyatām tattva bodhāt atha atattva abodhāt rajata vedanāt  dṛṣṭe pravṛttiḥ pūrvasmin viparīta artha tā mateḥ na dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭayoḥ bhedaḥ parasminna upayoginī sva yoga darśane te hi samāropa upayoginī na adṛṣṭe asaṃprayukte vā cākṣuṣaḥ syāt viparyayaḥ yadi cakṣuṣā saṃprayuktam śukti śakalam ‘na rajatamiti pratīyāt  rajatam vā tathā na śuktikā śakala āditsayā pravarteta rajata arthī tasya ‘rajatamiti anavagateḥ loṣṭa ādivat  na ca smaryamāṇe rajate sā pravṛttiḥ tad deśa asaṃnidheḥ na hi pratītim upagate api vastuni yatra tasya asaṃnidhiḥ tatra tena arthī pravartate syāt etad  rajatasya pratīteḥ asaṃnidheḥ ca apratīteḥ tatra pravṛttiḥ tad na śuktikā śakala eva pravṛtteḥ tatra eva tu pravṛttiḥ tad saṃnidhi nibandhanā rajata mātra pratīteḥ smṛti viveka śūnya tvāt ca pravṛttiḥ anyatra api syāt  asaṃnidhāna agrahaṇasya tatra api aviśeṣāt atha matam anya deśeṣu vastuṣu sa viśeṣa pratyakṣa avagateṣu rajatāt viveka grahaṇāt apravṛttiḥ śuktikā śakale tu rajata sādhāraṇa śukla bhāsvara rūpa mātra pratīteḥ viśeṣāt pratyayāt ca smṛti viparivartinaḥ  rajatāt viveka grahaṇāt pravṛttiḥ evam api adṛṣṭeṣu loka ādiṣu tatas  anya tā anavadhāraṇāt pravṛttiḥ syāt  atha na teṣu rajata avagamaḥ itaratra api na bhāve vā viparītā khyātiḥ abhyupagatā syāt  atha adṛṣṭa tvāt eva adṛṣṭeṣu na pravartate śuktau= api na pravarteta nanu yad tu tathā rajata rūpam na tena avagamaḥ sa yathā cakṣuṣā saṃprayuktasya na asti tathā saṃprayuktāyāḥ  api śukteḥ yadi manyeta dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇa yoga vivekāt cakṣuḥ saṃprayukta eva pravartate na itarasmin tatra api idam vicāryam viveka grahaṇasya viveka kṛtaḥ  abhāvāt saṃnidhi pratīteḥ abheda bodhaḥ tatas  vā pravṛttiḥ bheda avabodha abhāva mātrāt vā pūrvasmin viparyayaḥ uttarasmin dṛśyamānādṛśyamānayoḥ saṃprayuktā saṃprayuktayoḥ vā na viśeṣaḥ bheda agrahaṇasya tulya tvāt  na hi indriya saṃyogasya darśanasya vā kaścid agraha upayogaḥ abhūta samārope tu asti na kathañcid agṛhīte asaṃprayukte vā aindriyakaḥ samāropa upapadyate smṛtam pratyakṣataḥ bhinnam sva jñānāt eva ced kutas  avivekaḥ  anyathā tu syāt sadā sāmānya darśane viparyayaḥ  anyam smarataḥ  na ca saṃśaya darśanāt  smṛta dvayauviveka uttham
