saṃśayam yadi manyate tad na ubhayoḥ api yatas  smṛtau dṛṣṭaḥ  viparyayaḥ viśeṣa jñānataḥ  adhyakṣe smṛtam yadi vivicyate na sva jñānāt asati asmin dvismṛtau katham eka dhīḥ eka tvam eva smarataḥ prāgrūpam śaśini sphuṭam timira ādi pradoṣeṇa katham te dvi tva vibhramaḥ pipāsataḥ ca salilam śuktikā hita cetasaḥ viparyayaḥ  na hi bhavet bhavan vā salile bhavet  api ca idam tatra bhavān vyācaṣṭām smaryamāṇam dṛśyamānāt sva jñānāt eva vivicyate na vā smṛti jñānasya svarūpam eva tādṛśam yad pramātavyāt bhedena avabhāsayati sva rūpa mātra niṣṭham vā tatra pūrvasmin smaraṇa gocarayoḥ avivekaḥ kutas  sva jñānāt eva vivikta tvāt  itarasmin= api sadā smṛtau viparyayaḥ syāt  sāmānya darśane ca anya smṛtau= avivekāt na ca tad tathā saṃśayasya api darśanāt  atha matam ekasmṛtau viparyayaḥ tatas  avivekāt  anekasmṛtau tu saṃśayaḥ na ekasmāt avivekāt  tad asat  aneka smaraṇe api hi dṛśyate viparyayaḥ yadi ca pratyakṣe arthe viśeṣa jñānāt smaryamāṇam vivicyate na sva jñānāt  asati tatra viśeṣa jñāne ca dvayoḥ smṛtau saṃśaya eva syāt  na eka avabhāsaḥ  viparyayaḥ atha tu sva jñānāt smṛtam vivicyate smṛti viparyaya bhedaḥ ca abhyupagamyate tadā aneka smaraṇe api indriya doṣa viśeṣāt yuktaḥ  viparyayaḥ darśitam ca idam sāmānya darśane api kadācid ekām koṭim smarataḥ  na saṃśayaḥ  na viparyayaḥ doṣāṇām apuṣṭeḥ atas  sva jñānāt eva tadā smṛtam vivicyate na dṛśya viśeṣa paricchedāt  evam ced kutaḥ dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇauvivekaḥ api ca anyat eva smarataḥ pūrvarūpam eka tvam śaśini dvi tva vibhramaḥ na smaryamāṇā viveka jaḥ na ca jñāna indriya vṛtti bheda avivekāt tayoḥ apratyakṣa tvāt smaryamāṇa tvāt ca śuktikā hita cetasaḥ ca salilam pipāsataḥ  na syāt viparyayaḥ salila ābhāsaḥ  vā smaryamāṇasya sva jñāna vivekāt na ca sarvā niyogena bhrāntiḥ sādṛśya bandhanā śvete pīta bhramaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  madhure tikta vibhramaḥ kiñcid sādṛśyataḥ  hi syāt na kaścid tatra na bhramaḥ tasmāt indriya doṣāṇām sāmarthyasya vibhāgataḥ bhrameṣu niyamaḥ  doṣāt agrahe na bhrame yamaḥ yadi ca sadṛśa darśanāt sadṛśa smṛteḥ bhramaḥ katham śvete pīta bhramaḥ madhure vā tikta bhrāntiḥ āntara pitta saṃvedane avyāpārayataḥ  api bahis indriyam syāt  añjanavat ca akṣi gatasya tad gata kṛṣṇim ādivat ca adṛśya tvāt kiñcid sādṛśye sarva prakāra bhrama prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt indriya doṣa sāmarthya bhedāt niyatā viparyaya utpattiḥ agraha mātre tu doṣa vyāpāre kāmila ādi doṣāt bhrānti niyamaḥ  na syāt  na hi sādṛśya nimittaḥ asadṛśe api bhrānti darśanāt  viśeṣa smaraṇāt na api smṛtau= api tad agrahaḥ deśa kāla viśeṣāt ca na smṛtam pravivicyate aneka deśa adhi gatam viviktam na punar tatas  smṛtiḥ iti api vijñānam smṛteḥ anyat udāhṛtam na ca māna phalāt bhinnāt tad siddhi ati phalāt ṛte sati smṛti viveke ca pratyabhijñāna vibhramaḥ atha ana saṃnihitaḥ  vyarthaḥ  vedyaḥ saṃnidhimat tayā avivikta smṛteḥ evam viparīta artha tā bhavet  manasaḥ  anupaghātāt ca na asaṃnidhya parigrahaḥ doṣaḥ  hi agrahaṇe hetuḥ indriyāṇām udāhṛtaḥ pravṛtti niyamaḥ  na syāt iti ca atra niveditam sarva jñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante atra kalpane sarva ātmanā arthaḥ  jñānena kenacid na hi gṛhyate tathā ajñāta vivekasya dvi candra ādi viparyayāt anuvṛttimataḥ paśyan kasya sva ātma apanihnute atha matam sva jñānāt eva smṛtam vivicyate kadācid tu tatra pratyakṣa iva viśeṣa agra hastataḥ avivekaḥ sataḥ  tu viśeṣa grahaṇa indriya saṃyukte sāmānya darśane api na avivekaḥ tatas  ubhaya koṭi smaraṇe na saṃśayaḥ ekasmṛtau na saṃśayaḥ  na viparyayaḥ evam api dvayoḥ smaraṇe na viparyayaḥ syāt  na ca smṛtau viśeṣa grahaṇam viśeṣa smaraṇāt  atha deśa kāla viśeṣāt smaryamāṇam vivicyate tatra deśa kāla bheda agraha iti tad na ananta deśa kāla bheda avagatam tad deśa avagatam ca dṛśyāt smaryamāṇam viviktam gamyate na ca deśa kāla bheda grahaṇāt ananta smaraṇa anupapatteḥ tad deśa avagate ca deśa bheda abhāvāt atha smaryamāṇa tayā agrahaṇāt avivekaḥ smaryamāṇa tā jñānāt ca vivekaḥ tasmāt  ‘smarāmiiti jñāna śūnyāni rajata ādi jñānāni bhrānti hetavaḥ paripūrṇā eva tarhi smṛtiḥ na tayā sva viṣayasya kiñcid na gṛhītam svayam eva sā sva viṣayam dṛśyāt vivinakti iti na asti dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇayoḥ avivekaḥ yatas  smarāmi iti jñānam anyat eva darśana smaraṇa viveka kāri smṛteḥ tatra idam vicāryam smṛtiḥ sva viṣayam vivinakti vā na vā yadi vivinakti tadā viparyaya abhāvaḥ atha na smṛtiḥ sva viṣayam vivinakti tadā sāmānya darśane ca anyasmṛtau viparyayaḥ syāt iti uktam na ‘smarāmi aiti vivekāt ced  sa eva smṛteḥ svayam avivecaka tvena syāt  kārya gamyasya hi jñānasya bhedaḥ kārya viśeṣa unneyaḥ na ced smṛteḥ pramāṇa kāryāt kāryam viviktam syāt  kena sā viviktā gamyeta sati api smṛti viveke dṛṣṭaḥ pratyabhijñā bhramaḥ ‘sa evaiti na ca pratyakṣasya āvivekaḥ eka vivekena ubhayoḥ vikārāt smṛtāt avivekāt ca smṛti vibhramaḥ syāt  na pratyakṣa bhramaḥ tasmāt na ‘smarāmi aiti pramoṣāt avivekaḥ atha asaṃnihitasya saṃnihita ātmanā pratītiḥ avivekaḥ smṛteḥ viparīta artha tva prasaṃgaḥ atha asaṃnidhya grahaṇāt bhavatu sa svapna jñāne natu indriya jāyām bhrāntau manasaḥ  anupaghātāt upaghāta hetu tvāt ca agrahaṇasya na ca ittham pravṛtti niyamaḥ syāt iti uktam sati ca vastu grahe kasyacid aṃśasya agrahāt bhrāntau sarva jñāna bhrama tvam na hi kasyacid jñānasya sarva ātmanā vastu viṣaya iti sati api ca viveka jñāne pramāṇa antarāt  dvi candra diś moha ādi anugatiḥ dṛṣṭā iti na agrahaṇa mātram viparyayaḥ prasakta pratiṣedha ātmā khyātiḥ prāptau prakalpate na agrahaḥ prāpakaḥ abhāvaḥ prāpikā viparīta dhīḥ ye ca khyātī tu rajataḥ cakṣuḥ saṃyukta vastunoḥ na ayam tad upanīta artha pratiṣedhaḥ  avagamyate na ca agrahaṇam eva eṣā pratītiḥ apabādhate sarvā hi agraha bādhena janma na syāt tathā īdṛśī viveka vijñānam idam na prasakta niṣedha dhīḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ  vaiyātyāt svām pratītim apahnute na krame yaugapadye vā viveka matiḥ īdṛśī prāpte syāt aikya saṃvittau na bhedasya anirūpaṇe rajatasya smaran= cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ca vastunaḥ sāmānya dṛṣṭyā rajatāt abuddhvā ca viviktatām paścāt viviñcan pratyeti na evam sāmānya darśane koṭi dvaya smṛti abhāve saṃśayaḥ  na niyogataḥ viveka grahaṇa abhāvāt kāla saṃnidhi saṃvidaḥ tadvat ābhāsanāt prāpta āviṣṭaḥ syāt anyathā grahaḥ tatra āgrahaḥ  nimittam syāt athavā saṃnidhi grahaḥ bheda graha apavādena rahitaḥ  bhāva rūpataḥ viparyaya anabhyupāye bhramaḥ  agraha nibandhanaḥ śabda eka gamya uktaḥ syāt agrahaḥ  agraha bandhanaḥ ‘nedam rajatam aiti prasakta pratiṣedha rūpā pratītiḥ na agrahaṇe avakalpate prasaṅga abhāvāt na khalva grahaṇam kasyacid prasañjakam abhāvaḥ  hi saḥ viparītā tu khyātiḥ saṃnihitasya rajata tām abhūtām rajatasya vā saṃnihita tām ādarśayantī prasañjayati nanu ca rajata nayana ghaṭita vastunoḥ khyātī staḥ te eva prasañjike satyam na tu tad upanītayoḥ iyam niṣedha avagatiḥ na hi ‘nedam rajatam aiti rajata mātram cakṣuḥ saṃyukta vastu mātram vā nirasyamānam avasyāmaḥ kim tu cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya tu rajatatām rajatasya vā cakṣu saṃyuktām na caitayoḥ agrahaṇam prāpakam agrahaṇa tvāt eva tasmāt avaśyam pratiṣedhya prāptaye viparīta khyātiḥ upāsanīyā na ca ‘nedam aitya grahaṇam eva vāryate sarva jñāneṣu tādrūpya prasaṃgāt  sarva jñānānām agraha bādhena utpattau ca viveka jñāna mātram idam na prasakta pratiṣedha rūpam iti prati iti anusāriṇaḥ  anurūpam na hi rajata śukti kāśa kalayoḥ yugapad viviktayoḥ grahaṇe īdṛśī pratītiḥ na krameṇa aviviktayoḥ grahaṇa īdṛśī syāt iti ced  yuktā viviktayoḥ grahaṇe aviveka pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt  viviktayoḥ grahaṇe prāpti abhāva yuktā api ca bhavati kadācid  yaḥ smarati ca rajatasya cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya vastunaḥ sāmānya mātra darśī na rajatāt vivekam gṛhṇāti punar cakṣuḥ prasādāt pratyeti na ca tadā tathā pratītiḥ aviveka grahaṇa abhāvāt nanu sāmānya darśane na ced viparyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ syāt  tad apanodi ca nirṇaya jñānam īdṛśam eva na etad sāram na hi asati koṭi dvaya smaraṇe sāmānya darśane api saṃśayaḥ na ca viparyayaḥ bhavati hi puraḥ avasthite bhāsvara rūpa mātra pratītiḥ rajate ca smṛtiḥ na ca tayoḥ anya tvam pratipadyate na ekatvam ca tatra na viveka jñānam evaṃrūpam ekatva apratipatteḥ atha matam viveka agrahaṇāt kāla saṃnidhi pratīteḥ ca rajatam vā cakṣuḥ saṃprayuktavat avabhāsate cakṣuḥ saṃyuktam vā rajatavat  atas  prāptiḥ iti pratiṣedha upapattiḥ abhyupetā tarhi viparīta khyātiḥ na hi anyā sā atada ātmanaḥ tathā avabhāsanāt  kāmam tattva ajñāna nimittā syāt  na hi sā tattva jñāne sati udeti virodhāt iti tatra api saṃnidhi khyātiḥ eva nibandhanam tasyāḥ tu viveka grahaḥ  apavādaḥ agrahaṇe nirapavādā sā eva kāraṇam na abhāvaḥ viparīta khyāti anabhyugame ca agrahaṇa nibandhanaḥ  bhrama iti agrahaṇam agrahaṇa nibandhanam iti su vyāhṛtam svapne ca dvitīya abhāvāt kutaḥ avivekaḥ smṛta tvena aviviktasya tathā viveke dharmiṇi pratipanne dharma antara pratipanne dharma antara pratipatteḥ bādhaka tvam pūrvasyāḥ ca bhrānti tvam syātām iti yaḥ pratīti virodhaḥ tu sa sva doṣa udāhṛtaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena bodhāt rūpyam idam mitam aidam śuklam rajatam aiti sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīteḥ ātma upālambhaḥ parasmin= āsajyate pratīti virodhaḥ jñāna bheda kalpanāyāḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt  anāśvāsaḥ  jñāyamāne jñānena eva apabādhyate vyabhicārāt asāmarthyam na tad kāryasya lābhataḥ vyabhicārāt prameya tve kāryam eva na labhyate yaḥ  hi jñāyamāne arthe anyathā api syāt iti anāśvāsaḥ tasya tena eva jñānena tathā tva paricchedinā utpattiḥ nirudhyate tathā hi anāśvāsa nivṛttaye tadvidham jñānam eva apekṣyate tad ca asti eva na ca vyabhicāra doṣāt asamartha pramāṇam jñānam iti yujyate pramāṇa kāryasya paricchedasya jñāna rūpāt eva siddha tvāt  paricchedataḥ  hi prāmāṇyam atantra tā tu vyabhicāra avi abhicārayoḥ asati tasmin dhūma ādeḥ avyabhicārasya api apramāṇa tvāt  vyabhicāravataḥ  api ca sita asita ādiṣu cakṣuṣaḥ sati tasmin prāmāṇyāt  na ca vyabhicāraḥ  bādha hetuḥ doṣavat  prāmāṇya upaghātī kvacid  dṛṣṭaḥ cakṣuḥ ādau vyabhicāravati pramāṇa tvāt  nanu dṛṣṭaḥ  vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇya upaghātī prameya tva ūrdhva tva ādau na etad sāram na tatra vyabhicārāt aprāmāṇyam api tu pariccheda kārya abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca hetu abhāvāt  avyabhicārāt hi liṅgāt liṅgi paricchedaḥ yatra tu avyabhicāraḥ  na kāraṇam tatra vyabhicāre api sati paricchede prāmāṇyam avivādam akṣeṣu tadvat eva ca jñānam pariccheda nimittam na liṅgavat  na ca saṃśaya utpattyā vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇyam upahanti samyak paricchinne dvaividhi asya asaṃśaya hetutvāt na niścite sthāṇau= ūrdhva tvena saṃśerate utpattyā eva jñānam artham avadhārayati anavadhārakam tu na eva iha adhikṛtam evam ca avadhāraṇā deva anavadhāraṇam iti vipratiṣiddham ya eva tu avyabhicāram arthayate jñānasya āśvāsa artham tasya eva anāśvāsaḥ avyabhicāra jñāne api anāśvāsāt na hi tad asiddha vyabhicāram ātmani jñāna antareṣu ca āśvāsa kāraṇam jñāna antarāt siddhau= anavasthā api ca jñāna rūpāt ced na artha āśvāsaḥ tasya asiddhau kena saha avyabhicāraḥ  jñānasya gṛhyeta kim ca jñāna rūpāt eva avyabhicāraḥ  api kathyate viparīta khyātau tad virodhāt  tathā sati tad eva viṣayasya sādhakam vyarthaḥ  avyabhicāraḥ na ca vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇyam upahanti iti uktam api ca agrahaṇe abhīṣṭam yad viveka nibandhanam na parāṇudyate daṇḍaiḥ tad viparyaya darśane na udreka hetava u doṣāḥ kārya sāmarthya ghātinaḥ graha āgraha vibhāgaḥ syāt atas tad sadasattvataḥ viparyaye hi nitarām upaghātaḥ prakalpate iṣṭa kārya uparodhena viparīta udayena ca tasmāt tad sat asat tvābhyām vivekaḥ  atra api kalpate doṣe asatigraha āśaṅkā katham ca vinivartate na hi kāraṇa sadbhāve kārya sattā niyogataḥ pratyakṣam kāryam evam ca hetunā anumitam bhavet  viparyaye phala abhāvaḥ  hetu abhāvāt tu yujyate viveka upāyaḥ ca doṣa abhāva bhāvau grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ na daṇḍa vāritau viparyaye viparyaya hetavaḥ  abhyupaghātakāḥ sutarām iṣṭa kārya uparodhāt viparīta udayāt ca na ca aduṣṭeṣu api indriya ādiṣu agraha āśaṅkā nivṛttiḥ yatas  hetu bhāve api na niyogataḥ kāryam viparyayaḥ ca syāt  pratyakṣā saṃvittiḥ hetunā anumīyeta phalāt tu hetoḥ hetu bhāva anumānam doṣa abhāvāt tu viparyaya kārya asattvam yukta anumānam hetu abhāve kārya anutpādāt  anālamba natā pattiḥ yathā ākāra antara arpaṇam svarūpa ānarpaṇāt evam bhavet agrahaṇe api te kasyacid tu arpaṇam tulyam atha tatra na tad tathā parasya api hi tatra evam atha tatra tathā sthiteḥ sarvatra syāt tathā bhāvaḥ syāt evam grahaṇe api te yathā tatra animitta tvāt samya jñāne animitta tā śaṅkyate grahaṇe api evam agrahe sā nirūpitā jñānāt eva nimitta tvam anyeṣām na viśiṣyate ālambana tvahānam ca yathā ākāra antara avabhāse cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya tathāgrahaṇe api sva rūpa ānarpaṇasya tulya tvāt  atha kasyacid sāmānya rūpasya suākāra tvāt  atha kānicid cakṣuḥ saṃyuktāni vastūni svena rūpeṇa gṛhyanta iti kasyacid agrahaṇe api nānā ālambana tvam tulyam ākāra antara avabhāse api keṣāñcid  suākārāṇām avabhāsanāt  atha agrahaṇe na eva cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ālambana tvam iṣyate paraḥ  api na eva viparyaya icchati evam hi uktam atasmāt yad anyathā santam anyathā pratipadyate tad nirālambanam jñānam abhāva ālambanam ca tadatha viparyaye cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ālambana tvāt anyatra api anālambana tā śaṅkā agrahaṇe api tulyā yathā khalu viparyaya jñāne cakṣuḥ saṃprayukta vastu svabhāva nirapekṣa tā dṛṣṭā samyak jñāne api śaṅkyate jñāna tva sāmānyāt tathā cakṣuḥ saṃprayuktam api vastu na avikala rūpam gṛhyate tena anālambanam bhavati sadṛśa smṛti hetu tām ca pratipadyate iti agrahaṇe dṛṣṭa anālambana tā grahaṇeṣu api kasmāt na śaṅkyate doṣa abhāvāt iti ced  viparyaye api tulyam na ca anyathā ālambane nirālambana tvam cakṣuḥ tu anyathā api na ālambyate ālambana arthaḥ ca rajata vyavahāra yogya tā śukteḥ tathā hi rajata arthī tām ādatte ghaṭasya api hi na eva anyat sva jñāna ālambana tvam anyatra vyavahāra yogya tāyāḥ yatas  na viṣaya ākāram jñānam tatra śuktiḥ sva rūpeṇa na ālambitā rajata jñānena tad nibandhana vyavahāra bhāvāt rajata rūpeṇa tu tad nibandhanasya upādāna vyavahārasya tatra bhāvāt iti kriyā niṣṭhe api vidhau vastu svarūpa siddhaye kaścid āha avaghāta prokṣaṇa ādeḥ yathā dravya artha tā sthitā jñānam svabhāvāt dravya artham karma tvāt ca ātmanaḥ tathā bhavatu evam tathā api iṣṭa rūpa siddhiḥ kutaḥ matā śabdaḥ tad artha kārya tve tau= ajñānasya niṣṭhitaḥ jñānāt jñeyasya kaḥ  anyaḥ  arthaḥ sva rūpa pratibhāsanāt  adṛṣṭa kalpanā yuktā na ca dṛṣṭasya saṃbhave tasmāt yathā prokṣaṇa ādi vidheḥ vrīhiṣu gamyate adṛṣṭā saṃskṛtiḥ jñānavidhe rūpam tathā ātmanaḥ yathā avaghāta prokṣaṇa ādayaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva dravya arthāḥ dvitīyayā ca dravyasya karma tvena nirdeśāt  tathā jñānam api sva rūpeṇa para artham karma tvena ca ātmanaḥ  nirdeśāt tad artham atas  jñāna viṣayaḥ  api vidhiḥ ātma rūpam saṃspṛśati na jñāna mātre paryavasyati jñānasya ātma rūpa artha tvena kartavyatā avagamāt jñāna niyogena eva ātma rūpasya ākṣepāt  syāt etad  bhavatu jñānasya ātma arthatā abhipretā apahata pāpma ādi rūpa ātma pratītau tu pramāṇam vācyam śabdaḥ tāvat evaṃvidha ātma jñāna kartavyatāyām paryavasitaḥ ‘evaṃvidhātma uddeśena jñānam kuryātna tu ‘evaṃvidha ātmāiti tatra ucyate na hi tatra akiñcitkarasya tādarthyena kartavyatā yujyate jñānasya ca karmaṇi na anyat phalam tad rūpa saṃvitteḥ na hi tasyām dṛṣṭāyām anyasya adṛṣṭasya kalpanā tatra yathā ‘vrīhīn prokṣati aiti prokṣaṇa vidheḥ eva vrīhiṣu adṛṣṭa saṃskāra avagamaḥ prokṣaṇa viṣayāt api na anyathā vrīhi arthe prokṣaṇe kartavyatā yujyate na hi tatra kiñcid akurvat prokṣaṇam tad artham kṛtam syāt iti evam vidheḥ eva adṛṣṭa saṃskāra sadbhāva siddhiḥ yathā ‘svarga kāmaḥ  yajetaiti na anyathā svarga kāmasya yāga kartavya tā pratītiḥ yujyate yadi na svarga upāyaḥ  yāgaḥ anupāye ced niyujyate na svarga kāmaḥ  niyuktaḥ  bhavati anuṣṭhitaḥ  api na svarga kāmena anuṣṭhitaḥ  bhavati iti kriyā viṣayāt api vidheḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva avagamaḥ śābdaḥ tathā jñāna viṣayāt api vidheḥ ātma rūpa bodhaḥ na hi tadvidham ātmānam uddiśya jñāna niyogaḥ  yujyate atadvidhaḥ ced ātmā tena jñānena pratīyata iti ukta uttaram idam yasmāt arūpeṇa api bhāsakam jñānam pradarśitam na syāt anyathā tad vidheḥ phalam layaḥ  nivartya u na tathā vikṣepaḥ  hi yathāsukhaḥ laya vikṣepa bhedaḥ ca na syāt agraha mātrake nanu arūpa avabhāse syāt adṛṣṭa phala kalpanā rūpa avabhāse dṛṣṭam tu phalam tad siddhi lakṣaṇam na dṛṣṭa mātrād dṛṣṭa artham puruṣa artha anugam tu tad  na bhidyate ca tad bhāvaḥ  rūpā rūpa avabhāsayoḥ yathā prapañca śūnya tve tattve jñāna avabhāsite duḥkha karma kleśa hānam atattve api tathā bhavet  etad ca atra bhavet yuktam pratyakṣa ādi avirodhataḥ anaupacārikā arthāḥ ca syuḥ karma viṣayaḥ  yatas  ātma artha jñāna vidheḥ etāvat gamyate jñānena saḥ  avabhāsyate ālambyate vyavahāra yogya tām āpadyate tad ca avabhāsanam sva rūpeṇa ca dṛṣṭam para rūpeṇa ca rajata ātmanā śuktikāyāḥ pratipāditam etad  na agraha mātram etad  anyathā ākhyātiḥ tu tatra ubhayathā saṃbhave kuta etad  tattva pratipattiḥ avaśya abhyupeyā na atasmin= tad khyātiḥ anyathā na ātma jñāna vidhiḥ phalavān syāt  sa khalu ana ātma rūpa pravilaya arthaḥ anātma rūpa vilayena hi vastunaḥ  avagatiḥ dṛṣṭā iti yadi ca na ātmanaḥ  nāma rūpa prapañca rūpeṇa prakāśanam kim pravilāpyeta atha matam dvi prakārā iyam avidyā prakāśasya acchādikā vikṣepikā ca svapna jāgaritayoḥ vikṣepikā suṣupta ācchādikā laya lakṣaṇā tatra ācchādaka avidyā nivṛttiḥ jñāna vidheḥ phalam tad ca asat  yatas  na acchādikāyā avidyāyāḥ  nivṛttiḥ puruṣeṇa arthyate tathā yathā vikṣepasya sa hi vividha duḥkha ātmakaḥ layaḥ tu vividha duḥkha nivṛtteḥ asakṛt ānanda tvena śrutau gītaḥ pratyuta arthanīyaḥ syāt  api ca viparyāsam anicchataḥ  avidyā bheda eva na syāt  avasthā traye api agrahaṇa mātra tvāt tasmāt agrahaṇa viparyaya grahaṇe dve avidye kārya kāraṇa bhāvena avasthite svapna jāgaritayoḥ ubhe kāraṇa bhūta agrahaṇa lakṣaṇā suṣupta iti avidyā pravibhāga upapadyate tad uktam kārya kāraṇa baddhau tāviṣyete viśva taijasau prājñaḥ kāraṇa baddhaḥ tu dvau tu turye na sidhyataḥnanu anyathā ayam bhedaḥ agrahaṇa samyak grahaṇābhyām agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa acchādikā suṣupte asamyak grahaṇam itarayoḥ tathā hi abhinnasya vastunaḥ  apradeśasya grahaṇe tathā abhāvasya ca agrahaṇāt pṛthaktvena pratyavabhāsaḥ na etad sāram yadi tāvat asamyak grahaṇa mātram tad apaṭu tvam vā jñānasya kenacid drūpeṇa vā grahaṇam na sarva ātmanā tatra dūra sthe sūkṣme ca bhavati apaṭu jñānam sāmānya jñānam na ca tad avidyā na ca kiñcid jñānam sarva ātmanā arthasya grāhakam iti sarva jñāna mithyātva apātaḥ abhedasya agrahaṇe api bhedasya āvartane api bhedasya asaṃvitteḥ na nivartanīyam asti vidyayā na khalva bheda agrahaṇam nivartanīyam na hi tad kiñcid aparādhyati bhedaḥ tu vividha duḥkha āyatanam atha asamyak grahaṇam pṛthak pratyavabhāsaḥ  apṛthak ātmanaḥ abhyupetā tarhi viparyaya khyātiḥ apṛthak  pṛthak  prakāśata iti atha ucyeta na brūmaḥ pṛthak  prakāśate kim tu pṛthak iva prakāśata iti ka iva arthaḥ yadi yathā pṛthak bhūtam aprakāśa māna eka tvam prakāśate tathā ekam api ātma tattvam agṛhyamāṇā eka tvam prakāśata iti kenacid aṃśena grahaṇam sarva ātmanā ca agrahaṇam uktam bhavati tatra ca uktam atha prakāśata iva na tu prakāśate prakāśane ka upamā arthaḥ tad nibandhana vyavahāra pravṛttiḥ tad nibandhanaḥ ced vyavahāraḥ prāptam prakāśanam na asati kāraṇe kāryam bhavati iti atha abheda agraha eva pṛthaktva c raha abhimānaḥ tad asat  agrahaṇasya abhāvasya sva rūpeṇa para rūpeṇa vā grahaṇa anabhyupagamāt aprakāśamāne ca pṛthaktve kutas tad avagrahaḥ abhinne ca bheda abhimānam parityajya abheda agrahaṇe bheda graha abhimānam ūrīkurvatā kim parihṛtam syāt  tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate ‘laya vikṣepa bhedaḥ ca na syāt agraha mātrakeiti nanu anātma rūpeṇa pratipatteḥ na dṛśyate kiñcit phalam tatra adṛṣṭa kalpanā syāt  ātma rūpa pratipatteḥ tu dṛṣṭam phalam tad svarūpa siddhiḥ ucyate na yasya kasyacid darśanāt  dṛṣṭa artha tā kim tu puruṣa artha saṃsparśinaḥ tena hi tad vidhiḥ nirākāṅkṣā bhavati na ca puruṣa arrha bhedaḥ tattva atattva pratipattyoḥ yathā hi viśuddham advaitam ātmānam pratipadyamānaḥ tathābhūtaḥ  na śokena saṃspṛśyate śocanīya abhāvāt na karma āśayam upacinoti kartavya abhāvāt na kvacid drajyati kiñcid  dveṣṭi vā viṣaya abhāvāt ‘evam jīvan= eva vidvān vimuktaḥ  bhavati tathā atathābhūtam api tathā abhāvanā puraḥsaram sākṣāt iva pratipadyamānaḥ abhūtaḥ  api arthaḥ paribhāvanā atiśayāt bhūta vyavahāra hetuḥ bhavati idam eva ca atra yujyate pratyakṣa ādīnām avirodhāt  karma vidhīnām ca bhūta artha tvāt parama arthe hi prapañca śūnya tve pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni bādhyeran karma vidhayaḥ ca ābhūta kalpanā upādāna vyavahāra siddhārtha gocarāḥ syuḥ tasmāt aparama arthena eva advaita ātma jñāna vidhiḥ yujyate jānātiḥ tattva bodhe ced na mithyā ādi viśeṣaṇāt na ātmā jñātaḥ tathā syāt ced na tad rūpā vidhānataḥ pramāṇa antara siddha tve natarām anyathā yadi śabda arpitena rūpeṇa tasya jñānam vidhīyate atattvena api tena asya vijñānam avakalpate yadi matam ‘sa vijijñāsitavyaḥiti jānātiḥ tattva pariccheda eva vartate tena na abhūta samāropeṇa jñāna vidhiḥ syāt iti tad na mithyātva ādibhiḥ jñānam viśeṣyate mithyājñānam samyak jñānam saṃśaya jñānam iti tad eka niyame na upapadyeta paunaruktyāt virodhāt ca syāt etad  asvarūpeṇa pratipattau na tad ātma jñānam anya jñānam eva bhavati tattva jñānam ca vidhīyate tasmāt tattva siddhiḥ iti tad ca na na khalu etāvat eva tad  ‘a ātmā jñātavyaḥ iti yadi syāt tad rūpa jñāna vidhiḥ tad ca na ubhayathā anupapatteḥ pramāṇa antara siddham ced ātma rūpam na tad jñānam vidheyam atha asiddham aśakyam eva tad  syāt etad  ‘apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ  vimṛtyuḥ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā aiti śabda samarpita rūpasya tasya jñānam vidhīyate tena ca tattvena api tad saṃbhavati samāropitena api tena na niyogataḥ tathābhūta jñāna vidheḥ tathā abhāvaḥ  asya pratīyate jñānam yadi ca dṛṣṭa artham prāptam dṛṣṭata eva tad  ātma rūpa vijijñāsaḥ rajijñāsoḥ vṛthā eva tad  tad upāyaḥ  na ced jñātaḥ tasya eva astu vidhiḥ tatas  avaghāta ādi vidhayaḥ  na adṛṣṭa sparśa varjitāḥ alaukikam idam jñānam atas  yadi vidhīyate na rūpa siddhaye tāvat yatas  kartavyatā vidheḥ kartavyatā ca dṛṣṭa arthe dṛṣṭāt eva prasiddhyati alaukike artha rūpe atas  śabdena pratipādite jñāne jñeya abhyupāya tvāt svayam eva unmukhaḥ pumān tad upāye tu avijñāte vidhinā sa pravartyatām niyoga anupraveśaḥ  atas  vihanti eva pramāṇa tām bhūtartha iti na upāsyaḥ  bhūta artha gatim icchatā yadi ca jñānasya dṛṣṭam phalam tatas  eva pravṛtti siddhe vyarthaḥ  vidhiḥ yaḥ  hi ātma rūpam anubhavitu kāmaḥ sa tasya jñāne svayam eva yatate yaḥ tu na tathā tasya tad vyartham iti vidhi śatena api sa na pravartyate atha upāya ajñānāt dṛṣṭa phale api na pravartate svayam atas  vidhīyata iti tad ca vārtam yatas  sa eva upāyaḥ vidhīyatām yatra ayam ajñānāt na pravṛttaḥ jñāne tu dṛṣṭa phala tvāt pravartata eva syāt etad  avaghāta ādiṣu dṛṣṭa phaleṣu api dṛṣṭaḥ  vidhiḥ satyam na tu adṛṣṭa saṃsparśa rahitaḥ tatra api hi niyama adṛṣṭam phalam taṇḍuleṣu tad praṇāḍyā vā pradhāna pūrva siddhiḥ adṛṣṭā eva atha matam advaita ātma jñānam adṛṣṭa pūrvam alaukikam atas  anantara phalam api vidhīyata iti tatra ucyate kimartham vidhīyate pramāṇa antara agocarasya svarūpa pratipatti artham āhosvit anuṣṭhāna artham tatra na svarūpa siddhi artham anuṣṭhāna phalaḥ  hi vidhiḥ na anuṣṭhānāya dṛṣṭa artha tvāt eva tad siddheḥ tasmāt alaukike apahata pāpma ādi rūpa ātma tattve śabdāt pratipanne tasya sākṣāt jñānam prati tad anubhava upāya tvāt svayam eva puruṣasya abhimukhyam bhavati iti vyartham tad vidhānam yathā āścarya bhūte kasmiṃścid arthe āgamāt pratipanne tasya sākṣātkaraṇe svayam eva unmukha tvam bhavati tad upāyeṣu tu ajñāteṣu upāya tva jñāpanāya vidhānam yujyate tad evam jñāne niyoga anupapatteḥ niyoge ca vastu rūpa avagame prāmāṇya ayogāt vyavasthita ātma tattva pratipattim icchatā śabdān na tasya niyoga anupraveśaḥ  abhyupagantavya iti idānīm dvitīya pratipatti vidhi nirāsāya āha ata eva na vijñāna saṃtāna vidhi niṣṭhatā tatra api pūrvavat na syāt svarūpa avagati pramā sva rūpa niṣṭhāt śabdāt tu pramitasya vacaḥ  antarāt  upāsana vidhānam syāt prāpteḥ tad api vā vṛthā abhyāsena pratyayasya prakarṣasya abhivīkṣaṇāt  tasmāt bhavati akārye arthe vedāntānām pramāṇa tā yad api matam ‘sa kratum kurvīta aprajñām kurvīta‘nididhyāsitavyaḥiti yatra api svarūpa niṣṭhatā eva lakṣyate ‘tattva m asiiti tatra api ‘sat asmi iti cetaḥ  dhārayet aiti vivakṣita tvāt śravaṇāt anyat anucintanam dhyānam pratyaya pravāhaḥ  vidhīyate karmavat eva amṛta tva phalam tad api ata eva na yujyate pūrva uktāt tattva avagati pramāṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt anya niṣṭha tvāt vākyasya atha tu vākya antarāt tattva niṣṭhāt adhigate tad viṣaya pratyaya pravāha vidhānam iṣyate bhavatu na kaścid doṣaḥ tathā ca ‘vijñāya prajñām kurvīta aiti ātma tattva vijñānasya siddha tām darśayati tad api vā vyartham eva prāpta artha tvāt sākṣātkaraṇa phalam hi tad tad anucintanam dṛṣṭa artham na tatas  anyat phalam ākāṅkṣyate amṛta tvam hi na svarūpa āvirbhāvāt anyat iti prāc varṇitam dṛṣṭā ca jñāna abhyāsasya samyak jñāna prasāda hetu tā loke bhāvanā viśeṣāt hi abhūtam api anubhavam āpadyate kim punar bhūtam ‘sa kratum kurvītaiti tu na sakala viśeṣa atigātma tattva anucintanam vidhīyate tad bhāva phalam api tu nāma rūpa upādhi manaḥ maya prāṇa śarīra ādi rūpa anudhyānam aiśvarya phalam krameṇa vā sākṣātkaraṇa phalam ‘tam eva dhīraḥ  vijñāyaiti na prajñā karaṇa vidhiḥ ‘tam eva aiti anya nivṛtteḥ śrutattvāt nivṛttau tātparyam gamyate ‘raktaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati aiti tayā rakta para tvam vākyasya atra ākāśa ādi tattva bheda pūrvam avibhāgaḥ pratipāditaḥ tatra tathā eva prajñā karaṇa prasaṅge ‘tam evaiti vidhīyate tathā ca pūrva ardhe ‘virajaḥ para ākāśāt aja ātmā mahān dhruvaḥiti ākāśa ādibhyaḥ paratvena ātma tattvam darśitam tasya tathā eva prajñā karaṇa prasaṅge tad nivṛttaye ‘tam evaiti ucyate anyathā na eva śabdasya phalam na ca nivartyam vijñāyeta tathā ca tad eva uttareṇa prapañcyate ‘nā anudhyāyāt bahūn śabdāniti eka vākyatā anyathā vākyam bhidyeta śabda mātre ca anudhyāna aprasaṅgāt  śabda pūrvat tvāt tasya śabda artha viṣayam eva idam iti evam ‘a ātmā iti eva upāsīta aiti evakāra śruteḥ tad artha vidhiḥ ‘nididhyāsitavyaḥiti api ‘a ātmanaḥ tu kāmāyaiti upakramāt  ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā aiti upasaṃhārāt ātma svarūpa param ekam vākyam tad antargatāḥ ‘draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ  nididhyāsitavyaḥiti na pṛthagvidhayaḥ kṛtya pratyaya yoge api kṛtya pratyayasya artha antare api smaraṇāt arha ādau stuti arthāḥ yathā upāṃśu yāja vākya antargatāḥ ‘viṣṇuḥ upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ aiti evamādayaḥ ‘a etad ātmyam idam sarvam tad satyam sa ātmā tad tvam asi aiti bhūta eva paryavasitam vākyam tatra ‘sat asmi iti dhārayetiti kalpanā iyam tasmāt trividhasya api jñānasya vidheya tva ayogāt vinā ca vidheḥ vākya artha pratipatteḥ apauruṣeya tvena nirapekṣa tvāt bhūte api arthe vedāntānām prāmāṇya siddhiḥ tathā ca ‘tattu samanvayāt aiti codanā lakṣaṇāt dharmāt tu śabdena viśeṣyam brahma samanvaya gamyam uktam samanvayaḥ  hi padārthānām saṃsargaḥ  viniyogaḥ tatas  brahma gamyate na codanāta iti arthaḥ nanu aviśeṣeṇa kārye arthe vedasya prāmāṇyam varṇitam ‘codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharmaḥiti codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  veda artha  iti arthaḥ na etad sāram evam hi siddha prāmāṇya veda artha vicāra u ayam syāt tad uttara lakṣaṇavat tatra anantaram prāmāṇya pratipādanam na yujyeta ‘vṛttam pramāṇa lakṣaṇamiti ca mantra artha vādeṣu ca kārya artha tvena vipratipattiḥ na syāt  sā ca upariṣṭāt eva nirasiṣyate bahu ca atra vaktavyam iti alam prasaṅgena yathā anya māna vyatibheda muktā matiḥ pramāṇa tvam upaiti kārye apauruṣeya āgama labdha janmā tathā eva siddhe nirapekṣa bhāvāt  iti niyoga kāṇḍa s tṛtīyaḥ caturthaḥ (siddhi)kāṇḍaḥ evam tāvat pratipatti kartavya tā prāmāṇya vyājena yaiḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam tad pratibodhanāya kṛtaḥ prayatnaḥ idānīm tu aprāmāṇyam eva āhuḥ ye tad bodhanāya prayatyate tatra pūrva pakṣaḥ nanu anvita padārtha tvāt vākya arthasya padārtha tām aprāpya na syāt vākya arthaḥ padārtha tve anya mānakaḥ na tāvat brahma antaryāmya ādi padam pramāṇam saṃbandha jñāna apekṣayā pūrva siddhe pratyaya hetu tvena na api vākyam na hi tad sākṣāt vācakam padārtha dvārā tu tad  pratipattiḥ apadārthe jñānasya abhāvāt  te hi saṃsargāt guṇa pradhāna bhāvena itara padārtha viśiṣṭam ekam padārtham gamayanti tatra padārtha eva viśiṣṭaḥ  vākya arthaḥ  bhavati na ca anadhigateṣu pramāṇa antareṇa padārtha tvam sambandha jñāna apekṣaṇāt  iti uktam tatra āpadārtha tve na vākya viṣaya tvam anavabodhakam teṣām vākyam padārtha tve pramāṇa antara adhigateḥ anuvādakam tatra atyanta aparidṛṣṭa brahma ādi artha pramāṇa abhimateṣu vākyeṣu tad vācīni padāni syuḥ na vā yadi na santi na ta itaraiḥ saṃsṛjyeran na bhidyeran= iti na teṣām prameyāḥ loṣṭa ādivat  atha tu santi tathā api taiḥ adhigata saṃbandhaiḥ na pratipādyeran apratipannāḥ ca na viśiṣṭa vākya artha pratipatti hetavaḥ tatra yathā avanāt pika ānīyatamiti pika padārtha jñāne avabodhaka tvam tathā teṣām api tasmāt na codanātaḥ  apūrva padārtha avagamaḥ sā hi vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām kriyāsu puruṣam adhikaroti traividhya vṛddha parigrahaḥ tu japa upayogāt upaniṣadaḥ  vedāntāḥ iti tatra viniyogāt  tatra ucyate sāmānyena padārtha tve siddhe asādhāraṇaiḥ guṇaiḥ śakyā pūrva viśeṣasya lokavat  pratipādanā yathā loke ‘dvīpa viśeṣe evaṃnāmānaḥ  marataka maya pādāḥ padmarāga maya cañcavaḥ sauvarṇa rājata pakṣāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ aiti pakṣi sāmānyam pramāṇa antaradhigatam ananyasādhāraṇena dharma kalāpena saṃsṛjyamānam pramāṇa antara anadhigatam viśeṣa rūpam āsādayati vākyena ca pramīyate pramāṇa antara anadhigatena viśeṣa rūpeṇa sarvasya eva hi vākyasya anadhigataḥ  viśeṣa eva prameyaḥ tathā kāraṇa sāmānyam vā sat sāmānyam vā ‘yataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyanteiti ‘a sthūla m anaṇva hrasvam aitya ādi padārthaiḥ saṃsargāt bhedāt ca pramāṇa antara anadhigatam viśeṣa rūpam āsādayati vākyasya ca prameyam bhavati tad evam loka siddha padārtha anvayena eva apūrva artha pratipatteḥ na anavabodhaka tvam anuvādaka tvam vā sarva pratyaya vedye vā brahma rūpe vyavasthite prapañcasya pravilayaḥ śabdena pratipādyate pravilīna prapañcena tad rūpeṇa na gocaraḥ māna antarasya iti matam āmnāya eka nibandhanam athavā na loke atyantam aprasiddham brahma sarva pratyaya vedya tvāt brahmaṇaḥ  vyatirekeṇa pratyetavyasya abhāvāt  viśeṣa pratyayānām ca sāmānya rūpa anugamāt bheda upasaṃhāra avaśiṣṭam ca satyam brahma iti pratipādanāt  ‘vāca ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyamiti dṛṣṭāntāt  kim tarhi śabdena pratipādyate prapañca abhāvaḥ tatra prapañca padārthaḥ  api siddhaḥ niṣedhaḥ  api siddhaḥ tayoḥ saṃsargāt tad abhāva pratipattiḥ āmnāya eka nibandhana tvam tu tasya ucyate pratyakṣa ādīnām avidyā saṃbhinna tvāt pratyastamita nikhila bhedena rūpeṇa aviṣayīkaraṇāt bheda pratyasta mayasya āmnāyau= agamya tvāt iti paraḥ punar  pratyavatiṣṭhate nanu ca apuruṣa artha tvam bhūta niṣṭhe prasajyate yad  khalu vākyam na puruṣam kvacid hita sādhane pravartayati ahita sādhanāt ca nivartayati kevalam siddham artham anvācaṣṭe tad apuruṣa artham apuruṣa artha tvāt ca unmatta pralāpa vadapramāṇam tathā ca prāyeṇa vedāntāḥ ucyate pramāṇasya na ca etāvat puruṣa artha eka niṣṭhatā (upekṣām api hi phalam pramāṇasya pracakṣate) (anena śloka ardhena atra bhavitavyam iti abhyūhaḥ param tu mātṛkāsu na dṛśyate edita ūr) api ca ajñānataḥ śokī duḥkhī jīvaḥ prakāśate tad nivṛttiḥ ca vijñānam puruṣa arthaḥ svayam matam kasmiṃścid arthe vijñāte kutūhalavatām nṛṇām ākulānām jñāna janma puruṣa artha tva saṃmatam akṣa ādau ca yathārūpa niṣṭhe na apuruṣa artha tā na ca pravṛtti niṣṭha tvam tathā asmin kena vāryate jñeyasya puruṣa artha tvam tatra ced atra tad samam puruṣa arthaḥ svayam brahma praśāntam vijara ādikam atas tad tvam asi iti evam anuśiṣyāya śiṣyate para pravṛtteḥ aṅga tvam pratyakṣa ādeḥ matam yadi atra api sākṣātkaraṇa pravṛttau= aṅgatā iṣya tām na tāvat niyogataḥ pramāṇasya puruṣa artha phala tā na khalu hita upādāna ahita hāne eva pramāṇa phale upekṣām api hi pramāṇa phalam pramāṇa vida ācakṣate na ca puruṣa artha tā pramāṇa lakṣaṇam pramāhetu tvam tu tasmāt na puruṣa artha abhāvena aprāmāṇyam api ca ‘śokī aham aduḥkhī ahamadhana ādīni mama naṣṭāni aiti viśuddha brahma ātmanaḥ  jīvasya mithyājñānam etad nivṛtti rūpam ca viśuddha ānanda prakāśa brahma ātmata tva jñānam tad  sva rūpeṇa eva puruṣa arthaḥ aniṣṭa nivṛtti rūpa tva āt iṣṭa āvirbhāvāt ca yadi api ca saṃskārāt tasya anuvṛttiḥ tathā api śābda jñānam anusaṃtanvataḥ  viduṣaḥ  na pūrvavat bhavati nivartate ca atyantāya dṛṣṭā ca jñāna utpatteḥ eva puruṣa artha tā kvacid  kutūhala ākulitānām ajñāte arthe na hi tad jñānāt  param anyadarthyate na ca pravṛtti nivṛtti viṣayasya eva puruṣa artha tā iti niyamaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni hi pramāṇāni na ca tāvat pravṛtti nivṛtti parāṇi siddha vastu viṣayāṇi na ca puruṣa artha tām jahati yadi matam pratyakṣa ādi jñeyam hi siddham vastu puruṣa arthaḥ salila ādiḥ tad upakārāt  tatas  pratyakṣa ādīnām puruṣa artha tā bhūta niṣṭhānām api atra api ca śabda prameyam svayam eva brahma puruṣa arthaḥ  jarā ādi vividha aśiva upaśamāt parama ānanda prakāśa tvāt ca su prasannam ata eva atat tvam asi aiti śvetaketu mukhena āśāsanīyāya puruṣāya śrutyā abhinnam upadiśyate abhinnam hi tad anuśāsanīyāt  bhedena ca pratīyamānam na puruṣa arthaḥ tattve tādātmya jñāne ca tathā abhāvāt viśvāśivā upaśamāt parama śiva bhāvāt ca paripūrṇaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ  āptaḥ  bhavati yadi matam pratyakṣa ādīni api pravṛti aṅgāni eva pramite arthe hāna upādāna ādi lakṣaṇāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tad mūla tvāt īdṛśam pravṛti aṅga tvam atra api asti eva śabdāt  pramite brahmaṇi sākṣātkaraṇāya pravṛtteḥ iṣṭa tvāt iti eṣā vedānta tattva pravicaya catura prasphurat nyāyatejā mārgam mukteḥ nirundhat nibiḍam api tamaḥ  anādi nirdārayantī sadyas  prakṣālayantī ghanam api jagatām tīrtha dustarka paṅkam vyākhyāta utkhāta viśvā śiva niratiśaya śreyase brahma siddhiḥ iti maṇḍana miśrāṇām kṛtiḥ  brahma siddhiḥ samāptā
